Chapter 1140: Childhood Dharma Transmission Statue

The Infantile Image of Dharma Transmission

Wu Ninglu put away the jade talisman handed to her by Li Fan and hesitated to speak.

"It's only three hundred years! I'm going!"

Li Fan waved his hand, saying no more.

He followed the Sun family patriarch towards the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters.

The jade talisman given to Wu Ninglu, besides serving as a communication talisman, was essentially a miniature aggregation formation.

It contained a clone of Li Fan's soul.

It could not only achieve comprehensive surveillance of Wu Ninglu but, more importantly, allow him to place an eye in the outside world to constantly monitor the Myriad Immortals Alliance's movements.

The clone possessed the Origin permission of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, allowing it to reside within the Heavenly Profound Mirror and continuously monitor the situation in the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

After all, during the period of guarding Yanfajue, it might be in complete isolation, making even the Heavenly Profound Mirror difficult to use.

And the clone was in the Great Qi small world, rarely venturing out.

Having a contingency plan was necessary.

With Li Fan's current strength, this clone possessed combat power comparable to an ordinary Dao Integration cultivator.

The only drawback was that, unlike normal cultivators, it could not recover quickly after combat.

Without the main body's replenishment, its power diminished with each use.

As for the "friend" Li Fan mentioned to Wu Ninglu...

It was naturally his created Saint Blood Fetus.

However, without the True Immortal Net and the infusion of Origin Power Essence, the Saint Fetus had only managed to break through to the Qi Refining stage at the moment.

Li Fan had sent it to the ruins of the Heavenly Sword Sect to subdue the Black Sword Tian Zhi Qi.

With previous experience, there would be no problems, but it would require slow and steady effort.

...

Sun Xingyao, the patriarch of the Sun family, had been at the Dao Integration stage for over five hundred years.

In his youth, he had also served as a guard for Yanfajue.

On their way to the Immortal Alliance headquarters, he introduced Li Fan to the details of this "job."

"Yanfajue is the foundation of our Immortal Alliance. Although it is located within the Immortal Alliance headquarters and appears extremely safe, we must constantly guard against the schemes of villains."

"In the past thousand years, the Five Elders Society has planned at least three operations targeting Yanfajue. They have painstakingly tried to approach Yanfajue and then used a technique called 'evil curse' to launch mental and spiritual attacks."

"Yanfajue she..."

"Her defensive capabilities against such attacks are practically non-existent. Once afflicted, it means at least a century of stagnation. The last successful attempt by the Five Elders Society resulted in heavy losses for the Immortal Alliance. Furthermore, this matter could not be publicized, merely causing the exchange price of cultivation techniques in the Heavenly Profound Mirror to nearly double. The cultivators of the Immortal Alliance grumbled endlessly..." Sun Xingyao recalled his youthful experiences and shook his head.

"So, this task of yours is not as simple as it appears."

"Patriarch. If I fail to stop these malicious attacks during my tenure, leading to Yanfajue's damage, what will happen?" Li Fan asked.

Sun Xingyao's steps halted abruptly.

He turned to look at Li Fan and, after a pause, said, "The promise remains unchanged; we will take good care of Ninglu. You can go with peace of mind."

Li Fan was momentarily speechless.

He hadn't noticed it before, but this Sun Xingyao possessed a touch of humor.

As light and shadow shifted, Li Fan found himself back in the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters.

As before, an illusion appeared before his eyes.

However...

This time, unlike the previous encounter with the illusory image of Dharma Transmission.

In boundless fields, curling smoke rose from farmhouses. On the roof of one such farmhouse lay a seemingly simple and honest youth.

His eyes were vacant, gazing at the sky, seemingly lost in thought.

"Gou Dan, come down for dinner."

The scene abruptly ended.

Emerging from the illusion, Li Fan couldn't help but be slightly stunned.

Sun Xingyao thought he was still shocked by the extremely realistic illusion and began to explain, "The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters retains a trace of Dharma Transmission's aura, so..."

Li Fan was naturally aware of this. He was thinking about something else.

"That simple and honest youth named Gou Dan..."

"Is it Dharma Transmission in his childhood?"

Replaying the brief scene in his mind, there were indeed some faint resemblances to the elderly Dharma Transmission.

"Could it be that Dharma Transmission is a native of the Xuanhuang Realm?"

"No."

Li Fan replayed that short scene multiple times.

"The face of this Gou Dan, by any means, cannot be associated with Dharma Transmission, who dominated the Xuanhuang Realm for an era."

"That confused gaze, and the drastic turn in his later life trajectory, seem more like..."

A word surfaced in Li Fan's mind.

Transmigration.

"If my previous guess is correct, then this young man named Gou Dan should be the Heavenly Doctor's soul transference?"

"Coming from the Heavenly Law Realm, with consciousness dormant since birth, only awakening years later."

"Was this method used to evade the pursuit of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects and the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao?"

Just like Li Fan himself now, in the eyes of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, he was an unmistakable native cultivator.

At that time, no matter how the outside world investigated, Dharma Transmission's true identity remained undisclosed.

Li Fan did not yet understand the "transmigration" mechanism.

But he was very clear that it was definitely different from a simple soul possession.

"Using some secret technique to deceive heaven and earth, reincarnating as a Xuanhuang Realm person."

Li Fan's thoughts slowly turned. As he pondered, Sun Xingyao casually inquired about the illusion he had seen.

Li Fan naturally replied that he had seen the illusory image of Dharma Transmission before.

Sun Xingyao nodded slightly upon hearing this. "It seems your future achievements are destined to surpass mine, Lu'er."

Without waiting for Li Fan to ask, he explained proactively, "Every cultivator who comes here for the first time sees a different illusion.

"It is said to be closely related to their fundamental Dao path. As everyone knows, all cultivation techniques practiced by cultivators originate from Dharma Transmission. Therefore, the closer the vision is to the Heavenly Venerate, the more boundless the future prospects."

"It is said that some true geniuses can see the scene of the Heavenly Venerate's first discourse in his early years..."

Sun Xingyao said enviously.

Li Fan remained silent, his vigilance suddenly heightened.

This time, his strength had rapidly increased, allowing him to glimpse Dharma Transmission's childhood.

If he pushed further, he might directly alert Dharma Transmission's aura.

The two traversed the void of the Immortal Alliance headquarters, using formations.

Soon, they arrived at the location of the Law Enforcement Hall headquarters.

"Follow me." Sun Xingyao commanded, forming a hand seal.

An invisible force field instantly enveloped him and Li Fan.

The spiritual energy within his body, which had become sluggish due to the [Spirit Transformation Stone] underfoot, became active again.

"It has a certain suppressing effect on me, but the effect is not as obvious as when I was at a lower realm."

"If it really came to a fight, I would still be invincible among Dao Integration cultivators."

Li Fan felt at ease and followed Sun Xingyao into the Law Enforcement Hall.

Unlike the waiting space when using the Jinfeng Jade Token before.

They had arrived at the actual location of the Law Enforcement Hall.

A circular dome, densely packed with starlike points.

Chapter 1141: Time Flows Through Gaps

The Flow of Time

Upon closer inspection, those starlike points resembled tiny windows.

Through these windows, varying scenes were reflected.

Countless characters swirled, clearly representing cultivation techniques.

Beneath the dome, no Law Enforcement Hall cultivators were visible, only streaks of light continuously shuttling through the space.

Sun Xingyao seemed to be reporting to someone. After a short while, a figure flew down from the dome and landed before Li Fan and the two of them.

The avatar, formed entirely of flowing characters, was not a real person.

He sized up Li Fan and nodded slightly. "Little fellow, I saw you over a hundred years ago. You were a Golden Core cultivator then. In the blink of an eye, you've grown so much..."

"Follow me."

With that, the characters paved a path leading directly to the dome.

Li Fan followed Sun Xingyao, standing on this path of characters. After a moment, his body seemed to transform into characters as well, about to scatter across the path and form an article.

A sense of crisis suddenly surged within him.

Li Fan sensed that under the influence of the surrounding characters, his memories within his soul seemed to be involuntarily seeping out, writing the chapters of his past life.

"Is this how they probe one's past experiences by perceiving the soul's memories?"

Li Fan pondered this and immediately reproduced the memories of the first half of Sun Ang's life, which he had possessed, within his soul. He then released them, allowing them to be perceived by the character path beneath them.

The transformed characters bore unique personal markers, clearly distinct from the path underfoot.

As for Sun Xingyao, he seemed to have been unaffected by the inspection.

The character path quickly reached its destination, and Li Fan and Sun Xingyao arrived at a starlike window above the dome.

Their figures transformed back from characters into human form, though Li Fan's experiences were recorded separately in a scroll.

The guiding cultivator now revealed his true appearance.

He looked even younger than "Sun Ang," around seventeen or eighteen years old.

His long hair fell to his shoulders, with a cinnabar mark between his brows, giving him a delicate and gentle appearance.

"This is Elder Nangong of the Law Enforcement Hall," Sun Xingyao introduced to Li Fan.

Nangong glanced at the scroll in his hand and nodded slightly. "No problems. This first round of tests is considered passed."

With a casual toss, the scroll containing "Sun Ang's" life story turned into a streak of light and flew off somewhere unknown.

Li Fan observed his surroundings.

It was as if he were in the void outside the Xuanhuang Realm, with a giant light cluster floating before him.

Much like the miniature model of the Xuanhuang Realm he had seen in the long-distance teleportation formation,

"Passing through the [Xuanhuang Realm] without causing the light cluster to vibrate means passing the second test," Nangong said, then transformed into a beam of light and flew ahead.

Li Fan did not hesitate and followed closely.

The yellow halo was dreamlike and illusory, even giving off a strange sense of warmth. It was like returning to the womb, without any mishaps. Li Fan soon flew out of the light cluster.

As he left, he even felt a faint sense of reluctance.

Li Fan keenly sensed that the operational speed of his [Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Incantation] had increased several times over its usual pace!

"Is this to verify whether one is a native cultivator of the Xuanhuang Realm?"

Li Fan suddenly understood something in his heart.

The third test was to verify whether one was a cultivator of the Five Elders Society.

In the void, five stone statues with obscured faces circled around.

Li Fan needed to stand still within the encirclement of the stone statues for half an hour.

If there were no abnormalities during this period, he would pass the test.

In this lifetime, Li Fan was clean and pure. He had not yet had any connection with the Five Elders Society.

Therefore, he passed the test with ease.

"These stone statues are quite remarkable. They seem to possess a trace of the power of the Five Heavenly Venerates' contrary logic..."

While being observed by the Five Elders Society's stone statues, Li Fan was also observing the five Heavenly Venerates.

He also had a realization: "Even if it's not the Heavenly Venerates themselves, it's not far from it." "If I were to arrive here after experiencing Sister Zhao's illusion, even if it were just a clone that had experienced it..." "It would likely trigger a reaction from the stone statues."

The five stone statues dispersed, and Li Fan faced the final test before taking office.

The surroundings suddenly fell into a void.

Sun Xingyao and Elder Nangong, who had been beside him moments ago, suddenly disappeared.

Li Fan frowned slightly and scanned his surroundings.

He did not detect any abnormalities.

It was not a trap, nor did it involve any conspiracy.

This was simply a void.

Apart from Li Fan, there was nothing else.

"What is this testing?"

Li Fan finally understood and did not rush.

He stood in the void, waiting to see what tricks the Law Enforcement Hall had up its sleeve.

In the void, time seemed to lose its meaning.

After an unknown period, even Li Fan, with his patience, began to feel annoyed.

It felt as if the entire world had forgotten him, and everything in the world except himself had disappeared.

Elder Nangong still showed no signs of appearing.

"Could they just leave me here?"

Driven by his innate distrust of others, this thought arose in Li Fan's mind.

He even considered revealing his true cultivation, breaking through this mechanism, and leaving directly.

However, this idea was immediately suppressed.

Calming his emotions, Li Fan opened the "Return to Truth" panel.

He confirmed that it was still Anchor Year 8, and all his anxiety and unease completely disappeared.

In the void, he continued to wait.

After what felt like hundreds or even thousands of years, Li Fan suddenly thought of something.

He began to appear somewhat impatient.

Instead of standing still, he flew around, exploring, seemingly trying to find a way out.

Then, Li Fan slowly amplified the emotions he was displaying.

However, he maintained perfect control, only showing some negative emotions.

After another period, as if hundreds or thousands of years had passed...

Finally, in the dark void, light reappeared.

Elder Nangong and Sun Xingyao reappeared.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes slightly, putting on an expression as if he had returned after a long absence. He even examined them carefully, as if contemplating their identities.

"This final test is also passed," Elder Nangong finally revealed a smile.

He looked at Li Fan and exclaimed with praise, "Your disposition is quite good. You endured over two hundred years in the flow of time before showing slight signs of losing control. And you maintained your reason. This result is quite excellent among past tests."

Li Fan remained silent for a long time upon hearing this.

It seemed he was processing the information.

Elder Nangong continued to explain, "This test is to examine the stability of a cultivator's mentality."

"After all, you will be accompanying Yanfajue for over three hundred years and cannot leave for any reason. If you were to break down mentally midway and become insane, it would be problematic."

Li Fan suddenly asked, "Are there any cultivators who have remained completely calm from beginning to end, showing no signs of impatience?"

One more chapter will be out around 1 AM. My hand is injured, so typing is a bit slow.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1142: The Law of Deduction Never Rests

Yanfajue Never Rests

Elder Nangong seemed surprised by Li Fan's question and paused for a moment.

Then, his gaze suddenly deepened. "If such a person truly exists..."

"Then we must absolutely not let him approach Yanfajue."

"To be alone for hundreds of years and maintain a consistently calm demeanor. Either one is a lunatic, or has an extremely peculiar temperament..."

Li Fan interrupted him. "I've heard that unparalleled geniuses can remain focused even after meditating for a hundred years. Not losing their composure due to being confined is perfectly normal, isn't it?"

Elder Nangong let out a wry smile, shook his head slightly, and stated with certainty, "Such geniuses wouldn't come here. Unless they have ulterior motives."

Li Fan was dumbfounded.

Sun Xingyao's expression also became somewhat awkward.

"Alright, welcome to the Law Enforcement Hall. Next, I will explain some special precautions. Besides the various regulations of the Immortal Alliance, there are more points to pay attention to when interacting with Yanfajue."

"Brother Sun, you may leave now. Your task is considered complete."

As soon as Elder Nangong said this, Sun Xingyao let out a sigh of relief.

After giving Li Fan a few more admonitions, he took his leave.

After rambling on for almost half an hour, Nangong then led Li Fan out of this space.

After completing the appointment procedures and receiving the materials for the Law Enforcement Hall elders, Li Fan put on the black and gold trimmed robes unique to the Law Enforcement Hall. He followed Nangong to the brightest starlike point at the very center of the dome.

"Once I send you in, completing the final handover, I will be free."

Nangong smiled, clearly expressing genuine happiness.

"Oh, right, one last piece of advice. There are two other Law Enforcement Hall elders who will guard with you. Unless absolutely necessary, do not communicate or speak with them via sound transmission."

"The space where Yanfajue resides records every ripple of sound transmission. And a dedicated person checks them periodically."

Nangong transmitted his message secretly, his expressionless face remaining unchanged.

It was as if he wasn't the one speaking.

Li Fan cupped his hands in thanks.

Then, bidding farewell to Nangong, he soared into the white starlike point.

What greeted his eyes was a scene he was already very familiar with – the space where Yanfajue resided.

A giant sphere composed of countless characters.

The characters on the sphere were in constant, endless transformation every moment.

Occasionally, an entire passage of characters on the sphere would pause momentarily, then emit a flash of light and disappear.

After which, the endless transformation and deduction would begin anew.

Beneath this giant spherical structure, a desk floated in the void.

A petite girl, appearing to be only five or six years old, was slumped over the desk.

She looked listlessly at the constantly appearing text on the desk.

ωwш⊕⊕CΟ

Just as Li Fan had seen her every time before.

As if sensing the newcomer, Yanfajue slightly raised her head.

Seeing Li Fan's stern expression and the black and gold robes he wore, she pouted and lowered her head again.

"Another ugly person arrived."

Li Fan clearly heard Yanfajue's soft murmur.

His body involuntarily paused.

"Heh heh heh, you'll get used to it later." An ancient voice echoed beside Li Fan.

It was one of the Dao Integration elders hiding here, responsible for the guard duties, transmitting his voice.

"Zhang Xu." He briefly introduced himself and then fell silent.

As for the other colleague, he never greeted Li Fan.

Li Fan paid it no mind and flew towards his "workstation."

The so-called "workstation" was actually a special position within this space.

It was like a key nexus in a formation, allowing one to oversee everything below with a commanding view of all energy fluctuations around.

Most of the time guarding Yanfajue was spent in this specific location.

"This is truly worse than being imprisoned. No wonder none of the Sun family's Dao Integration elders were willing to come."

Arriving at his post, Li Fan couldn't help but sigh.

He feigned observing his surroundings, seemingly familiarizing himself with the work environment, but in reality, he was secretly contemplating loopholes in the surveillance system.

Besides the constantly shifting light and shadow of the giant character sphere, the atmosphere here remained quiet, even suffocating.

Li Fan, despite his efforts, found no clues on how to bypass the restrictions and make contact with Yanfajue in a short time.

And so, roughly half a year passed like this.

Suddenly, the little loli, who had been diligently working at the desk, sat up straight, raising her hands.

She exclaimed excitedly, "Yay! It's time for a break!"

With that, she slumped back down.

"Six hours."

At this moment, the voices of Zhang Xu and the other Dao Integration guard simultaneously rang out.

Six hours was Yanfajue's rare break time.

Upon reaching the designated time, she had to be woken up promptly.

Looking at Yanfajue sleeping soundly, Li Fan sighed inwardly, "This is truly inhumane."

"At least twelve hours of rest should be allowed."

During the six months he had been on duty, for some unknown reason, no cultivator had entered this space using a Jinfeng Jade Token.

This meant Yanfajue had almost no opportunity to slack off.

After some thought, Li Fan still posed his questions to Elder Zhang Xu.

After all, this fell within the scope of his duties. Zhang Xu remained silent for a moment before replying, "Three years ago, a spy from the Five Elders Society somehow obtained a Jinfeng Jade Token and infiltrated. They intended malicious acts. Although we discovered it and stopped them in time, preventing any serious consequences, it still alerted the higher echelons of the Immortal Alliance."

"Until the responsibility for this incident is resolved, the process of using Jinfeng has been completely suspended."

"It is estimated that it will take several more years for it to resume."

Zhang Xu spoke briefly and then fell silent.

Li Fan pondered, "Each Jinfeng Jade Token is incredibly precious, awarded by the Immortal Alliance to cultivators who have made outstanding contributions."

"It actually fell into the hands of the Five Elders Society. And according to Nangong's instructions earlier, the possibility of Five Elders Society spies infiltrating is not low. It happens roughly once every few decades..."

"Although they are no match for the Myriad Immortals Alliance in direct confrontation, the Myriad Immortals Alliance is somewhat inferior when it comes to such cunning schemes."

Thanks to the Heaven Profound Mirror's Origin permission, which possessed heavenly capabilities, Li Fan knew the approximate whereabouts of most of the Jinfeng Jade Tokens currently in circulation.

"As one of the three guards, I am under strict surveillance, making it difficult to act directly."

"Perhaps I can take an indirect approach, using the Jinfeng Jade Token to create an opportunity to interact with Yanfajue alone."

Li Fan pondered inwardly.

Twelve hours passed quickly.

However...

Yanfajue remained slumped over the long table, fast asleep.

She showed no signs of waking up.

From the other two guards at the Dao Integration stage, Li Fan could vaguely sense a hint of helplessness.

"Brother Sun, it's your turn." Zhang Xu transmitted mentally with a chuckle.

Chapter 1143: The Stars of Xuanhuang Return

Xuanhuang Stars Return

Li Fan could acutely sense that Yanfajue had long since woken up.

Her current posture of being slumped over the long table was undoubtedly an act of feigning sleep.

The three accompanying cultivators were all aware of this, and Li Fan was asked to wake the little loli simply because he was "the newcomer."

Li Fan was well aware of Yanfajue's temperament: childish, prone to holding grudges, and petty.

She certainly wouldn't show a good face to anyone who disturbed her rest.

As for them, the guards, their responsibility was merely to monitor. They truly couldn't do anything to Yanfajue.

If the little ancestor threw a tantrum, they could only coax and indulge her.

Sensing the two divine senses falling upon him, Li Fan did not refuse.

Following the method previously taught by Elder Nangong, he invoked the sealing power of this Yanfa space and conjured a bronze gong above the little loli's head.

Then he struck it fiercely.

Clang!

Yanfajue's body trembled violently, and she suddenly lifted her head.

Her gaze immediately locked onto Li Fan, the perpetrator, her small face filled with anger.

Li Fan shrugged his shoulders, feigning innocence: "Rest time has already exceeded six hours. It's time to get back to work."

Yanfajue continued to stare wide-eyed, fixing her gaze on Li Fan.

It was as if Li Fan had committed some egregious sin.

Li Fan put on a stern face and continued, "Oh, and according to the rules, the time exceeded this time will be deducted from your next holiday."

"Uh... the time you spent staring at me also counts."

Li Fan rubbed his face, seemingly unbothered by Yanfajue continuing to stare.

Upon hearing that her next holiday time would be reduced, Yanfajue's demeanor instantly changed, becoming like a startled kitten.

A layer of mist gathered in her large eyes, and she looked at the other two guards with a face full of grievance.

Zhang Xu and the other turned their heads away.

Li Fan, however, revealed a gentle smile, observing Yanfajue with an expression of someone watching a good show.

He even conjured a sand hourglass, recording the passage of time.

After a period of stalemate, seeing the sand in the hourglass accumulating, Yanfajue finally couldn't hold back.

She glared fiercely at Li Fan, and with a slam of her small hand on the table,

the character light ball, which had been somewhat stagnant, instantly began to spin rapidly again.

Li Fan's smile remained unchanged.

Having spent several hundred years here, all he could do was tease the little loli to pass the time.

Just as Li Fan successfully infiltrated and approached Yanfajue.

In Great Qi, the Holy Capital.

After eight years of earth-shattering development, the Holy Dynasty's aura had transformed from crimson to purple.

As a result, the clone Li Ping's cultivation of the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex successfully advanced to the fourth layer.

"Leveraging the majestic fortune of hundreds of millions of beings, I now possess the strength to contend with cultivators at the Great Perfection of Deification in the Xuanhuang Realm."

"If I were to develop for a few more decades, fully capitalizing on this small world, it might not be impossible to rival the Dao Integration stage."

"However, to go further and rival longevity..."

The clone Li Ping shook his head slightly.

"The Myriad Spirits Grand Formation has been preliminarily established. It is time to expand our territory."

With a thought from Li Ping, Sun Erlang and Wang Xuanba appeared before him shortly after.

"Greetings, Master."

The two bowed in unison.

The clone Li Ping waved his hand, and a map resembling a sky filled with dense stars materialized out of thin air.

Each white light spot represented a grotto-heaven or a small world.

Great Qi itself, in contrast, emitted a sacred purple light.

Sun Erlang looked up at the map before him, lost in thought.

As his divine sense focused on those white light spots, information about the small worlds they represented simultaneously appeared in his mind.

"I have already explained the current structure of the Xuanhuang Realm to you before."

"Currently, we have not yet directly confronted the forces of the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Society. Therefore, the national policy for the next hundred years is to consolidate the power of various small worlds and expand the territory of the Holy Dynasty."

"A united myriad realms, counter-attacking Xuanhuang."

The clone Li Ping did not shy away from the current weaknesses of the Great Qi Dynasty, but instead painted a bright future for the Holy Dynasty for his two beloved disciples.

As for the Myriad Immortals Alliance, Sun Erlang was not ignorant. He even knew about the existence of the highest powers within the Alliance, such as the Dharma Transmission and the Mirror Holder.

Upon hearing the great emperor's divine plan, he did not feel a sense of absurdity like a moth flying into a flame.

Instead, his blood surged, and he felt eager to try.

It was not that Sun Erlang was ignorant, but rather that over these eight years, he had witnessed firsthand the various changes of the Holy Dynasty. Compared to what he had seen of the Myriad Immortals Alliance,

Sun Erlang firmly believed that sooner or later, the Holy Dynasty would eliminate the Myriad Immortals Alliance and unify the Xuanhuang Realm!

Over the past eight years, the population of the Great Qi Holy Dynasty had increased fivefold, and the average lifespan had soared from forty to seventy-three years.

With no more exploitation or oppression, everyone could study and cultivate.

It was a hundred times better than the rule of sages described in ancient books!

In eight years, Sun Erlang had also secretly visited neighboring small worlds.

They were no different from the decadent Great Xuan Dynasty of the past.

Some people even lived worse lives than the citizens of Great Xuan.

Sun Erlang felt that spreading the glory of the Holy Dynasty and the Holy Emperor to these decadent small worlds was a noble and honorable undertaking.

Therefore, upon hearing the Holy Emperor's explicit declaration, boundless fighting spirit ignited in Sun Erlang's heart.

Currently, Great Qi had nine legions.

Each legion commander had already achieved the Nascent Soul cultivation.

And as the commander of these legion commanders, Sun Erlang, who cultivated the "Seated Immortal Art," had a strength close to the Deification stage.

If it weren't for the Holy Emperor saying that his foundation was unstable and needed to accumulate more experience, he would likely have been able to absorb the changes in heaven and earth and complete his breakthrough by now.

Achieving Deification in eight years - Sun Erlang believed this cultivation speed was astonishing even in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Those so-called prodigies of Xuanhuang were not even a match for his legion commanders.

...

The more he understood, the more confident Sun Erlang became in the future of the Holy Dynasty.

"Give you one year to prepare."

"After one year, the Holy Dynasty's army will depart from the Holy Capital to conquer the myriad realms!"

As Li Ping declared with a killing intent, countless purple lines extended from the purple light spot representing the Xuanhuang Realm on the map before them. They were like tentacles, tightly binding all the myriad small worlds of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Weaving into a giant net, covering the map of the integrated Xuanhuang Realm!

Sun Erlang and Wang Xuanba witnessed this scene, their breathing hitched, and their hearts surged with emotion!

With this feeling, Sun Erlang excitedly went down to summon the various legion commanders and plan the preparations for war.

Wang Xuanba, however, remained behind to accept a secret mission from the Holy Emperor.

"All Stars Return to Position?"

Wang Xuanba looked at the mission codename, somewhat puzzled.

"First, travel to Congyun Sea and Yinyin Island to find a cultivator named Yin Shangren."

Wang Xuanba silently repeated the words to himself.

There is one more chapter coming in 15 minutes.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1144: Crossing the Past and Present

Seeing Through Past and Present

"Find Yin Shangren, persuade him, and bring him back to Great Qi."

Looking at the persuasion content, which consisted of only a few words, Wang Xuanba couldn't help but scratch his head.

Although he didn't quite understand the meaning, it didn't prevent Wang Xuanba from believing implicitly.

With a low roar, the shadow beneath him began to writhe slowly. Before long, a body identical to Wang Xuanba crawled out of the shadow.

This was a skill he awakened after successfully merging and absorbing the exotic beast "Shadow Follower."

The Shadow Body possessed half the power of the original body, and death had no effect on the main body.

It was perfectly suited for such a risky errand.

With this thought, Wang Xuanba's shadow body transformed into a dark, serpentine dragon and soared into the void.

More than ten days later, he finally found Yinyin Island.

The faint wails emanating from the island made Wang Xuanba's heart tremble somewhat.

He called out several times, but no one answered. Wang Xuanba walked into the building and was even more horrified by the various strange and bizarre creatures he saw.

"These things are more disgusting than the exotic beasts I've absorbed."

Proceeding further, he finally found the person in question in front of a transparent cage.

"Sir, my Master wishes to invite you for a gathering," Wang Xuanba said neither subserviently nor arrogantly.

Yin Shangren showed no reaction at all.

Wang Xuanba repeated himself several times, with the same result.

Seeing this, Wang Xuanba directly followed the Holy Emperor's instructions and said, "Sir, do you wish to know who created the Immortal-Mortal Miasma?"

Yin Shangren's body trembled, and he slowly shifted his gaze from the experimental subject to Wang Xuanba.

"You say... what?"

The repeated words made Wang Xuanba swallow his saliva.

However, he still bravely repeated it.

Then, before Yin Shangren could speak, he added, "Sir, do you wish to know the perfect method of [Using Myself as Foundation]?"

Yin Shangren's previously hunched body slowly straightened.

He stared at Wang Xuanba, a dangerous glint appearing in his eyes: "Who exactly are you?"

Wang Xuanba chuckled, "I am merely an errand runner. If Sir wishes to know the answers to your questions, simply come with me."

"Lead the way!"

To Wang Xuanba's surprise, Yin Shangren agreed so readily this time.

Thick mist sprayed out from the cage behind him, and several mortals shrieked and vanished.

Wang Xuanba's body stiffened, and he quickly nodded.

"Oh, and my Master also reminded Sir not to forget that rib, and to bring it along."

Yin Shangren's gaze turned cold, his killing intent no longer concealable.

However, seeing Wang Xuanba's unconcerned demeanor, he still forcibly suppressed his murderous intent.

He searched his body but couldn't find the rib.

Finally, he found it in the dog's kennel, next to the small dog that looked like a human hand. He kicked the dog away and gestured that they could leave.

Wang Xuanba then flew ahead to lead the way, passing through the entrance to the small world disguised by formations, and returned to the Great Qi Dynasty.

He was slightly surprised by the dense spiritual energy concentration of this place, but Yin Shangren still focused his attention on the tallest tower-like building in the Holy Capital.

He could sense that there seemed to be an extremely powerful existence there.

Soon, Yin Shangren stood before Li Ping, the Faceless Holy Emperor.

"Daoist friend, you have gone to great lengths to lure me here. What is your intention?"

Yin Shangren's expression was not very pleasant.

"It's merely that I have long admired your talent." Li Ping sat on the high Holy Emperor's Seat, looking down at Yin Shangren and said indifferently.

"Please explain how this method works?"

Before Yin Shangren could react, Li Ping lightly patted his hand.

A light screen unfolded before Yin Shangren.

Initially, Yin Shangren didn't pay much attention, but after a single glance at the content, his expression suddenly became solemn.

Solemnity quickly turned to shock.

"This..."

He repeatedly watched it several times before looking at the clone Li Ping with disbelief.

"I heard Sir treasures a rib?" the clone Li Ping asked again, without explaining.

Yin Shangren nodded: "It is the bone of the first cultivator in the world infected by the Immortal-Mortal Miasma..."

"May I borrow it for a look?"

Yin Shangren hesitated, but finally took it out and handed it to Li Ping.

Li Ping held the rib, falling into a state of recollection.

Then he sighed, seeming somewhat melancholic and sad.

Afterward, he returned the rib to Yin Shangren.

Li Ping's behavior left Yin Shangren feeling uneasy and bewildered.

"You..."

"Meeting an old friend again, and seeing him in this state. It's just some emotion, please don't mind, Sir."

Li Ping's words struck Yin Shangren like thunder.

"What? An old friend?"

His eyes filled with suspicion, Yin Shangren stared intently at Li Ping.

Li Ping was unconcerned, his voice low: "Heh heh heh, besides me, who else in this world remembers him now?"

"Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate, the perfect person in the world. Su Bai, Mr. Bai..."

As he spoke, a figure appeared before Yin Shangren.

It instantly captured Yin Shangren's attention.

The person in the image had such perfect features, without a single flaw.

His eyes were filled with gentleness and love; even in a virtual image, eye contact with him caused one's heart to tremble.

Yin Shangren was mesmerized for a long time.

Then, recalling Li Ping's words, his body shook violently, and he finally reacted: "What did you say? Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate?"

He instinctively clenched the rib in his hand, as if struck by lightning.

His eyes became vacant, and he mumbled, "Defying the principles of heaven and earth, defying the principles of heaven and earth..."

"Immortal-Mortal Miasma, Twin Heavenly Venerates..."

"It's actually like this?"

...

Yin Shangren staggered and collapsed helplessly to the ground.

As if suffering a major blow, he seemed to have lost all purpose, becoming lost and bewildered.

Li Ping waited for a long time until Yin Shangren slowly recovered from his shock.

Only then did he continue, revealing his ultimate purpose.

"The immortal path ahead cannot be trod, the Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate is above."

"Sir, can you help me fulfill Mr. Bai's unfinished wish, use the new dharma to break the foundation of the Dharma Transmission, and save Xuanhuang from dire straits?"

Li Ping stepped down from the emperor's seat, approached Yin Shangren, and helped him up, asking with utmost seriousness.

Yin Shangren quickly understood Li Ping's meaning.

"You mean, this flawless [Using Myself as Foundation Method] is his doing?" Yin Shangren's voice trembled slightly.

Li Ping nodded, sighing, "Yes. In the entire Xuanhuang Realm, besides him, who else could possess such talent?"

Yin Shangren's shock deepened.

"Yes, yes." He repeatedly murmured.

Looking again at the characters on the light screen before him, Yin Shangren seemed to be looking through the words, crossing through time, and meeting Mr. Bai's gaze.

"My thoughts and ideas are actually in sync with his from thousands of years ago?"

"Moreover, he was far superior to me..."

...

Li Ping looked at the completely lost Yin Shangren, knowing that the plan had succeeded.

Chapter 1145: Transmitting the Dharma, Old Acquaintance

Dharma Transmission Is An Old Acquaintance

"Can you tell me his story?"

Yin Shangren, slumped on the ground, asked somewhat dazed.

Breaking the prolonged silence.

Not long ago, Yin Shangren, who had held a sliver of hope, had conducted the final experimental verification in the underground prison of the Holy Capital.

The result was no different from what Li Ping had said.

Therefore, he said nothing more, carefully storing away Mr. Bai's rib.

He then returned to the Holy Emperor's Seat, staring blankly at Mr. Bai's image.

Li Ping did not interrupt, also staring intently at the portrait.

As if also in remembrance.

It was at this moment that Yin Shangren's question fell perfectly into Li Ping's lap.

He immediately recounted Mr. Bai's general life experiences.

Yin Shangren listened spellbound.

"I only knew that in the ancient Xuanhuang Realm, there existed a Great Heavenly Venerate who surpassed all Longevity Realm experts. I never imagined that..."

"Such a figure would sacrifice himself for mortals."

Yin Shangren's face showed confusion and bewilderment.

"The deceased is gone. What we can do is to fulfill Mr. Bai's last wish, to console his spirit in heaven."

"The reason I established this [Holy Dynasty Qi] was also for these mortals. Sir, compare the lives of mortals within my Dynasty to those in the Xuanhuang Realm."

Yin Shangren turned his head, his gaze seeming to sweep across all parts of Great Qi in an instant.

After a moment, he nodded slightly, sighing in admiration: "Compared to the situation in the Xuanhuang Realm where mortals are treated like livestock, your domain can be considered an ideal prosperous era for mortals."

"My aspiration is to extend this system to all the small worlds of Xuanhuang, and even to the Xuanhuang Realm itself!" Li Ping declared proudly.

Yin Shangren sized up Li Ping, sighed, and did not refute.

Li Ping smiled slightly: "Sir, there is no need to be disheartened. Please listen to me first."

"Xuanhuang's strength lies in its Dharma Transmission. Dharma Transmission's invincibility lies in its new dharma. If we can use the dharma passed down by Mr. Bai to undermine the foundation of Dharma Transmission..."

"Once the Dharma Transmission is resolved, others in the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Society will be like clay chickens and dogs."

Yin Shangren stared blankly at Li Ping, wondering why this cultivator, whose aura was only at the Deification stage, spoke with such immense confidence.

More importantly, Yin Shangren felt a strong sense of self-assurance from him.

"It doesn't seem like empty talk? Could it be that this gentleman has hidden his strength?" Yin Shangren carefully examined Li Ping again.

"To undermine the foundation of Dharma Transmission, I believe no one in this world but you can do it." Li Ping said again with utmost seriousness, not avoiding Yin Shangren's scrutiny.

Yin Shangren hesitated: "With my talent alone, I'm afraid..."

Li Ping leaned forward, tightly grasping Yin Shangren's hands: "Sir, I believe in you!"

Li Ping's eyes were filled with sincerity: "If ten years are not enough, then a hundred. If a hundred years are not enough, then a thousand! I have waited for so long, and finally found this sliver of hope. How can I give up easily?"

"I'm sure you wouldn't want to let Mr. Bai's expectations down, would you?"

Yin Shangren trembled slightly, instinctively clenching his fists.

"Sir, just focus on researching the new dharma. All other problems will be handled by me."

After this conversation, Yin Shangren finally gained the intention to stay here and study the dharma after using myself as a foundation.

For him, there was no limit to lifespan. If he didn't find something he was willing to do, he would likely lose his sense of self and assimilate with the wandering souls of the world before long.

Having received Yin Shangren's promise, Li Ping was overjoyed.

He immediately led him into the secret underground space in the Holy Capital.

It turned out that a large area had already been prepared for Yin Shangren's private research space.

"I have a plan. Sir, see if it's feasible."

"Select a group of budding youths with great talent, impart the [Method of Using Oneself as Foundation] to them, and then..."

Li Ping detailed the method he had used before.

Yin Shangren pondered for a moment, his expression becoming somewhat solemn: "It might be feasible. However, the specifics still require further practical verification."

Li Ping waved his hand: "The thoughts and ideas of children are as wild as the wind. Even if they can't forge a path through sheer luck, as long as it can provide even a little inspiration to Sir, that would be enough."

Yin Shangren was clearly not a pedantic person and agreed to Li Ping's plan.

He felt little sympathy for the inevitably tragic lives of these chosen children.

"By the way, there's something that has been bothering me, and I've always wanted to accomplish it, but haven't found a way..." Li Ping paused, seeming hesitant.

Yin Shangren glanced at Li Ping, signaling him to continue.

"Mr. Bai's remains are scattered throughout the Xuanhuang Realm. I wish to gather them and give him a proper burial. Other than that, it's mostly fine, as those are privately collected by cultivators. Only..."

"His skull is collected by the Myriad Immortals Alliance in their headquarters' Museum of Divine Treasures."

A trace of ferocity flickered in Li Ping's eyes as he spoke hatefully: "It is viewed by those insects of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, who point and gawk with no respect. Every time I think of it, I wish I could rush in regardless of the consequences and snatch back the skull."

"Unfortunately, I tried once. There was absolutely no possibility of success. The Museum of Divine Treasures seems to have a mysterious expert hidden within. Even placing Mr. Bai's skull in the very center of the Museum of Divine Treasures was his idea. It's clearly a trap, designed to lure people like me who value Mr. Bai to fall into it..."

"You've been to the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters?" Yin Shangren asked, startled.

After Li Ping described all the scenes and details of his infiltration, Yin Shangren's gaze towards him subtly changed.

"I was able to infiltrate once, and I can infiltrate a second time. But only that Museum of Divine Treasures..."

"It's truly difficult." Li Ping sighed.

Yin Shangren then said, "Daoist friend, you need not be discouraged. Actually, back then, I also had the same thought. However, after clarifying the identity of the Museum's curator, I gave up."

"This person is one of the three Demon Beast Race Emperors, who has existed since ancient times. Even the Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate treated him with courtesy back then..."

Li Ping frowned slightly: "He has such strength? Mr. Bai, who killed these demon beasts like slaughtering chickens and dogs back then."

"Dharma Transmission is even superior to Mr. Bai. With Dharma Transmission's strength and status, why would he need to be courteous to that Emperor?"

His tone was full of doubt, obviously Li Ping did not believe Yin Shangren's words.

Yin Shangren shook his head slightly: "In any case, I can be sure that when Dharma Transmission met that person back then, it was indeed the case. His attitude was completely different from how he treated others."

"Either his strength was recognized by Dharma Transmission, or..."

Yin Shangren paused: "They knew each other long ago."

"But it should have been their first meeting, right?" Yin Shangren lowered his voice, clearly confused himself.

Li Ping knew that Yin Shangren was a remnant soul from an old world that had been devoured by the Xuanhuang Realm.

He possessed fragmented memories of a bygone era, so what he saw should not be false.

"Di San Mo was originally an elder of the Beast Taming Sect, belonging to the lineage of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects. When the Ten Sects came into conflict with Dharma Transmission, he actually chose to side with Dharma Transmission. Furthermore, thousands of years later, he transformed into the curator of the Museum of Divine Treasures and one of the three highest ruling powers of the Immortal Alliance, the [Illusory Sage]..."

"An old acquaintance?"

Li Ping suddenly thought of a question.

Did the Heavenly Law Realm have existence of demon beasts?

The Xuanhuang demon beasts were all derived from Di Yi.

Then what about the Heavenly Law Realm?

...

At the same time.

Li Fan's true self, in Yanfajue's space within the Immortal Alliance headquarters, suddenly had a barely perceptible gleam in his eyes.

"Perhaps, I need to make another trip to the Immortal Ruins."

Only one chapter today. The next chapter will be released around 1 AM tomorrow. My heart is racing, so I'll get some sleep early.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1146: Young Master Qingxuan of the Business World

The Young Lord of Qing Xuan

The Divine Beast Emperor had long since led his beast horde to flee the Xuanhuang Realm, while Di San Mo remained hidden deep within the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, rarely seen by ordinary people. However, both had appeared during the "Change of the Beastmaster Sect" in the Immortal Ruins, making it possible to seek them out for clarification.

"Fellow Daoist Sun?" Elder Zhang Xu's telepathic message broke Li Fan's train of thought. His attention returned to the Yanfa Jue guarding space. The little loli was processing an urgent Yanfa task. With this new responsibility appearing out of nowhere, she looked sulky and full of resentment. The task only required a Harmonious Dao cultivation technique, yet it had already taken three days and three nights, and she still hadn't deduced it. There was a high probability that this little ancestor was slacking off.

In the Yanfa space, besides the three Harmonious Dao guards, there was also a young man in green. Although he stood tall and still, his demeanor revealed his inner anxiety. Considering the high level of this Yanfa task, delaying it could cause trouble. Guard Zhang Xu secretly sent another telepathic message, asking Li Fan to play the villain. After all, during this time, Li Fan's image in Yanfa Jue's mind had already been categorized as the most detestable person in the world. He no longer needed to conjure the bronze gong to remind her. When a sand timer silently appeared above the little loli's head, her expression changed dramatically, and the rotation speed of the character light sphere instantly increased severalfold. Not long after, the cultivation technique required by the young man in green was deduced.

The young man expressed his profuse thanks and then hastily departed. "So rushed, it seems the Qing Xuan Army has encountered trouble," Zhang Xu sighed. After repeatedly intervening and stopping Yanfa Jue's slacking behavior, Li Fan had gradually become familiar with the other two Harmonious Dao guards. Zhang Xu had entered this place more than a hundred years before Li Fan. As for the other, named Hua Yueye, although his name sounded somewhat feminine, he was a true tough guy. Hating evil as he hated his enemies, he had even fought with a Dharma Transmitting cultivator on the spot because he couldn't stand his behavior. The consequences were predictable. Although he was helped by friends and family and ultimately spared his life, he was still punished to guard Yanfa Jue here for five hundred years. Not even half of that time had passed yet. When Li Fan first arrived, Hua Yueye couldn't even be bothered to greet him, but now that they were familiar, he talked more than Zhang Xu.

"Although I dislike the Young Lord Shang's demeanor, being stationed in the Demon Suppressing Abyss for centuries without leaving his post is truly admirable... The Qing Xuan Army..." Through the snippets of their conversation, Li Fan recalled the identity of the green-robed cultivator from earlier. They had met once before; his name was Yan Huan. A confidant of Young Lord Shang, he was stationed in the Broken Hand Immortal City within the white mist, responsible for guarding and suppressing the "Roaring Abyss" along with the million-strong Qing Xuan Army. "My Young Lord's temper is even worse than mine. Once he sets his mind on something, even a Heavenly Venerate might not be able to change his mind. Yet, he still hasn't given up on a rejected proposal from both the Dharma Transmitting cultivator and the Mirror Holder, even after so many years." "Cough, cough, be careful with your words!"

Based on the fragments of their conversation and some secret information he had previously perused, Li Fan meticulously pieced together a covered-up history of the Immortal Alliance. In those days, the "expedition into the White Mist Labyrinth and expansion of exploration" was popular in the Immortal Alliance. This was somewhat different from the Great Exploration Era Li Fan had experienced. In that epoch, the exploration conducted by the Sky Profound Mirror for its sublimation was more like a full-scan of the white mist, marking all the hidden labyrinths and secret realms within. However, it did not delve deeply into the labyrinths themselves. The proposal rejected by the Dharma Transmitting cultivators, on the other hand, suggested a thorough cleansing of the labyrinths. The white mist barrier of the Xuanhuang Realm had appeared too strangely, and the labyrinths within the white mist were even more bizarre, hiding countless secrets. Just the ones Li Fan had encountered included world fragments destroyed by the Chaotic Character Technique, a frozen formation that reversed life and death, and a giant made of countless corpses... Putting aside the danger, Li Fan didn't believe that cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance were not curious about the labyrinths. However, this curiosity was decisively suppressed by the higher echelons of the Immortal Alliance.

"The Dharma Transmission's dismemberment and remaking of Xuanhuang, coupled with the unified stance of the Immortal Alliance's high command, clearly indicates that these labyrinths in the white mist are inextricably linked to Him." Li Fan recalled that when he was in the white mist, he often heard wails and murmurs similar to those of the Heavenly Doctor. Following the sensory guidance of the sound, he would always discover unknown labyrinths. Li Fan immediately formed a guess. "These labyrinths, like Congyun Sea and Luoyan State, are remnants of the former Heavenly Law Realm. However, perhaps due to the influence of calamities like the Chaotic Character Technique, their residual laws are more twisted and chaotic, not suitable for direct integration with the Xuanhuang Realm. Thus, they were first hidden within the white mist. Hmm... perhaps there are also remnants of other cultivation worlds." "The Dharma Transmission is waiting. Waiting for the moment the Heavenly Law Realm successfully possesses a new body." His attainments had not yet reached the level of the Dharma Transmission, so Li Fan could not yet fathom the specific uses of these world fragments. "However, this does give me inspiration. Although the Dharma Transmitting Heavenly Venerate has absolute power, the cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm still harbor doubts about the drastic changes caused by His world transformation. Perhaps we can guide them to uncover the truth behind it." Li Fan knew that the more something was forbidden, the more it would arouse people's curiosity. Once these cultivators discovered the grand conspiracy potentially involving the Dharma Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, they would, willingly or unwillingly, become Li Fan's allies. "Young Lord Shang, let's start with him." Li Fan nodded slightly, concealing the glint in his eyes.

...

In the Sword Mound within the ruins of the Heavenly Sword Sect. The Saintly Fetus Li Fan sat cross-legged beside the black sword, comprehending the myriad sword dao swirling around him. Although he had previously established his dao foundation using the Black Sword Tian Zhi Qi, here, surrounded by countless swords in the sword mound, the Saintly Fetus Li Fan still experienced new insights constantly. "Tian Zhi Qi is the manifestation of Heavenly Dao laws." "The world changes, laws flow; they are not immutable. The timing of my arrival here to collect the black sword differs, thus the sword dao generated also has subtle variations." The Saintly Fetus Li Fan rejoiced. His understanding of the world's operations deepened further. With a surge of inspiration, he let out a long roar, and the ten thousand swords on the ground trembled slightly in response. In the center of the myriad swords, the wooden sword left by Mr. Bai actually bent slightly, as if resonating with the Saintly Fetus Li Fan's comprehension. "Good." The Saintly Fetus Li Fan opened his mouth slightly, and the black sword soared into the air, entering his abdomen and transforming into his own dao foundation.

Chapter 1147: Suppressing Demonic Sound with a Single Sword

A Single Sword Suppresses the Demonic Sound

This time, obtaining the Heavenly Origin, since the Saint Fetus Li Fan had already received prior recognition, the wooden sword did not obstruct him.

The profound aura contained within the wooden sword slowly disappeared.

A mystical fluctuation gradually emerged from the Saint Fetus Li Fan's body.

The Xuanhuang Sword Dao had, at this moment, completed its transfer.

Amidst the silent reverence of the countless rusted swords in the Sword Tomb, the Saint Fetus Li Fan slowly departed.

"Possessing the Heavenly Origin, one can directly enter the Dao Integration realm."

"A sword as a foundation, the way of the sword, the sword transforming into a grotto-heaven, and..."

Li Fan, whose true self had already reached Deification, instantly understood the path the Saint Fetus was about to take.

"The transformation of the Xuanhuang Sword Dao itself."

"Afterward, one only needs to completely merge the Heavenly Origin with oneself to essentially devour and fully master the power of the laws of heaven and earth, achieving the status of a Dao Integration Immortal Venerable."

"Compared to ordinary cultivators of the New Dharma, it is indeed much easier. But as a price..."

"It practically severs the possibility of achieving longevity through defying logic. Just like Mr. Bai, who was the Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate, defied the principles of heaven and earth he presided over. Even if he possessed peerless talent and could succeed in defying the principles, he could never escape the backlash of the heavens and earth."

"The day of proving the Dao will be the day of his demise."

Thoughts churned in the Saint Fetus Li Fan's mind, and his realm also steadily climbed.

When he left the Sword Tomb, he was still in the early Foundation Establishment stage.

But by the time he exited Tianyou State, the Saint Fetus Li Fan had already advanced to the Golden Core stage.

And when the Saint Fetus Li Fan appeared outside the white mist barrier that concealed the Chizha Abyss, he had already entered the Nascent Soul stage.

Without needing to deliberately absorb, and without any hindrance, the spiritual energy of heaven and earth surged forth, pouring into the Saint Fetus Li Fan's body.

It transformed into a ladder for steady advancement.

"This is the benefit of receiving the acknowledgment of the Heavenly Dao."

"This is merely the Dao of [Sword]. If it were the entire Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, I cannot even imagine. No wonder Mr. Bai could advance from Deification to Longevity in one step..."

With the Heavenly Origin in his possession, cultivation no longer required external resources.

Coupled with the active cooperation of the grand cosmic trend, the Saint Fetus Li Fan's cultivation speed could no longer be measured by ordinary standards.

Sword Dao fluctuations permeated the surroundings, pushing back the Essence Devouring white mist.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan transformed into a streak of sword light and headed straight for the Broken Palm Immortal City.

As faint wails, like those of vengeful ghosts, reached his ears, the Saint Fetus Li Fan had already reached the same Deification realm as his true self.

However, after breaking through to Deification, his comprehension of the evolution of his own sword dao was still lacking.

This caused his cultivation progress to slow down considerably.

"If I refine this further in this lifetime, and come again later, my progress will be even faster."

"Halt! Who goes there!" a furious roar interrupted the Saint Fetus Li Fan's thoughts.

Simultaneously, a figure appeared and blocked Li Fan's path.

Clad in green light scale armor, holding a heavy halberd, and pointing directly at Li Fan.

"Who are you?! How dare you trespass into the Eternal Immortal Fortress!" the heavily armored cultivator questioned aggressively.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes slightly and recognized the voice.

In the 113th iteration, he had been ordered to construct the [Heavenly Profound Spirit Locking Formation] in the white mist outside the Eternal Immortal Fortress.

Later, when the Chizha Abyss suddenly became active, his outpost, designated Jiaxu, lost contact with the Immortal City.

Seeing his supplies about to run out, Li Fan reversed his Dao Heart and, alone, returned from the outpost to the Immortal City to seek rescue.

Although he encountered some minor setbacks along the way and mistakenly entered the [Chaotic Word Maze],

he eventually escaped the predicament safely.

Finally, before his lifespan ran out, he managed to return to the Broken Palm Immortal City in the nick of time.

He originally had a few decades left, but at the very last moment, a roar of "What impudent rogue!" blocked him.

Li Fan was forced to explain his reasons, which delayed him further.

By the time he returned to the Immortal City, he was exhausted and had little time left to live.

...

"Hmph!"

The Saint Fetus Li Fan glanced at the other party indifferently and did not explain.

He simply used his finger as a sword and lightly pointed forward.

The white mist, which seemed to have existed since the dawn of time, was instantly parted.

The wails from the Chizha Abyss were drowned out by a resonant sword cry.

Brilliant white sword light illuminated heaven and earth.

The Eternal Immortal Fortress, built with the remains of the ancient Heavenly Venerate's broken palm, and the terrifying abyss filled with murderous aura...

At this moment, all were exposed and rendered clear by the Saint Fetus Li Fan's sword light, revealing every detail.

The vast sword light pierced through the figure blocking Li Fan, crossed the Broken Palm Immortal City, and fiercely stabbed into the Chizha Abyss!

Heaven and earth fell silent.

As if captivated by this world-shattering sword strike, the wails from the abyss had ceased and did not reappear for a long time.

Only after the white mist slowly converged and the torn scar healed, and the abyss was once again hidden beneath the white mist,

did the murmuring wails gradually resume.

However, compared to their previous scale, they were far less intense.

Perhaps fearing further escalation and attracting another sword strike from Li Fan.

Recovering from their shock, the Xuanhuang Army within the Eternal Immortal Fortress all focused their gaze on Li Fan's position.

All was silent.

It seemed that even the thick white mist could not obscure the figure that resembled a sword immortal.

No one understood the horror of those demonic sounds better than they, the Xuanhuang Army, who had guarded the abyss for years.

But at this moment, thousands of demonic sounds were suppressed by a single sword strike.

What level of cultivation was this?

The Xuanhuang Army was stunned, their minds blank.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan stood with his hands behind his back, gazing calmly ahead.

The heavily armored cultivator in green before him had long since turned into a statue.

Facing Li Fan's single sword strike, though the sword light had not injured him, it had been deeply engraved into his mind.

From this day forward, he could no longer accommodate anything other than this sword light.

He appeared dazed, unresponsive to the outside world.

However, if he could comprehend this sword strike from Li Fan and absorb it into his own understanding,

this sword strike would be a great fortune for him, a cultivator at the Nascent Soul stage.

Even without resources for advancement, he could still defeat opponents of higher realms with this sword alone.

For Li Fan, at the present moment, there was no need to exact full vengeance on those who had offended him in the past.

If by chance he met them again, a lesson would suffice.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan's sword strike was primarily a warning, intended to force the appearance of Shang Shaojun, the leader of the Xuanhuang Army.

After all, demonstrating his strength first was the best way to negotiate the matters that followed.

As expected, facing Li Fan hovering in the white mist, no one in the Xuanhuang Army dared to step forward to greet him.

Moments later, the white mist stirred.

A figure with a strange, rippling appearance like water on its surface appeared before Li Fan.

"Fellow Daoist has a good sword!"

"I have guarded the Chizha Abyss for many years, and I never imagined such a person would appear in this world!"

Shang Shaojun stared at Li Fan: "Fellow Daoist, why have you come here?"

Li Fan pointed to the Chizha Abyss not far below and said with a smile, "The demonic sounds are ear-piercing and vexing. I wish to wield my sword and enter the abyss to end the demonic sounds forever."

"Does young lord wish to accompany me?"

The Saint Fetus Li Fan's gaze was sincere, and he spoke with utmost earnestness.

Chapter 1148: Alone, Destroying the Demon Tide

Alone, He Destroys the Demonic Tide

"Does young lord wish to accompany me?"

Li Fan's voice boomed like thunder, piercing the white mist, even temporarily suppressing the wails from the Chizha Abyss, echoing endlessly within the Eternal Immortal Fortress.

Feeling the gazes of the countless Xuanhuang Army soldiers converging on him, Shang Shaojun's constantly shifting form gradually calmed down.

He revealed his true appearance.

Clad in a green robe, his sleeves fluttering, he was tall and slender. A sharp glint flashed in his eyes as Shang Shaojun stared at Li Fan: "Fellow Daoist may be a bit overconfident. Your sword is sharp, but it might not be able to withstand that terrifying demonic sound tide. And you still claim to want to suppress the abyss forever..."

"How will we know without trying? I think young lord has been guarding the abyss for so long that your courage has been worn away!" The Saint Fetus Li Fan retorted forcefully, showing no sign of backing down.

"Hmph, mere quibbling."

In an instant, it was as if thousands of shadows appeared on Shang Shaojun's body. He himself seemed to have hidden within this dark tide, secretly observing Li Fan, ready to launch a fatal strike at any moment.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan felt as if he were surrounded by an army, even having the illusion of facing the Chizha Abyss alone.

"There is a rumor within the Immortal Alliance that says the demonic sounds from the abyss are beneficial to young lord's cultivation, which is why you are willing to guard here for a hundred years without leaving. It seems that is indeed true."

When he was still at the Foundation Establishment stage, Li Fan had personally experienced the horror of the abyss's demonic sounds up close.

And now, Shang Shaojun was like a walking abyss, capable of unleashing a demonic sound tide at any moment!

A simple, unadorned black longsword suddenly appeared above the Saint Fetus Li Fan's head.

Its tip pointed directly at Shang Shaojun.

Despite being imbued with the power of a million demonic sounds, the moment he was locked onto by the sword's edge, Shang Shaojun felt a sense of crisis.

He seemed to see countless swords pouring down like rain from behind the black sword, all pointing directly at him!

"Where did such a master come from..."

Shang Shaojun's heart grew heavy.

The two stood in confrontation in mid-air, a great battle on the verge of erupting.

At this crucial moment, a strange fluctuation emanated from not far from them.

Initially, there were a few sharp tearing sounds like autumn wind.

Then, it was like the rapid gallop of horses' hooves, suddenly erupting like a storm.

It was as if the endless hell was crying out in unison, or like the despairing wails echoing in the world before the apocalypse.

The white mist churned, rolling ceaselessly.

And the Broken Palm Immortal City, like a small boat on the sea, trembled precariously!

"Demonic Sound Tide!"

Perhaps due to the suppression of Li Fan's sword strike just now, it had provoked a backlash from the power of the Chizha Abyss.

This time, the intensity and scale of the demonic sound tide far surpassed previous occurrences.

The Eternal Immortal Fortress, directly hit by the tide, was like leaves on a tree branch, on the verge of being blown away at any moment!

Shang Shaojun's expression changed drastically. He could no longer pay attention to Li Fan, and his figure flickered as he returned to the Broken Palm Immortal City.

With Shang Shaojun's presence, the green light swirled, and the Eternal Immortal Fortress slowly stabilized amidst the demonic sound tide.

Just as the Xuanhuang Army was recovering from their shock, they were horrified to discover that Li Fan, whom they had thought had disappeared in the demonic sound tide, was still standing calmly in the void.

Even amidst the surging demonic sounds and churning white mist,

he remained completely motionless.

And then, Li Fan did something that astonished everyone.

He strolled as if sightseeing, arriving outside the Broken Palm Immortal City.

Facing the endless Chizha Abyss, Li Fan sat cross-legged.

A black longsword appeared beneath him at the right moment.

Li Fan lightly tapped the sword body with his right index finger.

"Ding!"

The crisp sound was clearer than the demonic sounds, even amidst the raging tide!

The sword's hum reverberated, and at the same time, countless different sword shadows appeared behind Li Fan.

The sword shadows stretched endlessly, like a Great Wall, standing before the Broken Palm Immortal City.

Myriad swords, like a forest, all pointed towards the abyss!

"The demonic sounds pierce the mind, yet he is completely unaffected! How did he do it?"

"Sitting in front of the city, what is he doing?"

This shocking scene rendered the million-strong Xuanhuang Army speechless.

Even Shang Shaojun jolted awake, gazing at Li Fan's back outside the city.

If the demonic sound tide was a relentless, ferocious, surging tidal wave,

then Li Fan at this moment was a giant rock standing firm on the shore,

unwavering, unmoving in all directions.

No matter how the demonic sounds raged, they could not harm him in the slightest.

And Li Fan's performance was just beginning.

"Go!"

Before the great tide, Li Fan softly uttered.

From the Great Wall formed by countless sword shadows behind him, a single sword shot out in an instant.

Just like the world-shattering sword light Li Fan had unleashed earlier, it charged headlong towards the demonic sound tide.

Facing the surging demonic sound tide, the sword light gradually dimmed.

But the Xuanhuang Army within the Broken Palm Immortal City clearly felt that the demonic sound tide had weakened considerably due to that sword light!

"Could it be..."

A thought inevitably surfaced in their minds.

Everyone in the Immortal City trembled slightly.

Then, a scene they would never forget appeared.

Tens of thousands of flying swords, one after another, fearlessly charged towards the Chizha Abyss.

Countless sword lights flashed successively, illuminating the Eternal Immortal Fortress completely.

With each attack, the demonic sound tide weakened a little more.

The terrifying wails that reached their ears gradually became faint and weak.

The vast Immortal City fell into complete silence.

Everyone was silently watching Li Fan's back.

No other thoughts could enter their minds.

Like the end of a heavy rain, the sky cleared after the storm.

Outside the Immortal City, the demonic sounds no longer echoed.

And the sword lights behind Li Fan remained.

Endless, inexhaustible.

"That Lord..."

"Perhaps his words of forever suppressing the abyss are not impossible."

The thought appeared in the minds of the Xuanhuang Army soldiers simultaneously.

Turning his back to the Broken Palm Immortal City, Li Fan did not get up.

The Xuanhuang Army seemed frozen, daring not make the slightest move.

"The sword blocks the demonic sound tide. The Xuanhuang Sword Dao's approval of me has deepened considerably."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan was, in fact, experiencing the changes happening within himself.

"As expected, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao instinctively rejects these [outsiders]. If one can conform to destiny, one will receive the corresponding favor of the Heavenly Dao."

Thinking thus, Li Fan slowly stood up, turned around, and looked at the countless cultivators within the Eternal Immortal Fortress.

He asked with a smile, "Does young lord still think I am overconfident?"

The Immortal City was dead silent.

Moments later, Shang Shaojun's figure reappeared before Li Fan.

He bowed slightly and sighed in admiration: "I was mistaken."

"Fellow Daoist's talent is rarely seen in this world."

Just as he was about to say something else, Li Fan interrupted him.

"So, does young lord wish to accompany me?"

Li Fan asked again.

Seeing this, Shang Shaojun gritted his teeth and reluctantly replied, "Since that is the case, I shall risk my life to keep you company!"

Following young lord's words, a thunderous cheer erupted from the Broken Palm Immortal City.

Chapter 1149: Annihilation Destroys the Pustule

Annihilation Destroys the Abscess

The Xuanhuang Army had guarded the Chizha Abyss for too long.

Some had been here since birth and had never left.

Family, friends.

Everything they knew bloomed and withered within the Eternal Immortal Fortress.

Most of the Xuanhuang Army had only heard about the true beauties of the Xuanhuang Realm, which they guarded, through the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

They had never actually seen them with their own eyes.

The horror of the Chizha Abyss made it impossible for them to even dream of leaving one day.

But now...

Li Fan's appearance brought a glimmer of hope into their endlessly bleak lives.

"With the two lords joining forces, perhaps the demonic sounds can truly be eliminated forever..."

The Xuanhuang Army cheered enthusiastically, their eyes fixed on Li Fan and Shang Shaojun standing outside the abyss, filled with hope.

"The cruelest thing in this world is to give hope and then cruelly extinguish it." Shang Shaojun glanced back at the expressions on the faces of his subordinates and sighed faintly.

"I had no choice but to agree to your request under duress. But in reality, I am not optimistic," he transmitted mentally.

"The Chizha Abyss is truly troublesome, and it's not just the demonic sounds. Otherwise, any Dharma Transmission cultivator from the Immortal Alliance could easily suppress it. What worries the higher echelons of the Immortal Alliance is the twisted path of world destruction from the bottom of the abyss."

"It is like a wound. If that wound is exposed, pus will flow out and infect the Xuanhuang Realm along the way..."

Forced into a corner, Shang Shaojun could only reveal the reason why the Immortal Alliance had chosen to guard rather than eradicate the problem once and for all.

"The demonic sounds are merely a superficial phenomenon. To truly eliminate the demonic sounds, one must not only suppress the demonic sounds but also deal with this wound."

Shang Shaojun originally intended to use these words to dissure Li Fan from dragging him into the depths of the abyss.

However, to his surprise, after hearing his explanation, the other party showed no astonishment, as if he had known the truth of the Chizha Abyss all along.

He even smiled slightly and retorted, "The demonic sounds are a superficial phenomenon, and the wound..."

"Is also a superficial phenomenon."

"The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao flows, constantly regenerating. If it were a normal world wound, it would heal within a hundred years at most. Yet, the Chizha Abyss has been rampant for hundreds of years and shows no signs of stopping, but is instead intensifying. Does young lord not find this curious?"

Shang Shaojun was stunned by this remark.

"You..."

His gaze towards Li Fan was filled with surprise.

Previously, he had thought Li Fan was a powerful cultivator full of righteous fervor, but now...

"My identity is not important, what matters is young lord."

"Regarding everything within the white mist labyrinth, and the strange attitude of the Myriad Immortals Alliance back then, are you truly not curious?"

Shang Shaojun's expression changed: "Are you from the Five Elders Society?"

Li Fan shook his head: "I am merely a sincere individual who does not wish to see the truth buried."

Then, Li Fan once again drew his sword and sat down: "I will wait here for three days."

"After three days, I will wield my sword and charge into the abyss."

"As for whether young lord wishes to accompany me... I will not force you."

Shang Shaojun remained silent.

His figure rippled like water and disappeared.

Three days passed in the blink of an eye.

During this period, Li Fan remained at the mouth of the abyss.

Whenever demonic sounds reappeared, he easily annihilated them with his sword light.

The Xuanhuang Army within the Eternal Immortal Fortress watched Li Fan's back with admiration.

Many intelligent individuals even recorded the images of Li Fan's sword light annihilating the demonic sounds.

They repeatedly studied them.

Indeed, some gained insights and significantly improved their strength.

As the agreed time arrived, the Saint Fetus Li Fan, without any hesitation.

Amidst the gaze of all, he stood up and walked towards the depths of the Chizha Abyss.

He showed no intention of waiting for Shang Shaojun.

And seeing Li Fan about to enter the abyss alone, inevitable whispers arose within the Eternal Immortal Fortress.

After all, no matter how high Shang Shaojun's prestige was before, if he showed no reaction on this matter, his image would irrevocably crumble.

These Xuanhuang Army soldiers were all his loyal subordinates cultivated over decades. If he lost their genuine support, it would undoubtedly be a devastating loss for Shang Shaojun.

Moreover, with Shang Shaojun's strength, even if he ventured deep into the Chizha Abyss and failed to suppress the demonic sounds, he would at most be injured, not lose his life.

Therefore, Li Fan was certain that Shang Shaojun would appear.

Even if he just followed behind him, merely going through the motions.

As expected, just as Li Fan fearlessly stepped into the Chizha Abyss, Shang Shaojun's figure reappeared at the right moment.

"Farewell, Commander!"

The Xuanhuang Army soldiers shouted in unison with thunderous voices, disappearing abruptly after Li Fan had completely entered the abyss.

"The last time I stepped foot here was nearly three hundred years ago," Shang Shaojun's voice echoed from behind.

Li Fan did not respond, only observing his surroundings.

It bore some resemblance to the Netherworld.

Endless darkness, causing one's heart to palpitate. The difference was that within the darkness, there were continuous dark red light bands, like the flowing blood of some ancient monstrous beast.

From these blood-colored light bands, substances resembling ashes occasionally drifted out.

Li Fan reached out and caught a piece. A rotten aura immediately began to erode his entire body from the point of contact.

In just a few breaths, the Saint Fetus Li Fan's body transformed into the same ashen substance.

A sword light cut through the darkness, and Li Fan was reborn from his inner world.

"These remnants are the result of the twisted path of world destruction contaminating it. This is merely the outermost layer of the abyss. The deeper one goes, the more twisted the degree becomes. It can even contaminate and destroy our fundamental cultivation foundations," Shang Shaojun transmitted mentally, warning him.

The cultivation foundations he spoke of referred to Foundation Establishment treasures, Nascent Soul grotto-heavens, and so on.

As long as these new dharma foundations were not destroyed, cultivators could be reborn continuously. However, if even they were damaged, cultivators would naturally perish.
