"Besides that, we also need to worry about sudden demonic sound tides. The demonic sounds outside the abyss are completely different from those within. In my past experience, though I prided myself on my steadfast will, I couldn't last a few breaths before nearly being driven mad by those terrifying whispers."

...

Shang Shaojun chattered on, but Li Fan ignored him, flying steadfastly towards the bottom of the abyss.

Wherever he passed, sword lights flashed, and the continuous, wandering dark red blood shadows were all annihilated.

Shang Shaojun watched for a while and discovered that those strange objects did not show signs of regeneration, and he was secretly surprised.

"This is the [Sword of Annihilation]. Wherever its sword light reaches, it turns into nothingness."

Li Fan's voice suddenly sounded in his ear.

"As for the 'festering wound,' one only needs to cut it clean." he said lightly.

"As for those demonic sounds..."

"I have an supreme secret art. I will impart it to you, and it will ensure your safety."

Chapter 1150: Yellow Rebirth Technique

Xuanhuang Rebirth Technique

"Supreme Secret Art?"

When Shang Shaojun heard these four words, he was somewhat dismissive.

After all, given his status and standing, he had even entered treasures left behind by the Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate.

Even within that treasure trove, there was no divine ability or secret art that dared to call itself "Supreme."

"Although his strength is formidable, his foundation is ultimately too shallow."

Shang Shaojun mused inwardly.

But as he read the first two or three sentences of the text transmitted by the other party, his expression changed drastically, and he immediately became solemn.

By the time he had read more than half of the text, his mind was thunderous, and he was completely stunned.

"Though subjected to myriad tribulations, the heart remains unchanged. This..."

Although he didn't know the name of this secret art, there was no doubt that it was a true profound technique that surpassed all the dharma he currently knew.

It truly deserved the title "Supreme"!

What shocked Shang Shaojun even more was that such a secret art, which would undoubtedly cause countless bloody battles in the Xuanhuang Realm, was so easily given to him!

It was as if it were a Foundation Establishment technique obtainable at will!

"Who exactly..."

Shang Shaojun suddenly looked up at Li Fan, who was diligently clearing the abyss's festering wounds, his heart filled with shock.

But Li Fan had no intention of explaining his identity, so Shang Shaojun did not dare to demand.

He could only honestly follow behind, while secretly practicing the supreme secret art.

This art was calm, peaceful, and filled with righteousness.

There was no need to worry about any traps hidden within.

And Shang Shaojun quickly experienced its power firsthand.

In the dark abyss, countless dark red "blood vessels" suddenly lit up.

Like continuous mountain fires, the light flickered uncertainly.

With the appearance of these blood-colored lights, the abyss seemed to contract violently.

Space was compressed, and incomprehensible sounds of destruction from before the ancient times, like the cries of ten thousand demons and the groans of the dying, spread from the blood-red lights that suddenly extinguished.

Visions surged into Shang Shaojun's mind.

He seemed to see one world after another being destroyed.

Cultivators cried out in despair.

Even heaven and earth themselves had reached their end.

Countless black rifts on the sky tore the heavens apart.

The earth cracked open, and red magma erupted from the abyss.

Countless fireballs rained down, creating towering infernos.

A serene blue wind blew, freezing all things in the world.

...

Scenes of apocalypse unfolded one after another in Shang Shaojun's mind.

Even though he considered himself a proud genius, facing such a terrifying, immersive scene, his body trembled, and his heart was filled with great fear.

However, unlike before...

As the supreme secret art automatically circulated, an extremely chilling aura instantly spread throughout his body.

Shang Shaojun then broke free from the boundless fear.

Although the apocalyptic illusions were still vivid, Shang Shaojun's mind was pure.

Without worry, without fear.

Like a passerby, he observed with cold detachment.

"Though subjected to myriad tribulations, the heart remains unextinguished."

"This, this is truly a supreme divine art..."

Shang Shaojun's current state of mind was somewhat strange.

Under the blessing of the cultivation technique, it was clearly a great cause for joy, yet he remained completely unfazed.

And his suspicion towards Li Fan, who had bestowed such a divine art upon him, deepened.

"It's hard to find even a few places in the Xuanhuang Realm that possess secret arts of this caliber."

"He's not from our Myriad Immortals Alliance, nor the Five Elders Society. Could he be from another perished immortal cultivation world?"

Shang Shaojun knew that there were refugees from other worlds in the Xuanhuang Realm. However, these people often hid very deeply, and even the Myriad Immortals Alliance didn't know everything about them.

"What is his true purpose for coming to the Chizha Abyss?"

While helping Li Fan suppress and eliminate the demonic sounds, Shang Shaojun pondered.

The demonic sounds in the Chizha Abyss did not erupt continuously.

After surviving one demonic sound tide, the inside of the abyss returned to silence.

And Li Fan and Shang Shaojun discovered some remnants of the demonic sound tide in the darkness.

They were somewhat similar to the ash-like substances from before, but they lacked that evil, twisted corrosive aura.

"Does young lord know what these are?" Li Fan suddenly asked.

Shang Shaojun observed for a while and shook his head slightly.

"These are remnants from the intermingling of different worlds."

"Previously, young lord mentioned that the demonic sounds of the abyss were the twisted path of a destroyed world. In fact, that's not entirely accurate."

"The Xuanhuang Realm is a complete, grand, and prosperous immortal cultivation realm. How could it be easily eroded by other destroyed immortal cultivation worlds? Even if there were the destructive paths of other worlds, they wouldn't manifest as demonic sounds on such a scale."

"The key is here, in this wound of the Xuanhuang Realm, where the destructive world's path connects with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao."

Li Fan explained to Shang Shaojun while observing the depths of the Chizha Abyss.

"The laws of the destroyed world have been transformed into the laws of the Xuanhuang Realm itself."

"It's like drawing out blood from one person and transferring it to another. Here, two different Heavenly Daos collide. The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao naturally emerges victorious, but..."

Li Fan suddenly fell silent.

He left half a sentence unspoken.

"The essence of the Heavenly Dao itself has also been subtly altered in this process."

"Is this the Heavenly Doctor's doing?"

"Dissecting world fragments, grafting and stitching. Transmitting the old world's Heavenly Dao, subtly changing the nature of the Heavenly Dao, so that the side effects of integration are minimized..."

Li Fan seemed to see countless existences like the 'Chizha Abyss' hidden deep within the white mist barriers throughout the Xuanhuang Realm.

Under their collective modifications, the Xuanhuang Realm was undergoing transformation, bit by bit, silently.

"A grand and precise surgery."

Li Fan couldn't help but sigh inwardly.

If not for the "Record of Mending the Heavens" gifted by the Heavenly Doctor, even if Li Fan cultivated to the Longevity realm, he probably wouldn't have had the ability to detect these events happening to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Just like Shang Shaojun now, even with Li Fan's guidance, he still couldn't quite grasp the hidden truth.

"In this lifetime, if I want to test them, I cannot be hesitant."

"Since I've come here, let's destroy one place first and see how they react."

Li Fan's eyes flickered.

Behind him, myriad sword shadows appeared, and he suddenly accelerated, charging towards the depths of the abyss.

Shang Shaojun, who was still in a daze, quickly followed.

The deeper they went, the less intertwined the laws of different worlds became.

The collision of Heavenly Daos, even between destroyed worlds, was not something ordinary cultivators could withstand.

Frenzied fluctuations swept through the darkness like a storm.

Shang Shaojun, at the Dao Integration stage, even felt that the Heaven and Earth Core he had refined was in danger of being decomposed.

"Even a Dao Integration cultivator here is like a small boat in the rain, a candle in the wind, unable to control themselves."

Shang Shaojun looked at Li Fan again, filled with confusion.

Clearly, the other party's cultivation realm was lower than his, yet he remained so composed amidst the fluctuations caused by the collision of different world laws.

"What is his cultivation realm?"

Chapter 1151: Destroying Worlds Leads to the True Culprit

Destroying Worlds Attracts the True Culprit

"Could it be..."

"Longevity?"

The thought of Shang Shaojun's mind couldn't help but arise.

As far as he knew, among the refugees from other immortal cultivation worlds, there were also some existences at the Longevity Realm.

Although they were not as peerless as the Heavenly Venerates of the Xuanhuang Realm, they were certainly not someone an ordinary Dao Integration cultivator could deal with.

"It should be so," Shang Shaojun's heart tightened, and his attitude towards Li Fan became even more cautious.

The two continued to delve deeper into the Chizha Abyss. As the intermingling of different world laws reached its peak,

new anomalies began to appear in the darkness.

Faint blood-red light illuminated the path ahead.

Fragments of shattered continents floated and hung suspended above their heads.

From afar, one could vaguely see ruins densely covering the land, and countless white bones scattered among the ruins.

All the floating world fragments were deathly silent.

Thick, root-like red threads grew from these fragmented continents, extending into the Chizha Abyss and hidden in the darkness.

Horrifying sounds sporadically echoed through the space.

Like metal blades scraping across bone surfaces, or like the heavy breathing of someone on the verge of death.

The eerie atmosphere made Li Fan and Shang Shaojun, who had come to explore the secrets, instinctively halt their steps.

Seeing Li Fan meticulously observing the strange scene ahead, Shang Shaojun, after pondering for a moment, transmitted his observation: "These fragmented worlds seem to be still alive?" he said uncertainly.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan did not reply.

He simply sent out a sword light, which flew straight towards one of the shattered worlds.

Seeing this, Shang Shaojun's heart tightened, and he immediately became vigilant.

Although he had witnessed the extraordinary nature of Li Fan's swordsmanship, the backlash of a world, even a dying one, was not to be underestimated.

The silver-white sword light instantly traversed space and arrived above the shattered continent.

To Shang Shaojun's surprise, the sword strike Li Fan unleashed did not seem intended for destruction.

After piercing the barrier and descending, it remained in a state of stasis.

The trace left in the air by its arrival had not faded.

The sword light condensed, seemingly forming a silver thread.

It connected Li Fan to the shattered world.

Li Fan floated and stood on the silver thread, closing his eyes as if sensing something.

"This is..."

Shang Shaojun was initially bewildered by Li Fan's actions.

But as he watched, for some reason, he recalled the scene of a mortal physician taking a pulse and diagnosing an illness.

"Using the sword as a guide, probing life and death."

"Could it be that this person is not only unparalleled in swordsmanship but also possesses profound attainments in the way of [Medicine]?"

Shang Shaojun's heart trembled.

And Li Fan's subsequent actions made his heart skip a beat.

Li Fan lightly stomped on the silver thread, and a ripple of energy spread along the thread into the shattered world.

Initially, it was an insignificant tremor.

Then, as if resonating with something, the tremor grew more intense. The earth, which had been deathly silent, suddenly awakened.

Rumbling sounds came from underground, and lava erupted along with the world's roar, spewing forth violently.

...

At this moment, Li Fan flicked his finger lightly, severing the sword light beneath his feet.

Then he retreated rapidly towards the rear.

"Move further away."

Before Li Fan's voice even fell, Shang Shaojun felt a powerful force strike him, sending him tumbling backward uncontrollably.

His internal energy surged, and he had clearly sustained minor injuries.

Shang Shaojun looked back in horror and discovered that the world Li Fan had "diagnosed" had already met its end in a violent self-collision.

Being mere fragments, the world was inherently fragile.

It could not withstand such intense energy fluctuations from its own core.

The earth completely disintegrated, transforming into endless crimson flames.

As it emitted its final radiance in the darkness, it also signified the demise of a world.

Shang Shaojun looked at this scene and couldn't help but fall into a daze.

Li Fan stood beside him and explained, "If we were to destroy this world using external force, it would not only provoke backlash from the world itself but might also alert the hidden existence behind all this."

"But if we were to forcibly stimulate the world's remaining strength, causing it to perish naturally..."

As Li Fan spoke, a thousand sword shadows reappeared behind him.

The sword lights intertwined, flashed brilliantly, and then merged into the air.

"Enter the formation."

Hearing Li Fan's transmission, Shang Shaojun's heart skipped another beat.

However, he was already numb from shock and instinctively followed.

Upon entering the formation space, Shang Shaojun saw sword shadows rapidly circling and flying around him.

The thousand swords flew in unison, carving out a concealed hiding place.

Before hiding in this sword formation, Shang Shaojun had seen Li Fan replicate the process, destroying several adjacent shattered worlds in quick succession.

The terrifying impact released during the destruction of these worlds turned the deepest part of the Chizha Abyss into a true inferno.

Innumerable dark red ashes, carried by the violent energy, surged outwards from the abyss.

Like a night parade of ten thousand ghosts, or a stampede of beasts.

The Thousand Sword Formation seemed to be straining.

It continuously contracted.

The myriad rotating sword lights spun faster and faster, almost forming concentric circles.

But Li Fan showed no concern about the formation failing.

He stood with his eyes closed, doing something unknown.

"Wait."

Sensing Shang Shaojun's confusion, Li Fan transmitted a simple message and then fell silent.

Shang Shaojun took a deep breath, and with the reinforcement of the chilling aura, his mind quickly calmed.

The surrounding sword lights flew about, not only isolating the external scenery but also blocking his divine sense, preventing him from seeing what was happening outside.

However, judging from the muffled thuds of the sword formation being impacted by massive objects, the destruction of several world fragments had undoubtedly caused an extremely terrifying impact on the outside world.

"If this gentleman wasn't here, I would have had to retreat in a sorry state from this impact alone."

"Swordsmanship, medicine, formations... Is there really someone in this world who is proficient in all these arts?"

Shang Shaojun's thoughts churned. Even with the acceleration provided by the Immortal Heart Incantation, he could not completely suppress his speculation about Li Fan's identity.

After an unknown period.

The storm outside the sword formation finally subsided.

But Li Fan still showed no intention of dispelling the sword formation.

And judging by his increasingly serious expression, there seemed to be some other existence outside, even more terrifying than the destruction of worlds.

"The mastermind behind the scenes?"

The thought flashed through Shang Shaojun's mind as he recalled the horrifying scene of countless world fragments suspended above his head.

This clearly could not have formed naturally.

The moment he thought of a powerful being who could treat worlds like playthings, possibly appearing nearby, Shang Shaojun couldn't help but feel his scalp tingle.

"I wonder if this sword formation can hide us?"

"If He discovers us, it will surely be a dead end!"

Chapter 1152: Reshaping the World with One Hand

With a Single Hand, the World is Reshaped

Although Shang Shaojun was a commander of the Xuanhuang Army, he had never directly confronted an existence at the Longevity Realm.

During the anxious wait, time seemed to drag on, making each moment feel like an eternity.

After an unknown period, the constantly rotating sword lights around them finally stopped.

Li Fan, who had been waiting with his eyes closed, finally opened them.

As the sword lights dispersed, Shang Shaojun subconsciously looked around.

And the scene he beheld made him feel as if he had fallen into an abyss of ice and chilling cold, his entire body turning icy.

Moments ago, the several shattered worlds that Li Fan had stimulated into destruction with his sword light had inexplicably reappeared!

They hung suspended above their heads, and sinister red threads intertwined, becoming even thicker.

Densely packed, they extended towards the Chizha Abyss.

"Not only did they not disappear, they even..." Shang Shaojun's heart chilled, and he looked at Li Fan.

He even began to doubt whether the scene of world destruction he had witnessed earlier was merely an illusion.

"He has been here."

Li Fan said in a deep voice.

"Who is he?" Shang Shaojun couldn't help but ask.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan shook his head.

"However, it's obvious."

Li Fan snapped his fingers and pointed towards the space ahead.

The thousand sword lights that formed the sword formation reappeared before the two of them.

Then they began to rotate rapidly.

As the speed of the sword lights increased, blurry images began to appear on the light screen formed by the sword lights!

"One who can accomplish all this must be an extremely powerful being. If we had secretly spied just now, even with my supreme formation concealing us, even with the impact of world destruction as a natural cover..."

"We would likely still have been detected by Him."

It was only now that Li Fan explained the reason for using the formation to shield Shang Shaojun's probing gaze.

Shang Shaojun's heart tightened, but he heard Li Fan continue: "Even I used these sword lights to record the information, not concentrating it in one place. Each sword light only records the information of a single fragmented piece. Only by combining them completely can the original scene be recorded."

"This way, the possibility of us being discovered is minimized."

As Li Fan whispered, the images on the sword screen shifted.

Shattered world fragments, destructive waves spewing outwards, ravaging the surroundings.

Just as this violent scene was slowly subsiding,

a figure suddenly appeared in the center of the storm.

The sword light recording did not capture the figure's appearance.

Or perhaps, he had not revealed his true form?

Shang Shaojun only knew that the moment this true culprit appeared, the originally frenzied energy fluctuations instantly calmed down.

The figure observed for a moment, seeming somewhat puzzled.

Then, he swept his gaze towards the direction of the Chizha Abyss.

Even though it was a simple recording, even though the figure's appearance was unclear, and even though they were separated by different spaces and times,

Shang Shaojun felt as if his body and even his soul were about to freeze from that single glance.

His entire body stiffened, unable to think.

Fortunately, the figure only glanced briefly and did not delve deeper.

Then, he withdrew his gaze.

Shang Shaojun felt as if he had gone through a great battle, his body exhausted, panting heavily.

But he still stared intently at the constantly shifting, rotating sword screen.

The figure pressed his hands forward in the space before him, and the storm in this area instantly ceased.

With a wave of his hand, the residual world embers were collected.

Then...

The figure seemed to ponder with gravity, carefully retrieving an equal number of world fragments from an unknown location!

Like a giant from ancient myth, creating the world.

He then inverted these shattered worlds at the bottom of the Chizha Abyss.

And with a light touch of his finger, strange red threads flew out from these fractured worlds,

like sentient beings, flying towards the Xuanhuang Realm.

A roar echoed from within the Chizha Abyss.

This was the sign of two worlds merging.

After completing all this and ensuring the inverted worlds were stable, the figure finally departed.

...

The scene abruptly ended.

When Li Fan gathered the thousand sword lights, Shang Shaojun was still immersed in the incredible scenes he had just witnessed.

"The Xuanhuang Realm actually hides such a figure?"

"The immortals in legends, who could pluck stars and seize the moon, would be no more than this, right?"

Recalling the scene where the figure retrieved and gently held up the world fragments, Shang Shaojun couldn't help but tremble slightly.

But Li Fan's answer suddenly pulled him out of his endless fear.

"Though this person is strong, he is still inferior to a true immortal."

His tone was casual, as if he had personally met an immortal.

"Now it seems my guess was correct. The Xuanhuang Realm's bizarre state is undoubtedly due to someone plotting in secret."

Without waiting for Shang Shaojun to reply, Li Fan continued.

"This figure we saw is one of them."

"Young lord, what do you plan to do?"

Shang Shaojun was suddenly stunned.

What to do?

The strength of that unknown, terrifying existence was definitely at the Longevity Realm, or even above.

What could he, a mere Dao Integration cultivator, possibly do?

"I must immediately return to the Immortal Alliance headquarters and report this matter."

Shang Shaojun said righteously.

Li Fan gave him a knowing smile: "Are you sure?"

"If you are truly insistent..."

"Then today will likely be the last time we see each other," Li Fan said in a low voice.

Shang Shaojun's expression changed: "What do you mean?"

"The Chizha Abyss clearly hides secrets. Many years ago, discerning individuals within the Immortal Alliance voluntarily organized an investigation, but it was rejected by the Immortal Alliance..."

"Does young lord still not understand? On the Myriad Immortals Alliance's territory, how could such a large-scale operation be concealed from them?"

Li Fan said calmly.

In fact, Shang Shaojun understood this logic.

But his heart had always refused to acknowledge this outcome.

Now, with Li Fan ruthlessly exposing it, Shang Shaojun's expression shifted rapidly.

He understood that if the Myriad Immortals Alliance was involved, or even leading this,

then the implications behind it...

Even though he had witnessed countless conspiracies and struggles, Shang Shaojun felt a deep sense of powerlessness at this moment.

"Young lord need not despair."

"This matter clearly exceeds the scope of what you and I can handle. Polluting the Xuanhuang Realm by using the chaotic Heavenly Dao of destroyed worlds is an act that makes one an enemy of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Although the Myriad Immortals Alliance may have high-ranking officials involved, I doubt they can cover everything up."

"The Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate is traveling the heavens, indifferent to worldly affairs. But I heard that there are special methods to summon him back..."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan gradually guided him.

Shang Shaojun's eyes lit up upon hearing this: "Indeed. The situation is so dire and dangerous that perhaps only by summoning the Dharma Transmission back can it be resolved. However, only..."

Shang Shaojun frowned slightly.

Li Fan recalled the scene he had just witnessed.

"Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate..."

Chapter 1153: Immortal Heart Falls to the Mortal World

The Immortal Heart Descends to the Mortal World

It wasn't that Li Fan intentionally concealed the figure's appearance.

The mysterious figure appearing at the bottom of the Chizha Abyss was too powerful. The abyss's inherently unstable environment couldn't accommodate an existence of such a realm.

This resulted in a blurry image when viewed from the outside.

However, judging by the aura the figure inadvertently exuded, Li Fan had more than a fifty percent chance of confirming that it was the Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate.

"But he seems younger than the weathered old man I remember. What's going on?"

Saint Fetus Li Fan fell into deep thought.

Meanwhile, Shang Shaojun snapped out of his thoughts and transmitted, "I know a way to invite the Heavenly Venerate back, but a vague, unclear image..."

"Is not enough. We need more evidence."

"Furthermore, it's impossible for us to directly present this collected evidence to him ourselves. Convincing him will be exceedingly difficult."

Li Fan, detecting Shang Shaojun's apprehension, responded with a smile, "Young Lord, there's no need for excessive pessimism. While the two of us are indeed weak and isolated, surely in the vast Xuanhuang Realm, we can find like-minded individuals."

"We can gather evidence while also seeking trustworthy people and strengthening ourselves," Li Fan said, already intending to bring Shang Shaojun along.

"But the Chizha Abyss..." Shang Shaojun still hesitated.

Li Fan immediately adopted a serious expression and advised, "If the skin is gone, where will the hair attach? If the entire Xuanhuang Realm falls into crisis, even if Young Lord suppresses this abyss and ensures your own safety, what would be the use?"

"Moreover, I've already devised a perfect method for suppressing the abyss's demonic sounds even if Young Lord travels far away."

As they spoke, they had already returned to the entrance of the abyss.

Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and a colossal sword seemingly composed of tens of thousands of different sword lights instantly spanned the abyss.

Pointing a finger into the air, the giant sword agilely maneuvered with Li Fan's movements.

Correspondingly, strands of dark red silk-like threads were sliced off.

Deprived of the original world's rules, these threads should have scattered chaotically and then annihilated.

But with Li Fan's sweeping gestures in the air, they slowly gathered together.

Quietly, they wove into a giant red net!

Shang Shaojun's heart trembled slightly again upon witnessing this.

Although not as shocking as the mysterious figure effortlessly manipulating ruined worlds, this effortless weaving of fragmented world laws into a net demonstrated that Li Fan's Daoist attainments far surpassed ordinary individuals.

"The reason the demonic sound tide is difficult to guard against is that the conflict between the fragmented world's rules and the Xuanhuang Realm's laws is too intense and focused in this narrow zone, with no buffer. So, I've slightly altered the spatial structure here to maximally delay the time for law integration..."

"Actually, that mysterious figure could have easily done this, concealing any traces to avoid detection. But he didn't. Perhaps that's also a form of confidence," Li Fan shook his head slightly.

"With the buffer of this rule net, the power of the demonic sound tide outbreak is estimated to be halved."

As Li Fan spoke, he gently clenched his hand, transforming the giant sword in the abyss back into myriad sword lights.

Innumerable sword shadows, following a specific pattern, soared like dragons, subtly forming a grand formation.

Shang Shaojun observed the sword formation swirling around the outer perimeter of the rule net, with a massive vortex forming at its center.

The dark red remnants overflowing from the rule net were occasionally drawn into the sword formation.

"This formation, with its sword intent that destroys all, will shatter the accumulated fragmented laws within the Chizha Abyss. It can extend the period of the demonic sound tide outbreak by more than two times."

"Young Lord can order the sword cultivators in the Azure Profound Army to come here. Not only can they comprehend the sword intent condensed within the formation, but they can also help charge the sword formation..." Li Fan calmly presented a solution to the demonic sound tide that the Azure Profound Army dreaded.

Shang Shaojun gazed at the formation and the net, speechless.

He had been called a genius since childhood.

But before Li Fan...

"Indeed, there's always someone better. I was ignorant before."

With his worries addressed, Shang Shaojun naturally had no reason to refuse Li Fan's invitation to journey together.

The two returned to the Eternal Immortal Fortress and announced the temporary suppression of the demonic sound tide, eliciting thunderous cheers from the Azure Profound Army.

Shang Shaojun then convened his trusted subordinates and passed down the manipulation method for the formation, which Li Fan had named the "Annihilation Sound Sword Formation."

With all matters settled and no longer a hindrance, Shang Shaojun summoned Yan Huan for a private meeting before their departure.

"Young Lord, please rest assured. The techniques deduced by Yanfajue are very effective. Those brothers who occasionally lost their minds have rarely acted out recently," Yan Huan replied respectfully, bowing his head.

...

Li Fan learned during their conversation the reason Yan Huan had hastily sought out Yanfajue, even expending a precious law-seeking jade token, to deduce cultivation techniques.

The Azure Profound Army had long guarded the Chizha Abyss, and due to the subtle influence of the demonic sounds, some individuals would become mentally unstable, even acting madly towards their comrades.

In the past, when the number of affected individuals was small, it was relatively easy to handle.

But with the passage of time, nearly one-fifth of the Azure Profound Army in Broken Palm Immortal City had contracted this strange affliction.

Shortly before Saint Fetus Li Fan arrived, there was a large-scale outbreak within the Azure Profound Army, resulting in heavy casualties.

Crucially, the deaths were not from the demonic sound tide but from friendly fire, which was especially difficult to accept.

The morale of the Azure Profuasion Army was low, and their ranks were fragmented.

Shang Shaojun, with no other recourse, had used his hard-earned law-seeking jade token to ask Yanfajue for a solution.

"'Heart Forging Against Demons Art,' cultivators of this technique can help others firm their Dao hearts and dispel evil thoughts from their minds. Although it can only resolve one person's worries at a time, it is indeed effective. The recovered soldiers have even developed some resistance to the demonic sounds," Shang Shaojun explained to Li Fan.

"How does this 'Heart Forging Against Demons Art' compare to the supreme secret art I transmitted to you, Young Lord?" Li Fan inquired.

Shang Shaojun was slightly taken aback, then blurted out, "Naturally, it's far inferior!"

"In that case, Young Lord, why not pass down the 'Immortal Heart Incantation' as well? Lest everyone suffer the torment of demonic sounds," Li Fan said with a look of compassion.

Upon hearing this, Shang Shaojun's eyes widened, and his heart trembled violently.

"Immortal Heart Incantation..."

He finally learned the name of that supreme secret art. The words "Immortal Heart" immediately sparked endless associations in his mind.

While astonished by Li Fan's generosity, Shang Shaojun felt a pang of reluctance at the thought of imparting such a supreme art to everyone unconditionally.

Chapter 1154: Rebuilding Foundation Changes

Reshaping the Foundation of the False Path

"Is doing so not a bit of a waste of heavenly resources?"

Shang Shaojun secretly transmitted his question to Li Fan in the presence of his confidant Yan Huan.

Then, seeing Li Fan's half-smile, he felt his own words were somewhat inappropriate.

He cleared his throat slightly to cover his awkwardness.

"The name 'Immortal Heart Incantation' is too ostentatious. Young Lord could rename it to something ordinary and then impart it," Li Fan suggested.

Shang Shaojun, recalling the cultivation technique deduced by Yanfajue earlier, said to Yan Huan, "This is the 'Heart Forging Technique.' It was transmitted by this senior. It can protect you from the erosion of demonic sounds. You must disseminate it quickly to the entire army and ensure everyone learns it."

The name "Heart Forging Technique" was too common, so after hearing Shang Shaojun's words, Yan Huan did not show much surprise. He merely bowed and accepted the order, immediately attempting to cultivate it.

"To have such a secret art by their side, yet they are unaware... truly..."

Watching Yan Huan's departing back, Shang Shaojun couldn't help but sigh.

"If they knew the preciousness of this secret art, they might instead become anxious and unable to learn it," Li Fan remarked.

"With the millions of soldiers in the Azure Profound Army, although I have strictly forbidden its external transmission, it's likely inevitable that the 'Immortal Heart Incantation' will be leaked. Aren't you worried, Daoist friend?" Shang Shaojun asked Li Fan, full of confusion.

He couldn't fathom Li Fan's actions since arriving at the Eternal Immortal Fortress.

It wasn't for fame, nor for profit.

"Xuanhuang cultivators cherish their own techniques. Although it's influenced by the prohibition of simultaneous cultivation, cultivators' internal perceptions have unconsciously changed."

"In the ancient immortal cultivation era, the grand occasion of discussing the Dao and sharing knowledge is no longer seen."

"I dislike this greatly."

Saint Fetus Li Fan said indifferently.

Coupled with his actions towards outsiders, he truly exuded an otherworldly, transcendent air.

"Let it be spread. As long as it aligns with my will, what does it matter if it's an immortal technique?"

Shang Shaojun gazed at Li Fan's figure, somewhat lost in thought.

Such magnanimity was indeed rare in the world.

Being with such a person, Shang Shaojun even felt his own spirits soar.

...

With all affairs at the Eternal Immortal Fortress concluded and no further concerns, Shang Shaojun and Li Fan stood outside the fortress, gazing at the vast white mist.

"Where shall we go next?"

Having inexplicably taken on the burden of "saving the Xuanhuang Realm," Shang Shaojun felt somewhat lost as they truly prepared to set off.

However, given the circumstances, he couldn't regret it.

Shang Shaojun glanced at Li Fan beside him, fully confident that if he were to renege now, the other party would surely draw his sword.

"The safety of Xuanhuang rests entirely on us. This feeling..."

"'It's not bad,' Shang Shaojun mused inwardly."

Li Fan, however, extended his hand, and a small sword no larger than his palm instantly appeared in his palm.

It rotated, seemingly sensing something.

Finally, its tip pointed in a direction and stopped.

Shang Shaojun followed the direction indicated by the small sword.

"All existence leaves traces. Although that mysterious figure is incomparably powerful, as long as they appear in the Xuanhuang Realm, they are bound to interact with reality. By tracking him, we can find more evidence," Li Fan said, his gaze intense.

Shang Shaojun felt Li Fan's reasoning made sense and promptly nodded in agreement.

He was unaware that the direction indicated by Li Fan's small sword was not for tracking the mysterious figure.

Instead, it pointed towards various mystery zones that Li Fan had previously explored and mapped in his memories.

Of course, all paths lead to Rome. They were bound to find ample evidence of the Xuanhuang Realm being reshaped there.

...

Just as Saint Fetus Li Fan was guiding Shang Shaojun to uncover the hidden truth of the Xuanhuang Realm, in the Great Qi small world, Yin Shangren's experimental base had been preliminarily established.

"When I last saw Mr. Bai, he told me that after my Foundation Establishment method, I might be able to achieve the 'Primordial Golden Core,' 'Mortal Body Nascent Soul,' or 'Mind Manifestation of Divinity.' Sir, please refer to these concepts for your deductions," Clone Li Ping said to Yin Shangren.

Yin Shangren had just performed a bizarre act in front of Li Ping.

His body split open, and another him struggled to crawl out from within.

Then, turning around, he proceeded to devour his own flesh and bones.

The sound of flesh and bone being chewed echoed throughout the experimental base, Yin Shangren's face covered in blood.

Yet, his expression was calm, as if he were engaged in research rather than eating.

Even Li Ping, with his myriad past memories, felt a chill down his spine watching Yin Shangren, not due to courage, but because it went against human nature.

After slowly chewing and fully consuming the other him, Li Ping noticed that Yin Shangren's visible cultivation realm had dropped from Foundation Establishment to Qi Refining.

Only then did Yin Shangren wipe his blood-stained hands on his clothes and explain, "To deduce the subsequent methods, one must first walk the correct path."

"My Foundation Establishment method was only half successful, so I had to destroy the foundation and start anew."

He looked up at the sky, "It might be troublesome, but I can handle it."

As Yin Shangren spoke, Li Ping instantly felt something descend upon the Holy Capital.

Cultivating the Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex, integrating the luck of the entire dynasty into one, Li Ping, at this moment, represented the Great Qi Dynasty alone.

Any external intrusion would naturally escape his detection.

It was like cold worms crawling on the surface of his skin, testing and then extending sharp spikes, attempting to penetrate the Great Qi small world.

"Hmm? This place seems self-contained. Perhaps their retaliation will be weaker than expected," Yin Shangren said.

Li Ping knew that Yin Shangren was referring to the remnant souls of the old world.

It was likely that Yin Shangren's forceful destruction and alteration of his own state had attracted the attention of his kin.

The sound of dripping rain began.

But there were no raindrops.

Dark, heavy clouds appeared above Li Ping's head,

covering the experimental base.

The hard Xuanwu Stone ground beneath them turned muddy with the dripping sound.

Pale arms suddenly emerged from the ground,

Li Ping frowned slightly, attempting to float away to avoid them.

But in this distorted and altered strange space, he unexpectedly lost the ability to fly.

Fortunately, these world specters were not targeting him.

The arms crawling on the ground, like phantoms, swarmed towards Yin Shangren.

Yin Shangren, however, revealed a sinister smile.

He grabbed the nearest arm and forcibly pulled it out, stuffing it into his mouth and devouring it.

Chapter 1155: Burying the Past, Opening a New Path

Burying the Old, Ushering in the New Path

Clone Li Ping clearly saw that the arms being torn apart by Yin Shangren's teeth did not bleed.

Instead, black pus flowed out.

Within the pus, countless painful faces, resembling tiny tentacles, emitted sharp, piercing wails. Yet, Yin Shangren remained unfazed, swallowing them directly.

*Pfft...*

Yin Shangren's skin seemed to be sliced open by sharp knives, and the tentacles he swallowed re-emerged from his body.

But this time, all the faces had transformed into Yin Shangren's likeness!

Li Ping hid in a corner of this mutated space, quietly observing the changes.

On the surface, it appeared as though Yin Shangren was madly cannibalizing,

but in reality, it was the collision and intermingling of laws from different fragmented worlds.

However, unlike the law integration process in the Chizha Abyss, the abyss's laws were carefully selected parts intended for integration into the Xuanhuang Realm.

Here, however...

It was chaos, disorder, and destruction.

It was like being thrown into a garbage dump, engaging in frantic self-cannibalization for a sliver of a chance at survival.

The conflict between the world specters did not last long.

Perhaps because this world was not part of the Xuanhuang Realm, or perhaps due to the protection of the Great Qi Holy Dynasty's fortune, the specters that descended were much weaker than Yin Shangren.

After swallowing all the limbs on the ground,

the cracked surface of his body slowly began to heal.

"It's been so long since I've enjoyed such a delicacy. I truly miss it,"

Yin Shangren's voice returned to normal, no longer strange and dual.

However, the aura he unconsciously exuded made Li Ping, who had already reached the peak of Deity Transformation, feel as if his back was crawling with cold dread.

Yin Shangren, however, harbored no ill intentions. After resolving the specter threat, he directly began cultivating his "My Foundation Establishment" technique.

Li Ping narrowed his eyes. From his perspective, the law fluctuations around Yin Shangren were rapidly diminishing.

They weren't disappearing mysteriously but were slowly being absorbed into Yin Shangren's body.

Yin Shangren's form, like a plume of smoke, shifted unstably. Faces, originally absorbed by him, reappeared on his skin.

Horror constantly flickered, struggling to break free from his body.

It appeared as if hundreds of bulging tumors, on the verge of bursting, had simultaneously protruded from Yin Shangren's body, a terrifying sight.

But Yin Shangren remained steadfast.

He sat quietly, without the slightest hint of panic.

Slowly, the faces seemed to be pulled by some force, returning into his body.

One by one, the tumors disappeared, and Yin Shangren's appearance gradually normalized.

When Li Ping sensed that the overflowing law aura had completely vanished, Yin Shangren abruptly opened his eyes.

His gaze, unlike the previous madness and obsession, was now like a deep, clear pool, tranquil and serene.

"My Foundation Establishment." He looked at his hands, lost in thought.

"How does it feel?" Li Fan asked.

Yin Shangren did not answer but directly pointed a finger at Li Ping.

*Boom!*

Nine golden dragons suddenly materialized, roaring protectively around Li Ping.

Beneath Li Ping's feet, a muddy pool had inexplicably appeared.

Li Ping himself was silently being swallowed by the pool.

And in Li Ping's perception, the overall fortune of the Great Qi Holy Dynasty was like a small hole had been pierced, constantly leaking away.

Although the rate of fortune loss was slow, he couldn't find a way to plug it for the moment.

Golden dragons circled, emitting protective light, shielding Li Ping above the muddy pool.

He did not counterattack but instead praised, "Sir has excellent means."

Yin Shangren waved his hand, and the muddy pool beneath Li Ping instantly vanished. "This is the most malevolent curse and resentment when a world is on the verge of death."

"In the past, to manifest such curses, I myself would have been significantly affected, becoming mentally incoherent for at least half a year. But now..."

Yin Shangren placed his finger in front of him.

At his fingertip, the muddy pool reappeared.

However, it was firmly restrained, moving within the range of his index finger.

"Everything within my body is the foundation of cultivation."

"As I wish, a single thought can achieve it," Yin Shangren murmured.

Next, Yin Shangren explained in detail his experience after "My Foundation Establishment" and his understanding of the "New Dharma" path.

"The Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate's new dharma is essentially imposing a shackle on all beings in the world, based on the existing cultivation system. As long as one cultivates, this shackle becomes a part of you. And all the bottlenecks on the path of cultivation ahead have been carved with specially shaped holes."

"Only by wearing the shackles and passing through these specifically shaped holes can one proceed."

Yin Shangren spoke meticulously, and before him, words materialized, spontaneously assembling and recording themselves.

"And the path of the new dharma, 'My Foundation Establishment,' is to integrate these imposed shackles into oneself!"

"On the bottlenecks ahead, you can adapt to any difficulty with your own changes..."

Yin Shangren described it in great detail, and Li Ping listened intently.

"For example, if you also wished to cultivate 'My Foundation Establishment,' you would likely have to refine and absorb this entire dynasty into your body..." he suddenly remarked.

Li Ping pondered for a moment, a look of comprehension appearing on his face, "If that were the case, my Emperor's Heavenly Qi Codex, and the countless subjects of Great Qi, would likely be frozen at the moment of my absorption."

"'My Foundation Establishment' buries all of one's past to forge a path of infinite future..."

Yin Shangren clapped his hands in praise, "Precisely!"

The words before him finally formed into a thin booklet. Yin Shangren held the booklet in his hand, his face filled with joy.

Even though it was his own summarized notes, he was intimately familiar with them, yet Yin Shangren flipped through it several times with great delight.

But looking at the blank pages that followed, his face showed difficulty.

"Primordial Golden Core. What is Primordial?"

...

Myriad Immortals Alliance, Immortal Alliance Headquarters.

Since Yan Huan's departure, no other outsider had entered the Yanfajue space.

Evidently, the impact of the previous curse attack had not yet subsided, and Yan Huan's visit had merely been a special arrangement.

Five hundred years of guarding time was not easily endured.

Thus, Elder Zhang Xu and Hua Yueye, the two guards, each had their own unique ways of passing the time.

Zhang Xu manifested a mortal world within his sea of consciousness.

Then, he sealed off a portion of his consciousness, cast himself into it, and reaped the rewards of experiencing various wondrous lives in reincarnation.

As for Hua Yueye, he divided himself into two.

The "two" individuals engaged in discussions and sparring.

No one understood oneself better than oneself, hence they were in perfect harmony and having a wonderful time.

As for Li Fan, his methods were not as playful.

While studying the latest array deduction results of the "End of All Dissolution Disk," he supervised the experiences of Saint Fetus and his clone.

Chapter 1156: True Foundation Building Explanation

The Essence of True Rebirth Solved

Therefore, when Li Ping heard Yin Shangren's Foundation Establishment insights, Li Fan's true self simultaneously became aware of them.

"Burying all of one's past to forge a path of infinite future?"

Li Fan mused in silence.

He suddenly thought of his "Return to Truth" treasure.

Based on his previous successful act of "Founding a True Foundation through a Hundred Lives," where a portion of "Return to Truth" was used to establish a new Dao foundation, it seemed "Return to Truth" had already merged with him.

"In other words, if I want to complete 'My Foundation Establishment,' I must encompass the entirety of 'Return to Truth'..."

The moment this thought arose, Li Fan found it somewhat absurd.

When "Return to Truth" is activated, everything in the world instantly transforms from substance to illusion, returning to its recorded anchor point.

Even True Immortals were no exception.

"After Yin Shangren completed 'My Foundation Establishment,' he gained complete mastery over the laws of his fragmented world. Similarly, if I were to achieve Foundation Establishment..."

"I would no longer need external assistance like 'Return to Truth,' and all restrictions like anchor points and energy charging could be ignored. With a mere thought, worlds could be created or destroyed, and I could return to any desired point in time..."

"This ability."

"There is probably no stronger Foundation Establishment stage than this, right?"

Li Fan shook his head inwardly.

"This forms a paradox."

"If I already possess such an ability, why would I still pursue the 'New New Dharma'? Defeating Dharma Transmission and crushing Faceless would be as easy as lifting a hand."

"Without a special method to help me understand and analyze the essence of 'Return to Truth' beforehand, this would be a dead end for me."

"Sometimes, having too strong a foundation isn't necessarily a good thing."

Li Fan unintentionally glanced towards the location of the Museum of Divine Treasures.

Earlier, when discussing with Yin Shangren, the latter had proposed a feasible method for stealing Mr. Bai's skull.

Lure the tiger away from its mountain and have Di San Mo tricked out of the Immortal Alliance headquarters.

Then, use a counterfeit skull to replace the original.

"Mr. Bai, at the cost of his life, reversed heaven and earth. All the spiritual essence on his body dissipated, becoming like the remains of an ordinary mortal."

"Uh... except for its exceptional hardness."

"So, as long as a perfectly identical skull can be replicated, and swapped without triggering the restrictions, it might be possible to retrieve Mr. Bai's skull unnoticed."

"Although theoretically possible, the practical execution..."

Yin Shangren shook his head and never mentioned the matter again.

But Li Fan never forgot it.

He was certain that Mr. Bai's remains held no anomalies.

Not only could Yin Shangren, a remnant soul from another world, not detect anything amiss, but even the Heavenly Profound Mirror, after analyzing Mr. Bai's rib, only gave it the lowest appraisal of 1 contribution point.

"But the skull is an exception."

"With Mr. Bai's eternal residual thoughts, it is bound to be extraordinary."

"During the use of eternal residual thoughts, 'Return to Truth' cannot be activated. Eternal residual thoughts also cannot be brought to the next life for use. Therefore..."

A glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"The best method is still to replicate the scene from the 119th iteration, stealing the 'Essence of Xuanhuang' and creating a relatively safe environment that others cannot attend to."

"Using the tactic of luring the tiger away from its mountain, what exactly is Di San Mo concerned about? Perhaps the answer can be found in the Immortal Falling Realm."

"And a large-scale operation within the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, without their notice..."

"The exposure of Dharma Transmission's scheme, forcing him into the open, attracting the attention of the entire Xuanhuang Realm."

A rough outline of a conspiracy instantly took shape within the original plan.

"Using Dharma Transmission's overwhelming and unfathomable power, forcing him to appear and explain is impossible through sheer strength alone. Only by threatening the Xuanhuang Realm, which he cares about..."

"However, this time, I don't have to be the villain."

On the chessboard, all the pieces were in place, awaiting Li Fan's slow move.

...

Just as Li Fan was concocting various nefarious schemes in the shadows,

the wisp of divine consciousness he had split off and attached to Wu Ninglu, discovered something quite interesting.

This Wu Ninglu was actually pregnant!

During the intervals of her focused cultivation, Li Fan's divine consciousness thoroughly examined the fetus in her womb, confirming it was indeed the offspring of Sun Ang, the identity Li Fan had assumed.

"However, it has been sealed by a secret method, halting its growth."

"This woman is quite interesting."

After observing for some time, Li Fan found that Wu Ninglu was not as simple-minded as Sun Ang appeared.

Her marriage into the Sun family seemed to have another purpose.

The news of Sun Ang's breakthrough to Dao Integration, which she had deliberately leaked earlier, led to Sun Ang being forced into the 500-year task of guarding Yanfajue. This was precisely to get Sun Ang out of the way.

And the benefits Sun Ang gained by sacrificing himself all went to this woman.

Using these precious resources, she cultivated with all her might.

Her progress in one month surpassed that of the previous three years.

Even Li Fan's divine consciousness faintly sensed that she would soon break through to the peak of Deity Transformation.

And one day, Wu Ninglu, who had been in seclusion at home, finally let her guard down.

As if she had suddenly become a different person, Wu Ninglu approached the mirror in the room, her slender fingers stroking her face.

Her gaze was dazed, yet occasionally a trace of ruthlessness flashed.

"My sister lives quite well, her cultivation speed is even faster than mine..."

Wu Ninglu's expression changed again, her smile vanishing. "Wu Ningjiu, have you gone mad! Possessing me now, aren't you afraid of being discovered by the Sun family!"

She tried to lower her voice, but her trembling body indicated her current anger.

Wu Ningjiu regained control of the body, still smiling smugly. "Sister, I'm not as idle as you think. If not for the elders' instructions, how would I dare to contact you so casually!"

"Listen carefully, we've received the latest news. Within three months, that treasure will return to the Sun family. At that time, you will need to ascertain the treasure's hiding place."

Wu Ningjiu's voice grew quieter and quieter, eventually becoming inaudible.

Wu Ninglu, who had returned to normal, had an unpredictable expression. She finally stomped her foot fiercely, seemingly having made a decision.

Li Fan's divine consciousness, observing the entire scene from beginning to end, became keenly interested.

"The Sun family's treasure? I've never heard of the Sun family possessing anything extraordinary."

The divine consciousness transformed into a wispy thread, stealthily infiltrating Wu Ninglu's sea of consciousness.

Although she had been trained and possessed strong defenses against divine sense intrusions, how could she escape Li Fan's deliberate assault?

Before long, Li Fan found the answer he was looking for.

This made him, who was initially merely bored and slightly interested, become quite serious.

"It's actually an existence suspected to be a transformed immortal artifact, similar to the 'Prosperous Bone Hand'?"

"How interesting."

The Sun family's ultimate treasure, its specific name and form were unknown to Wu Ninglu.

However, based on the Sun family's rise to prominence, the treasure's ability was likely related to deduction and foresight!

About a thousand years ago, the Sun family was merely an ordinary cultivation family.

The strongest in the clan was merely at the Nascent Soul stage.

But from a certain day onwards, the Sun family seemed to have suddenly struck gold. Not only did they break through several Deity Transformation realms consecutively, but they also encountered and saved a heavily injured Dao Integration cultivator by chance.

Under the protection of this Dao Integration grand cultivator, the Sun family soared to prominence.

The Sun family's sudden rise naturally attracted the attention of many forces. On the surface, it seemed purely based on luck.

But not everyone thought so.

Especially the forces who secretly plotted against the Dao Integration cultivator saved by the Sun family.

These were the forces that had instructed Wu Ninglu to risk seduction and infiltrate the Sun family.

The Chen family, one of the largest families in Tianquan Prefecture. Many family members were skilled in alchemy and held numerous important positions in the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Pill Hall.

At that time, they were simply plotting to kill that Dao Integration cultivator due to old grievances. However, a plan that should have been foolproof was thwarted by a mere Nascent Soul cultivator!

After eliminating possibilities, they confirmed there was no spy. Furthermore, the Sun family's Nascent Soul cultivator, on the day of the incident, suddenly traversed several prefectures via teleportation array, intercepting the Dao Integration cultivator who was fleeing in severe injury.

It was as if he had known this would happen!

All of this was highly anomalous. From then on, the Chen family began to watch the Sun family.

Under the Immortal Alliance's system, despite the vast disparity in strength between the two families, the Chen family dared not directly seize treasures. Especially after the heavily injured Dao Integration cultivator recovered and vaguely suspected the Chen family's involvement.

By the time the Chen family had resolved all their troubles and regained their composure,

the Sun family had already established connections with important figures in the Immortal Alliance headquarters and had relocated from another prefecture to Tianquan Prefecture. Furthermore, their own family had produced a Dao Integration cultivator.

The Sun family's rise was too rapid. The coincidences in their ascent further convinced the Chen family that the Sun family must be hiding a formidable treasure.

But the Sun family was extremely cautious. After solidifying their foundation, they rarely used the treasure.

Although the Chen family coveted it, they could not find a suitable opportunity to seize it.

Even within the clan, the matter had gradually been forgotten.

It wasn't until fifty years ago, when the Sun family once again made a significant impression within the Myriad Immortals Alliance, that it stirred their dormant memories.

On the path to the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, merely passing by, the Sun family patriarch recognized the identity of the infiltrator from the Five Elders Society!

He directly attacked, engaging in combat with the spy.

This incident naturally alarmed the higher echelons of the Immortal Alliance, who apprehended both of them. After an investigation, it was discovered that the Sun family patriarch's accusation was indeed true!

That Five Elders Society spy, possessing a law-seeking jade token, was ordered to attack Yanfajue with the "Vile Curse."

Fortunately, it was detected in time, averting a disaster!

After this incident, the Sun family progressed further, establishing influence within the Law Enforcement Hall.

Meanwhile, the Chen family refocused their attention on the Sun family.

After investigating past events, a few elders from the Chen family who remembered the incident at the time recalled their suspicions from back then.

Following this, a conspiracy surrounding the Sun family's ultimate treasure slowly unfolded.

After decades of constant probing, the Chen family had grasped several crucial clues.

First, the treasure might not be complete. Over the years, the Sun family had been secretly searching for something.

Second, every time the treasure displayed its ability, it seemed to require some form of replenishment. After each astonishing performance by the Sun family, the patriarch would mysteriously disappear for a period.

Third, the activation of the treasure seemed to come at the cost of depleting the Sun family's bloodline. Over the years, several Sun family descendants had vanished without a trace, neither seen alive nor dead.

Despite possessing much information, the Chen family had hesitated to seize the treasure, naturally due to its suspected "precognitive" ability.

If the attempt failed, they would expose themselves and possibly lose the chance to acquire the ultimate treasure forever.

Now, the Chen family, who had been patiently waiting, had finally encountered the best opportunity.

The spy discovered the whereabouts of the Sun family patriarch. It seemed he had sustained some injuries while assisting the treasure with replenishment. To prevent any accidents, he would likely cease his external activities and return home promptly to recuperate.

The treasure was still in its cooldown period, and the Sun family's strongest member, the patriarch, was heavily injured.

This was simply a godsend!

Therefore, the Chen family, risking discovery, ordered contact with Wu Ninglu, instructing her to constantly monitor the Sun family patriarch's movements.

...

"I never expected the enmity between the two families to continue for nearly a thousand years."

Li Fan, having understood the entire story, became even more intrigued by this so-called Sun family ultimate treasure.

If nothing else, the performance of the Sun family patriarch on several occasions bore too many similarities to his own past actions.

Li Fan had used "Return to Truth" to reverse everything, thereby achieving foresight.

What ability would the Sun family's ultimate treasure possess?

Li Fan did not have to wait long.

More than ten days later, Li Fan's divine consciousness keenly sensed the return of a somewhat disordered Dao Integration aura to the Sun family.

Leaving Wu Ninglu's body, he locked onto the target's location and stealthily approached.

Even though the Sun family patriarch was extremely cautious, the formations and restrictions he had set up were like thin air before Li Fan.

Without the slightest detection, a divine consciousness had followed him into the secret chamber.

"Cough, cough."

Sun Luyuan, the Sun family patriarch and a Dao Integration cultivator, even coughed up streaks of fresh blood.

However, he ignored his injuries, his eyes filled with heartache as he took out an object and carefully placed it back on its pedestal.

Then, he cut open a wound on his wrist and began refining it with his own blood.

And when Li Fan saw this object, both his true self tens of thousands of miles away and his clone simultaneously trembled slightly.

"This is..."

"The Heavenly Profound Mirror?"

The object Sun Luyuan was irrigating with his blood bore a striking resemblance to the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

However, in his previous encounters, the light representing the Heavenly Profound Mirror's power had mostly been green.

But the small mirror in the secret chamber before him now pulsed with a strange black light.

And even its aura...

Possessing a fragment of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's origin, Li Fan was very familiar with the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Yet, the peculiar small mirror before him felt like the Heavenly Profound Mirror's twin brother!

Li Fan's mind was shaken, and his thoughts raced.

"The Heavenly Profound Mirror was once called the Profound Heaven Mirror. The King of Profound Heaven of the Profound Heaven Sect obtained it from a flying ascension passage, an artifact from the Immortal Realm."

"Then what is this present one?"

At this moment, Li Fan couldn't help but have the urge to step forward and investigate.

But after contemplating for a moment, he ultimately stopped himself.

This black Heavenly Profound Mirror gave him an inexplicable sense of unease.

Li Fan decided to observe the situation first.

Drip, drip, the blood fell onto the mirror's surface. Sun Luyuan's face had already turned somewhat pale, but he showed no sign of stopping.

Li Fan even saw fear in his eyes, and his arm trembled slightly, attempting to retract.

But for some reason, he couldn't control his actions.

Only when the mirror surface emitted a strange fluctuation, the black light retracted inwards, and Sun Luyuan collapsed onto the ground as if drained of all strength.

After taking several pills and resting, his complexion returned to normal.

Sun Luyuan looked at the small mirror emitting a faint dark glow before him, a mixture of greed and fear flashing in his eyes.

He seemed lost in thought.

After a long while, his stiff body began to move again.

From his embrace, he took out another small mirror.

Adjusting the angle of its surface, he positioned it opposite the black mirror.

This newly retrieved mirror was, naturally, the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Li Fan clearly saw strands of green light being drawn from the Heavenly Profound Mirror's surface, flowing into the black mirror.

And after absorbing the Heavenly Profound Mirror, the black mirror seemed to become even more like the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Sun Luyuan appeared to be calculating the time.

After a while, while the black mirror was still devouring, his expression changed slightly, and he quickly made a hand seal to retract the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

But the ravenous black mirror was unwilling to let go!

A wave of black mist suddenly emerged from its surface, transforming into a humanoid shape, and roared at Sun Luyuan, "It's not enough!"

"I want to eat more!"

A powerful fluctuation surged from the black mirror figure, like a storm sweeping through the entire secret chamber.

Sun Luyuan gritted his teeth, insisting on retracting the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

While speaking to the black mirror figure, "Little brother, control your heart! Devouring too much at once will alert the Heavenly Profound Mirror, and we'll fail!"

The black mirror figure, upon hearing Sun Luyuan's words, seemed to regain a sliver of reason.

Its form flickered, as if resisting itself.

After a period of struggle, it finally suppressed its inner desires.

"Brother, I'm in too much pain..."

"Brother, I can't hold on."

"Brother, quickly let me out!"

Crying, pleading, hatred...

Various emotions flashed across the black mirror figure's form.

But regardless of its attitude, each sentence began with the word "Brother."

And Sun Luyuan seemed to suffer immensely from these calls.

Finally, he could only close his eyes and continue irrigating it with his own blood essence to quell the black mirror figure's resentment.

Having received the blood essence, the black mirror returned to calm.

Sun Luyuan, as if relieved of a great burden, slumped to the ground, devoid of the demeanor of a Dao Integration cultivator.

It took him a full half day to recover.

Standing before the black mirror again, he muttered.

As Sun Luyuan manipulated it, a beam of light emanated from the black mirror.

Countless characters and images flashed rapidly within.

Sun Luyuan watched with ravenous eagerness, concentrating intently, afraid of missing any detail.

Until finally, the brightness of the images dimmed and disappeared.

Sun Luyuan reluctantly withdrew his gaze.

"The gains this time are enough for our Sun family to overcome this crisis."

"Once Lu'er emerges from the Law Enforcement Hall and assumes an important position in the Immortal Alliance, with four Dao Integration cultivators in the family, our Sun family can truly establish a firm foothold."

Sun Luyuan muttered to himself.

Meanwhile, Li Fan's divine consciousness, which had observed the entire process from the side, began to understand some of its significance.

"It's not a comparable immortal artifact? But rather, using a human soul as a foundation, and employing some secret method to erode the Heavenly Profound Mirror? Thus obtaining a vast amount of information that cannot be acquired through normal means?"

"Even if it's not an immortal artifact, being able to infiltrate the Heavenly Profound Mirror is already extremely remarkable."

Li Fan looked at Sun Luyuan, who appeared to be greatly weakened.

While recuperating, he seemed to be digesting the information obtained from the black mirror with his eyes closed.

"With only one divine consciousness of mine, to control him..."

"I don't have absolute certainty. Especially with that bizarre black mirror beside him."

After repeated deliberation, Li Fan's divine consciousness chose not to act immediately.

Instead, he decided to lie in wait, to conceal himself.

To scheme gradually after Sun Luyuan separated from the black mirror.

Seven more days passed.

When Sun Luyuan opened his eyes, the first thing he did was repeatedly make hand seals, temporarily sealing the black mirror in the secret chamber.

Sensing Sun Luyuan's actions, the humanoid figure within the black mirror struggled again to emerge.

But it was firmly sealed within the mirror's surface, unable to escape.

With all turmoil subsided, Sun Luyuan breathed a sigh of relief.

He opened the layers of restrictions and left the secret chamber.

A moment later.

Li Fan's divine consciousness quietly flew to the side of the black mirror.

"The material of this mirror body..."

"It doesn't seem to be a product of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"It seems the speculation of it being an immortal artifact is not entirely incorrect."

"However, the origin power of the immortal path is long gone, leaving only an empty shell, occupied by that figure."

With Li Fan's current knowledge, after careful observation, he made a discovery.

To verify his guess, the divine consciousness began to study the seal left by Sun Luyuan.

"Hmm? It has some characteristics of an immortal-grade formation. But it's too crude."

The true self, utilizing the "End of All Dissolution Disk," provided support. In a short time, it was deciphered.

Then, Li Fan's divine consciousness did not directly destroy the seal but slowly modified it based on its foundation.

"Brother, why are you back so quickly this time?"

"Did you encounter any difficulties? Hehehe..."

The voice of the black shadow emanated from within the mirror.

Li Fan did not answer, continuing to modify the array seal.

The black shadow babbled to itself for a while before finally sensing something was wrong.

"You're not brother?"

"Who are you?"

Its voice was filled with anger and panic.

"Disgusting thing, stay away from me!"

The black shadow shrieked, and the black mirror trembled violently.

"Noisy!" Li Fan snorted coldly.

A silver lightning bolt appeared from the void and struck the black mirror fiercely.

The mirror body, forged from an unknown material, actually showed a trace of black scorching.

The black shadow's shrieks were interrupted by a scream of pain.

After a brief silence, the black shadow seemed to have recovered.

"You..."

It was about to lash out again, only to be met by another lightning bolt.

A recommended book on the 'farming' genre, titled 'Fourth Natural Disaster', is available for interested readers.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1157: A Different Kind of Profound Heavenly Artifact

The Immortal Artifact - Boundless Mirror

Silver flashes, like heavenly bolts, descended continuously.

Under the majestic divine power, the humanoid figure hidden within the black mirror, initially cursing, transformed into wails, and then into pleas.

But Li Fan's divine consciousness had no intention of showing mercy from the beginning.

Divine consciousness, unlike clones, cannot independently absorb spiritual energy from heaven and earth to recover. Every bit of power used is diminished, so it must be done with absolute certainty.

The silver lightning bolts acted like a giant grinding wheel, processing the black humanoid mist.

Meanwhile, Li Fan's divine consciousness, utilizing the "Array Refining" method, attempted to gain control of the black mirror.

The black mirror was not originally owned by anyone, but periodic irrigation with blood from Sun family disciples had established a subtle, mysterious connection with the Sun clan.

Under normal circumstances, only Sun family members could use and even refine it.

However, Li Fan's array, empowered by the accumulation of generations from the "End of All Dissolution Disk," had reached an unfathomable level.

Under layers of arrays, it could actually bypass this rule.

Even Sun Luyuan, who had a special connection with the black mirror, could not detect the black mirror being refined by Li Fan's divine consciousness.

As time slowly passed, unnoticed, the black mirror quietly changed hands.

Li Fan's divine consciousness materialized and juggled the black mirror in his hand.

He could feel the black mist humanoid figure, the "artifact spirit" of the black mirror, cowering within,

filled with fear and apprehension towards Li Fan.

Li Fan didn't care what the spirit thought. His eyes narrowed, and in an instant, he learned the origin of the Sun family's ultimate treasure.

Over a thousand years ago, the Sun brothers, Sun Luyuan and Sun Luoyao, accidentally discovered a slightly damaged bronze mirror during an exploration of an ancient ruin.

Initially, the two brothers thought the bronze mirror was just an ordinary antique and paid it little mind. However, when they took it to the Heavenly Profound Mirror to sell, something truly incredible happened.

The Heavenly Profound Mirror completely ignored the bronze mirror, or rather, completely overlooked its existence! Even though it was within the Heavenly Profound Mirror's space, it simply couldn't appear on the list of items for sale.

After repeated confirmations, the two brothers knew they had stumbled upon a treasure.

Subsequently, through various attempts, they tried to find the correct method to use this miraculous bronze mirror. But at that time, they were merely Golden Core stage cultivators, and their strength and knowledge were insufficient to achieve this.

A hundred years later.

Elder brother Sun Luyuan found a miniature cave-heaven and intended to use it to advance to the Nascent Soul stage.

Sun Luoyao acted as his protector. Despite their extreme caution, fate intervened, and they alarmed another passing cultivator at the peak of Golden Core.

Golden Core to Nascent Soul – a chasm of a realm.

With the opportunity for breakthrough right before him, the Golden Core cultivator naturally wouldn't give it up.

And to ensure his elder brother's smooth advancement, Sun Luoyao, to buy time, held back the enemy's attack with his own life.

When Sun Luyuan successfully broke through to the Nascent Soul stage and furiously slew the Golden Core cultivator, Sun Luoyao, due to his severe injuries, was on the verge of death. He was already beyond saving.

Just as Su Luyuan was plunged into despair, he suddenly discovered that the bronze mirror he had always carried finally reacted!

At the brink of death, Sun Luoyao's divine soul entered the bronze mirror, preserving itself.

Although he could no longer emerge from the bronze mirror afterwards, it was still better than being separated by life and death.

His divine soul merged with the bronze mirror, and Sun Luoyao subsequently learned all the information about the mirror.

The bronze mirror's original name was [Boundless], a supreme treasure bestowed by the Immortal Realm in ancient times to Xuanhuang's [Boundless Sect].

However, with the passage of time, this immortal artifact inexplicably became damaged and incomplete, losing most of its former power.

Even its artifact spirit was nowhere to be found, leaving only its physical form in the world.

But after all, it was an existence from beyond the mortal realm.

After merging with a new divine soul, it still displayed some incredible abilities.

For example...

When entering the Heavenly Profound Mirror, it could steal various information from the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

For example, after accumulating energy for a period, the Boundless Mirror could release faint projections.

These projections depicted future events!

Although the principle was unclear, this discovery sent the Sun brothers into raptures.

With the help of the Boundless Mirror, the Sun brothers began their legendary path to rise.

However, gradually, they also discovered the eerie aspects of this mirror.

Due to prior damage, the mirror's imperfection also affected Sun Luoyao within the mirror. His divine soul eroded, and no matter how many methods Sun Luyuan tried, he couldn't stop it.

Finally, by chance, he used his own blood essence to delay the dissipation of his brother's divine soul.

If it were merely this.

After reaching the Nascent Soul stage, New Dharma cultivators embodied cave-heavens and were indestructible. Blood essence could be squeezed out, so there was always some to spare.

The true trouble with the Boundless Mirror was its tendency towards self-destruction.

As if it had experienced unimaginable calamities, the "Boundless Light" projections of future scenarios always led to the same conclusion.

Endless darkness, great annihilation, utter void.

As if it were the fate of the entire world, no matter how the Boundless Mirror projected, it couldn't escape this outcome.

And each time it awakened from annihilation and projected the Boundless Light again.

The Boundless Mirror seemed to have absorbed the blackness of annihilation from the prophecy, becoming a shade darker.

Over a thousand years, although the Sun family, with the abilities of the Boundless Mirror, rose from an insignificant humble family to a behemoth with four Dao Integration cultivators,

Sun Luyuan also transformed from a former Nascent Soul cultivator to a grand Dao Integration cultivator.

Yet, he remained powerless to prevent the Boundless Mirror from heading towards destruction.

The only solution he could find was to locate the missing fragments of the Boundless Mirror and help it replenish itself.

Over the years, with the mutual sensory connection between their main bodies, he found another fragment of the Boundless Mirror.

However, this only slowed down the rate of destruction, failing to fundamentally resolve the issue.

And the abilities displayed by the Sun family during their rise had long attracted the attention of those with ulterior motives.

Setting aside the many malicious individuals outside, the greatest benefactor of the Sun family's rise was one of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's highest centers of power.

The Mirror Holder.

One of them, named [Fu], knew of the Boundless Mirror's existence.

However, he did not try to seize it. Instead, he even sponsored the Sun family's rise.

This was precisely because he valued the Boundless Mirror's ability to infiltrate the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"A damaged immortal artifact, though incomparable to a genuine Profound Heaven artifact, still has its merits."

"Find a way to restore its power to the maximum extent possible."

"Perhaps in the future, we Mirror Holders might find a use for it."

Sun Luyuan knew this was a poisoned chalice, but he had no choice but to swallow it.

According to [Fu]'s instructions, the Sun family had to earn enough merit before he could have sufficient reason to arrange for promotion.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance is not a monolithic entity. Even among us Mirror Holders, not everyone is united."

"So don't be afraid of you causing a stir, just be afraid of you not causing one."

It was precisely at Fu's instigation that Sun Luyuan performed the act of high-profilely and luckily capturing the Five Elders Society spy.

Anyone with discerning eyes could see the trickery involved.

However, those with backing, after investigating and discovering the Mirror Holder [Fu] behind the Sun family, quietly backed down.

As for those who lacked the ability to even know this much...

Sun Luyuan didn't care about them at all.

After all, one must consider the owner even when beating a dog.

There was no need for the Sun family to act; when those individuals showed hostility, numerous families eager to please the Mirror Holder Fu would silently and collectively tear them apart.

However...

It was highly unlikely that Sun Luyuan ever imagined he would encounter a monster like Li Fan, who defied all common sense.

A single divine consciousness could crack the Sun family's blood sacrifice accumulated over thousands of years.

And claim the immortal artifact, the Boundless Mirror, for himself.
