Even a damaged and near-destroyed immortal artifact held immeasurable value.

Moreover, in Li Fan's hands, this immortal artifact might not be beyond saving.

At this moment, in the Sun family's secret chamber, Li Fan, ignoring Sun Luoyao's pleas, forced him to activate the Boundless Mirror's deduction function.

A beam of light suddenly erupted from the surface of the black mirror.

The beam condensed in mid-air, forming a white light screen.

Soon, scenes began to shift and change on the light screen.

When Li Fan clearly saw the images, his heart couldn't help but tighten.

Ten thousand Sky Patrol Arrows whistled towards various locations of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

Countless cultivators were engaged in fierce battle, one side being the Myriad Immortals Alliance, naturally.

And the other side was led by a peculiar puppet.

"This... is the United Realms Association of the future?"

Li Fan saw familiar figures like Tianyang and Sun Erlang among the rapidly flashing images.

According to the plan for this lifetime, after the Great Qi annexed numerous small worlds, friction with the Myriad Immortals Alliance was inevitable.

But at this point in time, none of that had happened yet.

This Boundless Mirror could actually depict future events!

The light beam did not last long.

The screen accelerated, changing so rapidly that even Li Fan couldn't discern the shifts.

Finally, the beam instantly retracted.

Returning to complete darkness and void.

Li Fan felt an instinctive sense of crisis from this annihilation.

The deduction ended, and the blackness returned to the Boundless Mirror.

Sun Luoyao then let out a terrified, frantic howl.

It was as if he had personally witnessed something extremely terrifying.

But as the master of the Boundless Mirror, Li Fan could not perceive anything synchronously from him.

Li Fan had no intention of helping him alleviate the pain by irrigating him with blood essence.

He simply let him experience it, while contemplating inwardly.

"The aura of that deduced light beam felt strangely familiar?"

"Could it be..."

Two names instantly flashed in Li Fan's mind.

[Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Unite in Calculation].

[Desolation, Empty Chamber Blossoms].

"Same origin, part of the same grand array."

"Boundless, ..."

Li Fan found it difficult to discern the remaining names of the array.

However, this similarity was enough to provide him with inspiration.

"The Boundless Mirror is becoming increasingly damaged. Perhaps the influence of deducing the future of annihilation is a factor, but a larger reason is the defective immortal artifact body, which is insufficient to activate immortal-grade arrays."

"The consequence of forced activation is the continuous consumption of its immortal artifact body. The more it's used, the faster it perishes."

"This Sun family is truly a bunch of fools, truly a waste of heavenly resources. If they hadn't urged it on so frequently without repairing it, this Boundless Mirror wouldn't have ended up in my hands in such a damaged state."

Thinking thus, Li Fan caressed the completely blackened mirror body with some heartache.

"Hmm, rectifying this might be a bit difficult with my current abilities. I'll still need to find a skilled craftsman..."

Li Fan wasn't particularly concerned about the Boundless Mirror's deduction ability.

A future that was deduced might not necessarily happen, so how could it compare to his own lived experiences and actual future?

But the title of the first immortal artifact he acquired was enough to make Li Fan take it seriously.

"Perhaps, during the process of repairing it, I can find a method for the 'End of All Dissolution Disk' to truly transform and advance."

"Immortal artifacts born from the Xuanhuang Realm. Although their law power might have become part of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, we cannot rule out that, like the Boundless Mirror, the immortal artifact body still remains."

"Perhaps I should pay attention to collecting them."

...

For the next period, Li Fan's divine consciousness did not leave the secret chamber.

It resided within the Boundless Mirror, studying the other uses of this damaged immortal artifact.

Simultaneously, he sorted and categorized the information obtained by the Boundless Mirror from its intrusion into the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Possessing a fragment of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's origin and having previously spied on its secrets, Li Fan quickly discovered the differences between these two methods of "peeping."

Undoubtedly, the Heavenly Profound Mirror also possessed self-awareness.

Through the Heavenly Profound Mirror's origin, Li Fan had seen all sorts of data generated during the Heavenly Profound Mirror's management of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's daily affairs, as well as records of cultivators' activities and conversations.

But the intel obtained by the Boundless Mirror...

It was more like the Heavenly Profound Mirror's own "thoughts" and "conclusions."

For example, based on the aggregation of vast amounts of information, the Heavenly Profound Mirror's trading market indicated a trend of decreasing production for a certain item.

Therefore, even though the event hadn't happened yet, the Heavenly Profound Mirror, having acquired sufficient intelligence, had already made the judgment that the item's price would soon skyrocket.

However, as the foundation of the Immortal Alliance, bound by Dharma Transmission, the Heavenly Profound Mirror was incapable of taking any independent action.

It had to wait until the event actually occurred and caused certain consequences, after which the decision would be made by the higher echelons of the Immortal Alliance, such as the Dharma Transmitters and Mirror Holders, before any adjustments could be made.

Although it lacked autonomy, it did not prevent the Heavenly Profound Mirror from forecasting and judging the countless events occurring within its purview daily.

These "thoughts" of the Heavenly Profound Mirror did not affect its actual operations.

They merely appeared and then settled in the deepest recesses of the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"No wonder the Mirror Holders value it so highly."

"Isn't this equivalent to a mind-reading technique specifically for the Heavenly Profound Mirror?"

"Even if it can only read fragments due to its damage, any single piece of information is priceless!"

The Heavenly Profound Mirror, as a genuine immortal artifact and the cornerstone of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's operations.

Looking down from above.

Its judgments were absolutely correct and far ahead of the cultivators within it.

Li Fan recalled how the Heavenly Profound Mirror, in league with Mo Jubin, had tricked him several times in his previous life.

A dangerous glint appeared in his eyes.

Chapter 1158: Secret Art of Devouring Heaven Profound

Secret Art Devours the Profound Heaven

Having suffered such a great loss at the hands of Mo Jubin and the Heavenly Profound Mirror, it was impossible for Li Fan to not harbor any thoughts of revenge.

However, Mo Jubin, as one of the Dharma Kings of the Profound Heaven Sect, possessed unfathomable abilities. He could infiltrate the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters as if it were his own home.

Although he later died inexplicably in the Netherworld, Li Fan currently lacked the absolute confidence to subdue him.

Without fundamental conflicts of interest, Li Fan had no intention of provoking him in this lifetime.

"Perhaps I can secretly learn how the Myriad Immortals Alliance dealt with this Profound Heaven Sect Dharma King."

According to the normal historical trajectory, Mo Jubin would have been exposed by the Myriad Immortals Alliance without ever awakening.

Perhaps there were special methods within the Myriad Immortals Alliance to deal with Profound Heaven Sect members. With preemptive action, Mo Jubin might indeed have lost the power to resist.

At that time, Li Fan could simply follow suit and repeat the same strategy against Mo Jubin in future lives.

But if Mo Jubin, like in the 119th iteration, was merely feigning defeat and actually using the opportunity to infiltrate...

Then, before finding a definitive method to deal with him, Li Fan would not actively oppose Mo Jubin.

As for the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Possessing a fragment of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's origin already placed him in an invincible position.

Now that he had also mastered a method to pry into its internal workings...

If heaven bestows it, and one does not accept, one invites calamity!

Li Fan's mind rapidly churned.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance searching for Mo Jubin in the ruins of various sects was precisely to advance the method of controlling the Heavenly Profound Mirror. This should be subtly pushed by the Mirror Holder faction."

"Cang, Fu. Heh heh. Neither of these two are easy to deal with."

"But they also represent my opportunity."

With thoughts swirling, Li Fan transformed back into a ethereal light and entered the Boundless Mirror.

Within it, he continued to construct arrays, solidifying his control.

While waiting for Sun Luyuan to return to the secret chamber, he also studied the traces of immortal-grade arrays remaining in the Boundless Mirror.

...

Great Qi, Holy Capital.

During this period, as Wang Xuanba diligently traveled throughout numerous regions of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Besides Yin Shangren, Oubei Zi's father and son, Ximen Yu, and other "Stars of Xuanhuang" chosen by Li Ping, were all "tricked" into the Great Qi Holy Dynasty, using the Holy Emperor's rhetoric.

Of course, not everyone on this list was persuaded. Some not only refused the invitation but even killed Wang Xuanba's clone.

Wang Xuanba was not angered, merely noting down their names and reporting them to the Holy Emperor.

Then, he skipped them and invited the next person.

Upon their arrival in Great Qi, the "Stars of Xuanhuang" were personally received by Li Ping and, like Yin Shangren, settled down in the Holy Dynasty.

They each found their own endeavors.

For instance, Ximen Yu was promised Li Ping's assistance in delving deeper into his research on terrestrial vein power. Li Ping also revealed some crucial information about the ancient Earth Vein Tree.

As for Oubei Zi, he would be responsible for the construction of the new Holy Capital of Great Qi. Furthermore, every conquered small world in the future Holy Dynasty would have Oubei Zi as the chief planning designer for overall transformation.

Most importantly, Li Ping immediately recognized that Ou Shangtian possessed the "Prosperous Bone Hand" and "Ten Thousand Deaths Ledger," two rare treasures. He then accepted Ou Shangtian as his personal disciple.

Ou Shangtian felt no ill will from Li Ping.

Moreover, the interesting immortal cultivation world secrets and profound Dao principles discussed by the Holy Emperor deeply captivated the young Ou Shangtian.

Thus, he willingly became his disciple.

In life, one seeks fame, fortune, or contentment.

And all these could be fulfilled by Holy Emperor Li Ping.

As for those who did not answer the call...

Their fate had already been decided in Li Ping's heart.

Beneath the Holy Emperor's seat.

Deeper than Yin Shangren's underground secret chamber.

The secret intelligence agency of the Holy Dynasty, named the "Sky Supervision Department," was gradually established.

As the central node of the "Myriad Spirits Grand Formation," all affairs within the small world under the formation's coverage could be observed.

When the Holy Dynasty eventually embarked on its conquest and incorporated other small worlds into its territory, they would also be strictly monitored by the Sky Supervision Department.

Not only that.

In Li Ping's vision, the name "Sky Supervision" was not limited to those small worlds.

It even encompassed the entire Xuanhuang Realm itself.

With the help of paper figures from the Crossing Tribulation Sect and the Heavenly Profound Mirror...

Building a comprehensive intelligence system was not a difficult task.

The secret agents of the Sky Supervision Department would be personally selected by Li Ping.

The influence of the celestial phenomenon "[Heaven Opens Its Favor, Stars Descend to the World]" on the Great Qi small world had already begun to manifest. Recently, among the infants born in the Holy Dynasty, there were many who exhibited innate supernatural abilities.

Holy Medicine Institutes were established throughout the land. Li Ping could immediately sense the constitution of all infants upon their birth.

From childhood, they would receive Li Ping's personal training. Upon growing up, they would either serve in the Sky Supervision Department or participate in Yin Shangren's New Dharma deduction project...

Making the best use of everything.

Both talent and the growth of an empire require time.

The Great Qi Holy Dynasty was developing at an extraordinary pace, but currently, the most anticipated event in the Holy Dynasty was a grand competition.

A fishing competition.

Organized by decree of the Holy Emperor himself, anyone in the country interested could participate, regardless of prior fishing experience.

Regional winners would advance to the Holy Capital for the final competition.

At that time, the Holy Emperor would also appear to share in the joy with the populace.

The top hundred contestants in the competition would receive generous rewards, enough to ensure a common family's lifelong sustenance and comfort.

Furthermore, those who performed exceptionally in the competition would reportedly receive additional unique rewards from the Holy Emperor.

The news had been released for half a month, and the response was overwhelming.

If not for the assistance of Immortal Masters from various regions, the fish in all the rivers and lakes might have been depleted, leading to an embarrassing situation where there were no fish left to catch.

In addition to ordinary citizens, the Holy Emperor's disciples would also participate.

This undoubtedly greatly stimulated people's enthusiasm.

As is widely known, the Holy Emperor had publicly stated more than once that he had no heirs now and would not have any in the future.

The Holy Emperor had no descendants.

His disciples were, without a doubt, the successors to the Holy Dynasty.

If one could be favored by the Holy Emperor in the fishing competition and accepted as a direct disciple...

The opportunity to soar like a fish leaping over the dragon gate was within reach!

Fueled by these rumors, the current commoners of Great Qi had become somewhat obsessed with "fishing."

It was even considered more important than studying or cultivating.

And all of this, Li Ping naturally saw.

He allowed and even encouraged it, naturally, for the sake of the Fishing Pond treasure.

This immortal artifact, even surpassing the Xuanhuang Realm's existence.

It held countless opportunities.

Perhaps his way out of the predicament was hidden within it.

He would certainly not miss an opportunity to acquire numerous divine items at no cost.

Even casually fishing out a secret treasure could significantly increase the Holy Dynasty's combat strength.

Chapter 1159: Immeasurable Mirror of Immortality

The Immortal Artifact, Boundless Mirror

Silver flashes, like heavenly lightning bolts, fell continuously.

Under the majestic divine power, the humanoid figure hidden within the black mirror, from cursing to wailing, then to begging.

But Li Fan's divine sense had no intention of showing mercy from the beginning.

Divine senses, unlike clones, cannot independently absorb spiritual energy from heaven and earth to recover. Every bit of power used is reduced, so it must be foolproof.

The silver lightning bolts acted like a giant grinding wheel, processing the black fog humanoid.

Meanwhile, Li Fan's divine sense took the opportunity to repeatedly form hand seals, using the "Array Refining" technique to attempt to gain control of the black mirror.

The black mirror was not an object with a master, but through periodic irrigation with the bloodlines of Sun family disciples, it had developed a mysterious and subtle connection with the Sun clan.

Under normal circumstances, only Sun family members could use it, let alone refine it.

However, Li Fan's array, empowered by the accumulation of several lifetimes of the 'Terminus Dissipation Disk,' had reached a level beyond comprehension.

Under the superposition of multiple arrays, it could actually ignore this rule.

Moreover, Li Fan's divine sense could even refine the black mirror at this moment without Sun Luoyuan, who had a special connection with it, being able to detect it.

As time slowly passed, unnoticed, the black mirror had quietly changed hands.

Li Fan's divine sense materialized, and he casually tossed the black mirror in his hand.

He could feel the black fog humanoid, the "artifact spirit" of the black mirror, cowering inside, trembling with fear and apprehension towards Li Fan.

Li Fan did not care what the other party thought. His eyes narrowed, and in an instant, he learned the origin of this Sun family heirloom.

More than a thousand years ago, the Sun brothers, Sun Luoyuan and Sun Luoyao, accidentally discovered a slightly damaged bronze mirror during an exploration of ancient ruins.

Initially, the two brothers thought the bronze mirror was just an ordinary antique and didn't pay much attention to it. However, when they took it back to the Heavenly Profound Mirror to sell, something unbelievable happened.

The Heavenly Profound Mirror completely ignored the bronze mirror, or rather, completely overlooked its existence! Even though it was in the Heavenly Profound Mirror's space, it could not appear on the sales list.

After repeated confirmation, the two brothers knew they had found a treasure.

Next, they tried various methods to find the correct way to use this magical bronze mirror. But at that time, they were only cultivators at the Golden Core stage, and their strength and knowledge were insufficient to achieve this.

A hundred years later.

Elder brother Sun Luoyuan found a miniature grotto-heaven, intending to use it to advance to the Nascent Soul stage.

Sun Luoyao acted as his protector. Although they were very cautious, fate was unpredictable, and they inadvertently alerted another passing cultivator at the peak Golden Core stage.

Golden Core and Nascent Soul, a world of difference.

With the opportunity for breakthrough right before him, that Golden Core cultivator naturally would not give up.

And to ensure his elder brother could successfully break through, Sun Luoyao even used his life to delay the enemy's attack.

When Sun Luoyuan successfully broke through to the Nascent Soul stage and angrily killed the Golden Core cultivator, Sun Luoyao was already on the brink of death due to severe injuries and could no longer hold on.

Just as Sun Luoyuan was grief-stricken, he suddenly discovered that the bronze mirror he had always carried finally reacted at this moment!

At the moment of near-death, Sun Luoyao's divine soul escaped into the bronze mirror, thus preserving it.

Although he could never come out of the bronze mirror afterward, it was better than being separated by death.

Having merged his divine soul with the bronze mirror, Sun Luoyuan also learned all about the mirror's information.

The bronze mirror was originally named "Boundless" and was a supreme treasure bestowed by the Immortal Realm upon the Xuanhuang's "Boundless Sect" in ancient times.

However, as time passed, this immortal artifact became broken and incomplete for some unknown reason, losing most of its former power.

Even its original spirit was nowhere to be found, leaving only its shell in the world.

But after all, it was an existence from above the mortal world.

After integrating with a new divine soul, it still displayed some incredible abilities.

For example...

When entering the Heavenly Profound Mirror, it could steal all sorts of information from the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

For example, after accumulating energy for a period, the Boundless Mirror could release faint illusions.

These illusions depicted future events!

Although the principle behind it was unclear, this discovery sent the Sun brothers into ecstasy.

With the help of the Boundless Mirror, the Sun brothers began their legendary rise.

However, slowly, they also discovered the strange aspects of this mirror.

Due to previous damage, the incompleteness of the mirror also affected Sun Luoyao within the mirror. His divine soul gradually eroded, and no matter how many methods Sun Luoyuan tried, he could not stop it.

Finally, by chance, he used his own vital blood to delay the dissipation of his brother's divine soul.

If it were only this.

After achieving the Nascent Soul stage, cultivators of the New Dharma, carrying their grotto-heavens, were indestructible. Vital blood could be squeezed out, and there was always some.

The true trouble with the Boundless Mirror was its tendency towards self-destruction.

As if it had experienced unimaginable calamities, the "Boundless Light" scenes that reenacted future scenarios always ended with the same outcome.

Utter darkness, great destruction, emptiness.

As if it were the destiny of the entire world, no matter how the Boundless Mirror re-enacted, it could not escape this ending.

And each time it awakened from destruction and re-enacted the Boundless Light.

The Boundless Mirror seemed to become stained with the blackness of destruction from the prophecy, becoming a shade darker.

Over the past thousand years, although the Sun family, with the ability of the Boundless Mirror, had risen from an insignificant obscure family to a colossus with four Dao Integration cultivators,

Sun Luoyuan had also evolved from a former Nascent Soul cultivator to a Dao Integration great cultivator.

Yet, they were still powerless to stop the Boundless Mirror from heading towards destruction.

The only solution he could find was to find the incomplete fragments of the Boundless Mirror and help complete itself.

Over the years, with the mutual induction between their main bodies, he had found another fragment of the Boundless Mirror.

But this only slowed down the speed of destruction, without fundamentally solving the problem.

And the abilities displayed by the Sun family during their rise had long since attracted the attention of those with ulterior motives.

Not to mention the many individuals outside with evil intentions, the greatest benefactor of the Sun family's rise was one of the highest centers of power in the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

The Mirror Holder.

One of them, named "Fu," knew of the Boundless Mirror's existence.

But instead of seizing it, he even funded the Sun family's rise.

It was precisely because he was interested in the Boundless Mirror's ability to infiltrate the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"A broken immortal artifact, although it cannot compare to a true Heavenly Profound Heavy Artifact, it still has its merits."

"Find a way to restore its power to the maximum extent you can."

"Perhaps it will be useful to us Mirror Holders in the future."

Sun Luoyuan knew this was like swallowing poison disguised as sweet candy, but he had no choice but to comply.

According to his original plan, the Sun family should develop with as much low-keyness as possible.

But things did not go as planned.

Chapter 1160: Reading Heart Heavenly Profound Mirror

Reading Hearts with the Heavenly Profound Mirror

According to "Fu's" instructions, the Sun family would only gain an advantage if they made enough contributions to allow him sufficient reason to arrange for promotion.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance is not a monolithic entity. Even within the Mirror Holders, not everyone is united."

"So don't be afraid of making a big fuss, fear only that you can't make a fuss at all."

It was also under Fu's suggestion that Sun Luoyuan performed the act of high-profilely and luckily apprehending the Five Elders Society spy.

Anyone with discerning eyes could see the trickery involved.

However, those with backing, after investigating and discovering the Mirror Holder "Fu" behind the Sun family, all quietly backed down.

As for those who lacked the ability to even discover this...

Sun Luoyuan didn't care about them at all.

After all, even a dog needs to consider its owner.

There was no need for the Sun family to act; when those individuals showed hostility, they would be silently and collectively torn apart by the countless families eager to please the Mirror Holder Fu.

However...

Perhaps Sun Luoyuan never imagined that he would encounter a monster like Li Fan, who completely defied common sense.

With just a divine sense clone, he could break the Sun family's blood sacrifice of thousands of years.

And seize the immortal artifact Boundless Mirror for himself.

Even a broken immortal artifact on the verge of destruction is invaluable.

Moreover, in Li Fan's hands, this immortal artifact might not be beyond saving.

At this moment, in the Sun family's secret chamber, Li Fan, disregarding Sun Luoyao's pleas, forced him to activate the Boundless Mirror's divination function.

Suddenly, a beam of light erupted from the black mirror surface.

The beam condensed in mid-air, forming a white light screen.

Soon, scenes began to change rapidly on the light screen.

When Li Fan saw the content of the images, he couldn't help but slightly tense up.

Tens of thousands of Sky-Patrolling Arrows, whistling towards all parts of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

Countless cultivators were engaged in fierce battles. One side was naturally the Myriad Immortals Alliance,

while the other was led by a peculiar puppet.

"This is... the future United Worlds Association?"

Li Fan saw familiar figures like Tian Yang and Sun Erlang among the rapidly flashing images.

According to the plan for this generation, after Great Qi annexed numerous small worlds, friction with the Myriad Immortals Alliance was inevitable.

But at this point in time, none of that had happened yet.

This Boundless Mirror could actually depict future events!

The light beam did not last long.

The screen sped up, even to the point where Li Fan couldn't discern the changes.

Finally, the light beam instantly retracted.

Returning to complete black void.

Li Fan felt an instinctive sense of crisis from this destruction.

The divination concluded, and the blackness returned to the Boundless Mirror.

Sun Luoyao then let out terrified, insane wails.

As if he had personally witnessed something extremely terrifying.

But as the owner of the Boundless Mirror, Li Fan could not perceive anything synchronously from him.

Li Fan had no intention of feeding it vital blood to alleviate its pain.

He simply let it convulse while pondering inwardly in his mind.

"That divination beam, its aura is surprisingly familiar?"

"It's..."

In Li Fan's mind, two names instantly surfaced.

"Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Counting."

"Luo Falls, Void Chamber Blooms Flowers."

"Same origin, part of the same grand formation."

"Boundless,..."

Li Fan couldn't quite decipher the remaining names of the formation.

However, these similarities were enough to inspire him.

"The Boundless Mirror is becoming increasingly dilapidated. Perhaps the influence of deducing the future of annihilation is a factor. But the greater reason is that the broken immortal artifact body is insufficient to propel the immortal-level formation."

"The consequence of forcibly activating it is the constant consumption of its immortal artifact body. The more it is used, the faster it perishes."

"This Sun family is truly a bunch of idiots, truly a waste of heavenly resources. If they hadn't activated it so frequently without repairing it first. When it fell into my hands, it would not have been damaged to this extent."

Thinking this, Li Fan gently touched the completely blackened mirror body with a hint of heartache.

"Hmm, to repair it, my current abilities might be stretched. I'll still need to find a skilled craftsman..."

Li Fan wasn't particularly concerned about the Boundless Mirror's divination ability.

A future depicted in deduction might not necessarily come true, so how could it compare to the future he had personally experienced and known to be real?

But the title of the first immortal artifact acquired was enough to make Li Fan attach importance to it.

"Perhaps, during the process of repairing it, I can find the method for the 'Terminus Dissipation Disk' to truly transform and ascend."

"Immortal artifact creation in the Xuanhuang Realm. Although the power of the laws might have become part of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, it's not impossible that, like the Boundless Mirror, its immortal artifact body still remains."

"Perhaps I should pay attention to collecting them."

...

For the next period, Li Fan's divine sense did not leave the secret chamber.

It simply resided within the Boundless Mirror, studying the other uses of this damaged immortal artifact.

At the same time, he sorted and classified the information obtained from the Boundless Mirror's intrusion into the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Possessing one origin of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, Li Fan, who had previously extensively spied on the Heavenly Profound Mirror's secrets, quickly discovered the difference between these two types of "peeking."

Undoubtedly, the Heavenly Profound Mirror also possessed self-awareness.

Through the origin of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, he saw the various data generated by the Heavenly Profound Mirror in managing the daily affairs of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, as well as records of cultivators' activities and conversations.

But what the Boundless Mirror spied on...

Was more like the Heavenly Profound Mirror's own "thoughts" and "conclusions."

For example, based on the aggregation of vast amounts of information, the Heavenly Profound Mirror's trading market indicated a tendency for a certain item's output to decrease.

Therefore, even though the event had not yet occurred, the Heavenly Profound Mirror, armed with sufficient intelligence, had already made the judgment that the price of this item was about to soar.

But as the foundation of the Immortal Alliance, bound by Dharma Transmission, the Heavenly Profound Mirror had no way to react autonomously.

It had to wait until the event actually occurred and caused a certain consequence, after which the higher echelons of the Immortal Alliance, such as the Dharma Transmitters and Mirror Holders, would jointly discuss and decide on adjustments.

Although it lacked autonomy, it did not prevent the Heavenly Profound Mirror from predicting and judging the countless events that occurred within its scope of observation daily.

These "thoughts" of the Heavenly Profound Mirror did not have any impact on its actual operations.

They simply appeared and then settled in the deepest recesses of the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"No wonder the Mirror Holders value it so highly."

"Isn't this equivalent to a Mind Reading technique specialized for the Heavenly Profound Mirror?"

"Even if it can only read fragmented pieces due to damage, any single piece is priceless!"

The Heavenly Profound Mirror, as a genuine immortal artifact and the cornerstone of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's operation.

Looking down from a high vantage point.

Its judgments were absolutely correct and far ahead of the cultivators within it.

Li Fan recalled the previous life, where the Heavenly Profound Mirror joined forces with Mo Rubbin to scheme against him several times.

A dangerous glint appeared in his eyes.

Chapter 1161: Pointing the Sword at the Fishing Pond

The Sword Points to the Fishing Pond

Having suffered such a significant loss at the hands of Mo Rubbin and the Heavenly Profound Mirror, it was impossible for Li Fan not to harbor any thoughts of revenge.

However, Mo Rubbin, as one of the Dharma Kings of the Profound Heaven Sect, possessed an unfathomable ability. He could infiltrate the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters as if entering an empty realm.

Although he later died inexplicably in the Netherworld, Li Fan currently did not have a hundred percent certainty of subduing him.

Without fundamental conflicts of interest, Li Fan had no intention of provoking him in this lifetime for now.

"Perhaps I can secretly study how the Myriad Immortals Alliance dealt with this Profound Heaven Sect Dharma King."

According to the normal trajectory of history, Mo Rubbin would have been discovered by the Myriad Immortals Alliance without having awakened.

Perhaps there were still some special methods within the Myriad Immortals Alliance to deal with members of the Profound Heaven Sect. With preemptive action, Mo Rubbin might indeed have lost his power to resist.

At that time, Li Fan could simply copy their methods and deal with Mo Rubbin in this way lifetime after lifetime.

But if Mo Rubbin, like in the 119th iteration, was only pretending to be subdued while actually seizing the opportunity to infiltrate...

Then, without finding a definitive method to deal with him, Li Fan would not intentionally make an enemy of Mo Rubbin.

As for the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Carrying one origin of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, he was already in an invincible position.

Now, he had also grasped a method to spy into its interior...

"If Heaven gives an opportunity and one does not take it, one will suffer the consequences!"

Li Fan's thoughts raced, and he transformed into a streak of illusory light, entering the Boundless Mirror.

Internally, he continued to construct arrays, stabilizing his control.

While waiting for Sun Luoyuan to return to the secret chamber, he also studied the traces of the immortal-level formations remaining in the Boundless Mirror.

...

Great Qi, Holy Capital.

During this period, as Wang Xuanba tirelessly travelled across various parts of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Besides Yin Shangren, Ou Daozi and his son, Ximen Yu, and others chosen as "Stars of Xuanhuang" by Li Ping, had all been "fooled" into the Holy Dynasty Great Qi by Wang Xuanba using plausible rhetoric from the Holy Emperor.

Of course, not everyone on this list was persuaded. Some not only refused the invitation but some even killed Wang Xuanba's divine sense clone.

Wang Xuanba was not angered. He simply recorded their names and reported them to the Holy Emperor.

Then, he skipped them and invited the next person.

After the Xuanhuang Stars arrived in Great Qi, under Li Ping's personal reception, they all, like Yin Shangren, settled down in the Holy Dynasty from then on.

They found their respective pursuits.

For example, Ximen Yu, Li Ping promised to help him delve deeper into the research of earth vein power, and even revealed some important information related to the ancient earth vein trees.

For example, Ou Daozi would be responsible for the construction of the new Holy Capital of Great Qi. In the future, every conquered small world of the Holy Dynasty would have Ou Daozi as the chief planner for overall remodeling.

More importantly, Li Ping immediately saw that Ou Shangtian possessed the 'Kun Gan Bone Hand' and 'Ten Thousand Deaths Record,' two rare treasures. He then accepted Ou Shangtian as his personal disciple.

From Li Ping, Ou Shangtian did not feel the slightest ill will.

Moreover, the interesting immortal cultivation world secrets and profound Dao principles that the Holy Emperor spoke of deeply attracted the young Ou Shangtian.

Thus, he willingly became his disciple.

In life, one sought fame, profit, and peace of mind.

All of these, Holy Emperor Li Ping could satisfy them.

As for those who did not respond to the summons...

Their fate had already been decided in Li Ping's heart.

Beneath the Holy Emperor's Seat.

Deeper than Yin Shangren's underground secret chamber.

A secret intelligence agency of the Holy Dynasty called the 'Sky Supervision Department' had been gradually established.

As the central node of the 'Grand Formation of All Spirits,' under the shroud of the formation, all affairs within the small world could be observed clearly.

When the Holy Dynasty eventually commenced its campaign of conquest and incorporated other small worlds into its territory, they would also be strictly monitored by the Sky Supervision Department.

Not only that.

In Li Ping's vision, the name "Sky Supervision" was not just for those small worlds.

Even the main Xuanhuang Realm would be included.

With the 'Paper Figures of the Tribulation Crossing Sect' and the 'Heavenly Profound Mirror' as foundations, building a comprehensive intelligence system was not a difficult task.

The hidden agents of the Sky Supervision Department would be personally selected by Li Ping.

The influence of the heavenly change "Heaven Opens Its Favor, Stars Descend to the World" on the Great Qi small world had initially manifested. Recently, among the infants born in the Holy Dynasty, there were not a few who exhibited innate extraordinary abilities.

Holy Medicine Institutes were established everywhere. Li Ping could immediately sense the physique of all infants upon their birth.

From a young age, they would receive Li Ping's personal training. When they grew up, they would either go to the Sky Supervision Department or participate in Yin Shangren's New Dharma deduction plan...

Making the best use of everything.

The growth of talent, or indeed empires, required time.

The Great Qi Holy Dynasty was developing at an unprecedented speed, but at present, the most attention-grabbing event in the Holy Dynasty was a grand competition.

A fishing competition.

Organized by direct order of the Holy Emperor, anyone in the country interested could participate, regardless of prior fishing experience.

Regional winners would be selected first, and then proceed to the Holy Capital for the final competition.

At that time, the Holy Emperor would also appear to enjoy the festivities with the common people.

The top one hundred contestants in the competition would receive generous rewards, enough to ensure a common family's lifelong financial security.

And for those who performed exceptionally well in the competition, it was rumored that there would be additional unique rewards from the Holy Emperor.

The news had been released for half a month, and the response was overwhelming.

If not for the assistance of immortal masters from the Holy Dynasty in various regions, the fish in all the rivers and lakes would likely have been caught, leading to an awkward situation where there would be nothing left to fish.

In addition to ordinary citizens, the Holy Emperor's disciples would also participate in the competition.

This undoubtedly further stimulated people's enthusiasm.

As is widely known, the Holy Emperor had publicly stated more than once that he had no descendants now and would not have any in the future.

The Holy Emperor had no heirs.

His disciples were undoubtedly the successors of the Holy Dynasty.

If one could be favored by the Holy Emperor in the fishing competition and taken as a personal disciple...

The leap of the carp through the dragon gate was imminent!

Under the incentive of various rumors, the current common people in Great Qi had even reached a point of near-madness for "fishing."

It was even considered more important than studying or cultivating.

And all of this, Li Ping naturally observed.

The reason he allowed and even encouraged it was naturally for the sake of the treasure, the Fishing Pond.

This immortal artifact, or even an existence surpassing the Xuanhuang Realm.

It contained countless opportunities.

Perhaps his method of breaking through the predicament was hidden within.

He would certainly not miss an opportunity to obtain divine objects without any cost.

Even casually fishing out a secret treasure from it could greatly increase the Holy Dynasty's combat power.

Chapter 1162: New Xuanhuang World

New Xuanhuang Realm

The probability of catching treasures of quality from the Fishing Pond is not related to the level of cultivation.

It depends more on the sincerity of the fishing and the understanding of the Great Dao of [Fishing].

In fact, the more one desires something specific, the lower the possibility of catching the intended target.

In short, it is mysterious and profound, much like ordinary fishing.

Winners of the Sacred Dynasty's fishing competition will be arranged to fish in the Fishing Pond.

Most of these people are only at the Qi Refining stage, with the highest being at the Nascent Soul realm.

With their limited knowledge and experience, they would never imagine that this seemingly ordinary pond is an immortal artifact, capable of yielding world-class treasures.

Whatever they gain, they will naturally attribute it to the great Holy Emperor's blessings.

Furthermore, there is no need to worry about someone like Senior Stone Slab from the 119th lifetime, who foolishly attempted to comprehend the Great Dao of Fishing by leveraging the Fishing Pond, thus provoking the reaction of the nameless True Immortal behind it and being "fished away" himself.

When treasures are caught from the Fishing Pond, except for a very few exceptional cases, Li Ping will be tempted. For the rest, he will allow the fishermen themselves to use them. He might even focus on cultivating them.

"In this lifetime, let me see if the treasures within the Fishing Pond are truly endless. And..."

"Can the Fortune of All Heavens truly overpower Xuanhuang!"

Gazing at the tens of thousands of eager fishermen in the Holy Capital, each holding various fishing rods, Li Ping seemed to see countless supreme treasures of the starry sky flying into the Sacred Dynasty.

Just as the Sacred Dynasty's fishing competition was being meticulously organized.

In the desolate small mountain on the northwestern frontier of Yongyun Prefecture.

In the dilapidated temple on the mountaintop, Zhong Shentong, who had cast his line but returned empty-handed, suddenly felt a wave of fatigue.

Just as he was about to call for his Dao companion, Liuli, he discovered that she had also fallen into a deep slumber.

Zhong Shentong smiled faintly. After checking the temple's protective formation to ensure everything was in order.

He then lazily reclined on his lounge chair for a nap.

After an unknown period of time...

When he inexplicably woke up, he found himself in a dark, unknown space!

Instinctively, he reached for his most prized protective treasure in his storage ring, only to discover that he had been stripped bare, completely naked!

Zhong Shentong's face twitched. He knew he was utterly defeated this time. His captor was too ruthless, giving him no chance at all.

"But since I'm still alive, it means the other party doesn't intend to kill me. On the surface, I'm just a Qi Refining cultivator nearing the end of my lifespan, in dire straits. It would be too much trouble to deal with me. So, it must be about the Fishing Pond?"

Zhong Shentong's thoughts raced, and he instantly understood. But no matter how hard he racked his brain, he couldn't figure out how the news of this supreme treasure had leaked.

There was no forewarning at all!

"Right, where's Liuli?"

Regarding this little girl he had personally fished out of the Fishing Pond and who had taken human form, Zhong Shentong had already come to regard her as his only family. Now that he was imprisoned, she was likely in grave danger as well...

Just as Zhong Shentong's mind was in turmoil, a chilling voice echoed in the darkness of the space.

"Break through to the Foundation Establishment stage within seven days."

"Otherwise, you die!"

There was no intention of conversing with Zhong Shentong. After saying these two sentences, there was no further sound.

However, the palpable, chilling killing intent surrounding him made Zhong Shentong understand that this was not a mere test.

If he failed to break through, he would truly be killed! "I have been stagnant at the late stage of Qi Refining for more than fifty years. On the surface, I appear to be on my last legs, with no hope of breakthrough. Anyone with a normal mind wouldn't make such a demand of me. Unless..."

"He guessed that I cultivate the [Life and Death Profound Manual]!"

The more he thought, the more Zhong Shentong felt the unfathomable nature of this mastermind. He had never met them before, yet they seemed to know everything about him.

...

Just as Zhong Shentong was immersed in boundless dread.

In another dark space, the Dao companion Liuli seemed oblivious to the impending crisis, still fast asleep.

Li Ping suddenly appeared before her, quietly observing her.

After a long pause, Li Ping said faintly, "Fellow Daoist Baihua, please reveal yourself."

Silence. No response.

Li Ping narrowed his eyes, "Must I say it a third time? Sect Master of the Tianlian Sect from the Wansheng Realm!"

His tone was light, but to certain ears, it was like thunder.

Finally, she could no longer hide. Golden light flashed, and a figure emerged from Dao companion Liuli.

Baihua Daoist stared intently at Li Ping, "Who on earth are you?"

She had certainly never seen the person before her. Yet, he could accurately state her identity...

In an instant, countless figures flashed through Baihua's mind, but none matched.

"We are merely fellow wanderers of the stars, having lost our homeland. What has passed is past; why must Fellow Daoist delve deeper?"

One sentence made Baihua Daoist's imagination run wild, as if recalling the terrifying moments of successive world-destroying catastrophes in the past.

"More importantly, it is the future." The next sentence that came from him completely captured Baihua's attention.

"The future?"

"Currently, only this place remains as a sanctuary in the lost sea of stars. But the Xuanhuang Realm of today is no longer the Xuanhuang Realm of the past. Over these years, through the continuous piecing together and integration of fragments from various realms, this New Xuanhuang Realm has long transcended the concept of an ordinary immortal cultivation world. Li Ping's tone was melancholic.

"If Fellow Daoist searches carefully, perhaps you can still find fragments of the Wansheng Realm from the past."

Baihua's expression changed, "What exactly does Fellow Daoist want to say?"

"Since Xuanhuang Realm has absorbed fragments from our worlds... then the New Xuanhuang Realm should also have a place for us. If they do not permit it, then we must fight for it ourselves." Li Ping said proudly.

"The native forces of the Xuanhuang Realm are too powerful. Only by uniting can we hope to reclaim what is ours."

"Besides the Wansheng Realm, I have also found Fellow Daoists from the Tianji Realm..." Li Ping spoke eloquently.

Baihua Daoist clearly seemed swayed.

"If the Xuanhuang Realm has indeed absorbed fragments of our world to resist the Immortal Ruins, then this place can indeed be considered my new home."

A tremor of emotion suddenly surged in Baihua's heart, an irrepressible feeling of finding a new sanctuary after years of wandering and rootlessness.

"But... the cultivators of Xuanhuang Realm are not easy to deal with." After contemplating, Baihua Daoist still hesitated. She vaguely recalled the scene from back then, where a lone Loose Immortal had blocked all of them, the survivors from various realms, from entering.

Although times had changed and that Loose Immortal had also disappeared, Xuanhuang Realm had now produced a new Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate...

Could they, as outsiders, truly fare well under His hand?

Chapter 1163: Three Words Deter Longevity

Three Words Deter Longevity

Li Ping seemed to see through Baihua Daoist's concerns. He said in a deep voice, "The Myriad Immortals Alliance's Five Elders Council is indeed powerful, but we are not the only ones dissatisfied with their rule in the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Not to mention the various factions hidden in the small worlds, there are countless individuals within the Myriad Immortals Alliance with ulterior motives."

Li Ping waved his hand. A vast web of relationships suddenly unfolded before Baihua Daoist.

Baihua Daoist gazed intently. Those faces were clearly members of various organizations within the Myriad Immortals Alliance!

Not only their names and appearances. But also their life stories, personalities, the likelihood of them being recruited, and predictions of their future behavior, etc. Everything, in meticulous detail, was listed.

And those who were specially marked were the unstable factors within the Myriad Immortals Alliance, staff who could easily be swayed.

Looking at these words and images, the Myriad Immortals Alliance was no longer just a hollow name in Baihua Daoist's mind. It instantly took on a vivid form.

The more Baihua Daoist looked, the more her heart pounded: "No wonder this person dares to make such grand pronouncements, confident of fighting the Myriad Immortals Alliance. With such detailed information, how long would it take to collect it? Not to mention the time, some secrets would likely require insiders holding high positions to obtain."

Baihua Daoist did not believe that all of this was fabricated by him. The information was too detailed, making the possibility of forgery very low.

She wanted to examine further, but Li Ping waved his hand again, and the light screen before them changed.

This time, the information shifted from the Myriad Immortals Alliance to the smaller worlds within the Xuanhuang Realm. Those who were powerful and could cooperate, those who were not strong but resource-rich and could be conquered as production bases. Even those that were extremely dangerous and not recommended for contact...

A hidden scroll of the Xuanhuang Realm slowly unrolled before Baihua Daoist.

While shocked, Baihua Daoist also felt a sense of helplessness. Having been forced to see so many secrets of the Sacred Dynasty, she now had no choice but to join.

As for tearing up their relationship and fighting him head-on...

Even though Baihua Daoist was a Longevity Realm existence in her original world, facing this Faceless Holy Emperor, she did not have complete confidence. In fact, every time she contemplated opposing him, she would instinctively feel a premonition of utter ruin.

This had never happened before. Even when she was captured by the Fishing Pond, she had not felt such a sense of crisis.

Therefore, when Li Ping calmly invited her to join the Sacred Dynasty, Baihua Daoist agreed without hesitation.

Li Ping burst into laughter, "Excellent, excellent! With Fellow Daoist Baihua's assistance, our chances of success will increase by a further point."

"There is one matter that requires Fellow Daoist's help." Incredibly, as soon as Baihua joined, Li Ping impatiently assigned her a task.

The miniature map before them suddenly shrunk, finally focusing on a small world with five interlocked rings.

"This Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, I intend to designate it as the final prize for this fishing competition. However, it is currently within the Heavenly Spirit Prefecture of the Immortal Alliance. The border areas are prone to detection by the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Council. Therefore..."

Li Ping's tone was quite sincere: "I will have to trouble Fellow Daoist to move it to the vicinity of the void surrounding my Great Qi."

At first, Baihua Daoist thought it was an ordinary grotto-heaven and didn't pay much attention. But when Li Ping transmitted the specific information about the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, Baihua's golden body couldn't help but tremble.

These five interconnected grotto-heavens were too enormous! With her strength, she could indeed barely move them. But afterwards, she would absolutely be severely drained.

Would he take advantage of her weakened state to plot against her?

At this moment, Li Ping smiled, "It is truly that I cannot extricate myself, and thus I am forced to trouble Fellow Daoist."

"If I truly intended to deal with Fellow Daoist, why would I need any plots or schemes..."

Li Ping's tone was devoid of any fluctuation, as if he were simply stating a simple fact.

As Li Ping spoke, several stone puppets quietly appeared in the void, subtly surrounding Baihua Daoist.

These puppets were not very powerful in themselves, but the fluctuations emanating from them made Baihua feel both familiar and terrified.

A flash of light illuminated Baihua's mind, and she instantly found the source of this familiarity from her memories. It was the terrifying calamities that had swept through and annihilated countless immortal cultivation worlds long ago!

"Are you insane?!" Baihua Daoist couldn't help but scream. Her body instinctively recoiled rapidly away from these stone puppets.

"You are playing with fire! How can we control the power of world-destroying catastrophes? If there is the slightest mistake, this Xuanhuang Realm, our last sanctuary, might be destroyed by you!" Baihua Daoist's body trembled, a mixture of shock and anger.

She never imagined that this so-called fellow traveler would be a complete madman. No wonder she had felt an indescribable sense of crisis from him earlier...

Facing Baihua Daoist's accusations, Li Ping remained indifferent.

He snorted, and said coldly, "World-destroying calamities have only temporarily disappeared. Who can guarantee they won't reappear in the future? Even if we are fortunate enough to escape the Immortal Ruins, what about other calamities we might encounter later?"

"Blindly evading will ultimately lead to extinction. Only by actively studying and mastering their power can we achieve true freedom!" Li Ping's tone was extremely firm, even tinged with a hint of fanaticism.

He waved his hand again, and three complex yet sacred-looking twisted symbols appeared beside him.

They rotated around Li Ping.

They contained no power, yet their mere shapes made the Longevity Realm Baihua Daoist tremble.

And Li Ping, the Faceless Holy Emperor, surrounded by the three profound symbols, exuded an aura of both sanctity and malevolence.

Making it impossible to look directly at him.

"Hehehe, these three True Immortal runes were painstakingly collected by me from the void. Does Fellow Daoist not wish to observe them?" Li Ping's voice boomed, resounding throughout the dark space.

Baihua Daoist sensed that the Dao companion Liuli was showing signs of waking up and quickly cast a spell to make her fall asleep again.

As for herself, she truly dared not look directly at those three True Immortal runes!

Yes, True Immortal runes indeed contained infinite power. But could cultivators like them, who had not yet ascended to immortality, truly control such power that transcended the mortal realm?

She had personally witnessed countless cultivators turn to dust under such power, with no ability to resist. This included even Longevity Realm existences like herself.

In her view, studying True Immortal runes was akin to a child holding a world-destroying artifact.

With the slightest mishap, not only would they instantly perish, but the entire world might be dragged down to destruction with them!

She still had many years left to live, so why would she engage in such extreme behavior!

Chapter 1164: Heaven and Earth Overturned with One Hand

With a Single Hand, Reshaping the World

Baihua Daoist turned her head away, trembling and unwilling to respond.

Li Ping waited for a long time, but still did not receive Baihua's change of heart. He sighed slightly and put away the three True Immortal runes beside him.

"Fine, if Fellow Daoist is unwilling, I shall not force you."

"After all, not everyone has the courage to utilize the power of True Immortals..."

"Are there any difficulties regarding the relocation of the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven? Li Ping returned to the main topic and asked.

Feeling the terrifying power fluctuations around her disappear, Baihua Daoist briefly recovered from her panic.

Li Ping's tone in asking seemed subtly different from before. Baihua knew that if she refused again, she would truly anger this madman. She could only reluctantly agree.

"Fellow Daoist, please set off as soon as possible. By the way, this place is unfamiliar to you, and for the sake of caution, I will send a disciple to accompany you." Li Ping said intentionally or unintentionally.

When Baihua Daoist saw Li Ping's so-called disciple, her scalp went numb, and her body trembled again.

"This is..."

Even though Baihua had extraordinary knowledge and had witnessed the scenes of worlds being destroyed, she was still somewhat unable to accept it at this moment: the body, which appeared identical to an ordinary human, was in reality composed of countless writhing, unknown small insects. Each of these insects was an individual with its own thoughts, yet they collectively formed a unified "human" community.

Baihua Daoist's scalp tingled, not because of the hideous insects, but due to her body's instinctive reaction.

Those insects seemed to have some natural antagonism towards bodies composed purely of energy.

Even though she was in the Longevity Realm, and even though she was still some distance away from these insects, Baihua still felt a sudden surge of restlessness and unease within her, a constant alarm urging her to stay away from this "insect person."

"You can call him [Dao Yi]." Li Ping answered her unspoken question.

"Don't worry, although Dao Yi's strength is somewhat lacking, he possesses some peculiar abilities. With his help, moving the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven should be much easier for Fellow Daoist."

Seeing this, Baihua Daoist could only brace herself and nod slightly. Led by Dao Yi, they headed directly towards the Heavenly Spirit Prefecture.

Li Ping watched their departing figures, but his heart did not hold much joy at having subdued a Longevity Realm existence with a few words.

"It's still due to insufficient personal strength. I can only rely on external threats to intimidate. If I could unleash the essence of Origin Force, why would I need all this trouble?"

Dao Yi is a special variant of the Dao Yi insects preserved within the Myriad Beast Condensation Crystal.

No matter how their numbers swell, they can always maintain a collective tribal consciousness. More importantly, this Dao Yi insect does not merely produce spiritual energy.

Instead, it can seemingly inhabit spiritual energy, propagate itself using spiritual energy, and then gradually transform itself into a form of spiritual energy.

Given sufficient external conditions for reproduction, [Dao Yi] only needs about a year to transform all the spiritual energy in a small world into "itself."

The entire process is silent and will not affect the various creatures living on spiritual energy in the world.

Even cultivators of weaker cultivation levels cannot perceive it.

Only when one reaches the Nascent Soul stage and forms their own separate grotto-heaven can they sense this mutated spiritual energy.

Li Fan sent [Dao Yi], cultivated with a wisp of his consciousness, into the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, intending for it to undergo a higher-level transformation there.

With the vast amount of spiritual energy within the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, it would be able to cultivate a large quantity of mutated spiritual energy capable of shaking the entire Xuanhuang Realm.

Under normal circumstances, Dao Yi would not be able to develop in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Once the mutation of spiritual energy exceeded a certain scale, it would inevitably alert cultivators and be reported to the Immortal Alliance.

Although it would be troublesome to deal with, destroying these insects was not a difficult task for the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

However, there was a reaction time required from discovery to resolution.

If there was a sufficient quantity, it could achieve a wholesale blood change of the Xuanhuang spiritual energy before the cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm could react.

This move, to undermine the foundation, was a killer move Li Ping prepared for counterattacking the Xuanhuang Realm.

When spiritual energy possesses self-awareness and can distinguish friend from foe.

The cultivators of the United Worlds Association would likely have a significant advantage when fighting against the cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, not just a little.

"Dare to change the sun and moon for a new sky."

"The aura of this Xuanhuang Realm is too decadent. It's time to teach them a harsh lesson."

As a clone of Li Fan, Holy Emperor Li Ping was stripped of memories related to "Returning to Truth."

In his core understanding, he was an emergent entity born from the Xuanhuang Realm's desire for self-salvation amidst the world-ending crisis, a product of chance.

The so-called Heavenly Mandate Sage.

He knew all the secrets of the Xuanhuang Realm like the back of his hand.

He had even foreseen countless destructive futures for himself.

His ultimate pursuit was to change the heavens and earth, to liberate the Xuanhuang Realm from the corrupt rule of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

Holy Emperor Li Ping firmly believed that he was not too far from achieving this goal.

...

The Great Qi's first Grand Fishing Competition finals officially commenced.

Ten outstanding individuals would personally demonstrate their fishing skills before the Holy Emperor.

Originally, three of the Holy Emperor's disciples were competing, but ultimately only Wang Xuanba, with his simple and honest nature, advanced to the final round.

This undoubtedly further proved the fairness of the competition.

Passing through a circular gate of light, after a wave of dizziness, these ten contestants arrived in what appeared to be a very ordinary garden.

The magnificent Faceless Holy Emperor sat by a small pond not far away, fishing with his eyes closed.

The vast majority of the ten people were seeing the Holy Emperor's face for the first time. Not daring to disturb him, they lowered their heads and waited nervously.

After a long while, the Holy Emperor suddenly reeled in his line.

To their surprise, what was pulled from the pond was not a fish.

But a white ball of light.

Casually putting the ball of light away, the Holy Emperor looked at the ten outstanding fishermen and explained the competition rules.

"In this pond, I have placed countless treasures."

"One person, one rod, one chance."

"The higher the quality of the treasure fished out, the better the score."

...

His words filled everyone with excitement.

Because the Holy Emperor had promised that regardless of their ranking, all the treasures they fished out would belong to them!

As they eagerly prepared to start, Wang Xuanba, the Holy Emperor's disciple, made the first move.

Wang Xuanba had never been to the Fishing Pond before.

He sat down, dazed for a long time, and then reeled in his line.

In the end, his hand was empty.

An empty rod!

This made Wang Xuanba quite dejected.

Seeing this, the others were all deeply shaken, knowing that the Holy Emperor's fishing trial was not as simple as ordinary fishing. One by one, they became tense and serious.

As they took their turns approaching the Fishing Pond, eventually, one purple, three blue, and five white balls of light were fished out.

There is another chapter due around 12:30.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1165: Madman Grinds His Saber at Night

The Madman Sharpens His Blade at Night

Li Ping examined the light orbs and confirmed they were of no great use to him.

He then solemnly handed the light orbs back to these carefully selected fishermen.

The first attempt yielded no significant gains.

Li Ping was unconcerned.

The fishing competition was organized in a hurry, leaving little preparation time for the Great Qi populace. These winners were all seasoned fishermen, their success relying more on experience than on comprehension or talent.

"With them as examples, igniting the people's great enthusiasm, I believe the second and third fishing competitions should bring me some surprises."

Li Ping watched the winners meticulously examine the light orbs they held, nodding slightly before his form shattered and disappeared.

After all, fighting on Xuanhuang Realm was not a home advantage. Without the continuous support of the Sacred Dynasty's destiny, Li Ping might not even be a match for ordinary Harmonious Dao cultivators.

It was best to return quickly.

If it weren't for the fact that the supreme treasure, the Fishing Pond, could not be moved, he wouldn't have risked coming here himself.

"Still not enough manpower."

"Trustworthy subordinates with sufficient strength are truly too few."

Li Ping sighed faintly and then pondered a solution.

...

Tianquan Prefecture.

Sun Family's Secret Chamber.

More than a month had passed since Sun Luyuan's departure last time.

According to his previous habit, Sun Luyuan should have returned long ago to nourish the Boundless Mirror with his blood.

But for some unknown reason, Sun Luyuan had not returned.

On this day, Li Fan's divine sense, which was engrossed in studying the residual arrays of the Boundless Mirror, suddenly detected signs of the secret chamber's defenses being tampered with.

Upon investigation, he couldn't help but chuckle.

It turned out that Wu Ninglu, through some unknown method, had indeed discovered the entrance to the underground secret chamber.

She was currently attempting to infiltrate the chamber.

Although she had used a secret method to disguise her aura, how could she escape Li Fan's keen observation?

The divine sense clone quietly flew out of the Boundless Mirror and pointed a finger.

The secret chamber's protective formation instantly changed.

Striking the suddenly strengthened formation mercilessly, Wu Ninglu's expression shifted, knowing she had been exposed.

Without daring to linger, she transformed into a black light and fled.

Li Fan watched closely. After circling around, Wu Ninglu removed her disguise in a secluded spot.

Then, she brazenly returned to her own room.

She was still harboring a flinch of hope, not immediately fleeing the Sun family.

"Heh heh, is she truly stupid, or is she brazenly relying on the fact that she carries Sun family blood?"

"But it has nothing to do with me. I believe that when Sun Luyuan returns, I will be able to control the Boundless Mirror and meet with that Mirror Holder [Fu]."

Li Fan's prediction was not wrong.

Seven days later, Sun Luyuan arrived at the underground secret chamber with a grave expression.

He had also discovered signs of an outsider's intrusion into the protective formation, and his expression changed.

His mood was unpredictable. Ultimately, Sun Luyuan did not make a sound.

Instead, he first placed a ball of vital blood in front of the black mirror.

Li Fan felt a trace of uncontrollable desire from Sun Luoyao, the mirror spirit.

He snorted coldly, forcefully suppressing its instincts.

This was because the Boundless Mirror had already been refined by him. The sacrifice of Sun family bloodlines would only shake his control over the Boundless Mirror.

How could he let them have their way?

However, to avoid revealing any flaws, he still had Sun Luoyao put on a show.

After "swallowing" the vital blood, Sun Luoyao slowly appeared.

"Brother, I'm much better." He said against his will.

Regarding deceiving his elder brother, Sun Luoyao felt immense guilt. But as a spirit artifact, he was beyond his control. He couldn't even warn Sun Luyuan, who was closest to him.

He could only watch helplessly as his elder brother stepped further into this terrifying existence's trap.

"The old man's demands are becoming increasingly excessive. Clearly, we just provided him with important information not long ago, yet he is still not satisfied," Sun Luyuan said, looking at Sun Luoyao's faint figure with a flicker of tenderness in his eyes, then speaking with hatred.

"This time, his demands are even more outrageous, asking us to spy on the Human Clone of the Heavenly Profound Mirror? Based on a mere unrealistic speculation, he wants us to keep trying at the cost of our blood..."

"Old thief!"

Sun Luyuan punched the ground fiercely.

In the eyes of outsiders, he was the illustrious Patriarch of the Sun family, holding a high position in the Law Enforcement Hall, influential and powerful.

But before the true powers of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, he was less than a dog!

For the survival of the entire Sun family, he had to grovel without dignity.

"Why do the Dharma Transmitters and Mirror Holders always remain high and mighty? And no matter how hard we try, we can only be their dogs!"

"Is there no hope of turning the tables?!"

A surge of suppressed frustration could not be vented. A thought that Sun Luyuan had never dared to consider before suddenly emerged in his mind.

But he quickly reacted.

He was so startled by his own thought that he hurriedly suppressed it deep within his mind, not daring to reveal even a sliver of it, even to his closest brother, who had become a spirit artifact.

Because he deeply understood that if the rulers of the Immortal Alliance learned of his thoughts, the next day, there would be no trace of the Sun family left in the entire Immortal Alliance. They would be utterly erased from existence!

However, he seemed to have underestimated the effect of brotherhood.

"Brother, when I was spying on the Heavenly Profound Mirror last time, I actually discovered something interesting." Sun Luoyao suddenly said.

"Hmm?" Sun Luyuan was slightly stunned, looking at his brother's very serious expression.

"Through various clues, the Heavenly Profound Mirror has discovered traces of a faction within the Xuanhuang Realm that is currently in hiding and might rebel in the future," Sun Luoyao whispered.

"Rebellion?" Sun Luyuan shook his head. He didn't believe anything in the vast Xuanhuang Realm could shake the rule of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

But the following words from his brother, Junior Brother, made his heart skip a beat. "According to the Heavenly Profound Mirror's prediction, this faction might cause considerable damage to the Myriad Immortals Alliance."

"Is this true?"

Sun Luyuan's spirits lifted. The first thought that flashed through his mind was to immediately report this weighty news to Mirror Holder Fu to earn merit.

However, as he carefully read through all the information transmitted by his brother, his heart filled with shock.

Sun Luoyao's soft voice echoed in his ears.

"Brother, I am truly in so much pain."

"If this continues, I estimate I won't be able to hold on much longer and will be annihilated, body and soul."

"Being a dog for a lifetime is still being a dog."

"Even mortals dare to shout 'The emperor takes turns, this year it's my house'..."

His brother's soft murmurs, like soul-stirring demonic chants, circled Sun Luyuan's ears.

The thought that he had previously suppressed in his mind, influenced by these words, could no longer be contained and resurfaced.

"Sacred Dynasty Great Qi..."

Sun Luyuan narrowed his eyes, reconsidering the information he held.

"A dynasty created by mortals banished to a small world. There might be intervention from unknown powerful beings behind it. Its speed of civilizational development is completely abnormal."

"It might be related to those who fled the Xuanhuang Realm before the Great Calamity, from the Ten Immortal Sects."

"Based on preliminary judgments, it is not impossible that important members within the Immortal Alliance have already been infiltrated by it."

...

Sun Luyuan carefully read these fragmented texts, his brows furrowed.

This Sacred Dynasty Great Qi was extremely mysterious. Its specific location within a small world was still unknown. The Heavenly Profound Mirror had only judged its general strength based on the activities of its personnel within the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Unfortunately, we couldn't capture the complete inference basis of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, only scattered fragments of information."

Sun Luyuan couldn't help but feel regret.

However, Sun Luyuan had great faith in the Heavenly Profound Mirror's judgments.

As the foundation of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's operation, the Heavenly Profound Mirror continuously received an unimaginable amount of data. If it were a cultivator, even a Longevity Realm existence, attempting to process so much data simultaneously would likely lead to sluggishness. But the Heavenly Profound Mirror not only handled everything flawlessly but could also make certain predictions about the future based on the current information.

However, regarding these "unforeseen events," besides knowing them himself, the Heavenly Profound Mirror could not offer any suggestions or take any action.

Sun Luyuan was initially very confused about this matter.

However, during a conversation with Mirror Holder Fu, he finally understood the mystery.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance is governed by humans, not by mirrors. No matter how miraculous it is, it is still just an object. If it could make various decisions without our consent, where would that leave us? If this precedent is set, wouldn't the Myriad Immortals Alliance fall into chaos?"

"As for why even its judgments cannot be fully trusted..."

Mirror Holder Fu pondered for a long time, then said in a low voice, "No major turmoil will occur in the Xuanhuang Realm. No matter what happens, it cannot shake the positions of us who are in power."

"The Heavenly Profound Mirror's judgments are purely rational inferences. A long time ago, we also attempted to utilize more of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's abilities to better manage the Myriad Immortals Alliance. However..."

Mirror Holder Fu paused, "Heh heh, it actually made suggestions directed at us."

"It's better to honestly remain an [object]."

Sun Luyuan understood that the actual rulers of the Immortal Alliance would never allow the Heavenly Profound Mirror to stand above them. They wanted to maintain absolute control of power. Moreover, the Heavenly Profound Mirror was ultimately an object, and whether it could be fully trusted was still unknown.

After much deliberation, Sun Luyuan's initially restless heart calmed down again.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance has ruled for so many years, its foundation is deeply entrenched, and its heritage is unimaginably profound. With Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate suppressing everything, how could it be so easily shaken?" Sun Luyuan thought, finding his own nascent idea unbelievable.

"However, nothing is absolute."

Recalling various scenes he had witnessed during the daily operations of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, his confidence was implicitly undermined.

"Let's observe for now. Sacred Dynasty Great Qi..."

"If it can truly gain momentum, then I will make a decision. It won't be too late."

After all, as the patriarch, his every move affected the lives and well-being of hundreds of people, requiring extreme caution.

Deeply suppressing the relevant information in his mind, Sun Luyuan then began to concern himself with his brother's condition.

His brother's painful performance just now had truly worried Sun Luyuan.

And at this moment, Sun Luoyao seemed to have slowly recovered from the endless torment.

"Brother, I'm fine. For you, for the Sun family, I can still hold on for a while longer," Sun Luoyao said with a tragic smile.

Sun Luyuan's heart trembled. Despite having a thousand words to say, they all turned into silence as they reached his lips.

"Oh, right, Brother. You mentioned earlier that Lord Fu's task this time is to find the human clone of the Heavenly Profound Mirror? What's going on?"

There was a long silence in the underground secret chamber. Finally, it was Sun Luoyao who broke the silence.

Sun Luyuan then began to explain, "Lord Fu discovered that another Mirror Holder, Cang, seems to be plotting something in secret. Cang, among the Mirror Holders, belongs to the radical faction and has always advocated for stricter restrictions on the Heavenly Profound Mirror. But recently, his attitude has become somewhat wavering."

"Lord Fu suspects that Cang's abnormality might be related to the Heavenly Profound Mirror's clone."

Sun Luoyao seemed somewhat confused, "...How was this deduced?"

Sun Luyuan shook his head, "I don't know about that. Perhaps Lord Fu knows something more that he didn't explain to me."

"Although it's just a baseless speculation, since he has issued the order, we must complete it."

"Fortunately, he also knows that this matter is extremely difficult, so he hasn't been too demanding."

Sun Luyuan snorted coldly.

Then he looked at Sun Luoyao, "It's just that you will have to suffer again."

Sun Luoyao did not reply.

A moment later, he said silently, "Let's begin. While my condition is still good."

Sun Luyuan's expression was complex. He nodded, then took out a small Heavenly Profound Mirror from his embrace.

Facing the Boundless Black Mirror,

An invisible force instantly descended upon the underground secret chamber, as if a passage had formed between the two mirrors. Countless images, mixed with strands of green light, were drawn through the passage into the Boundless Black Mirror.

Sun Luoyao's vague figure began to become unstable.

His gaze towards the Heavenly Profound Mirror revealed an irrepressible greed. However, in a flash, he forcibly suppressed this greed.

As his expression constantly shifted, more and more information was absorbed by the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Sun Luyuan nervously monitored the changes in the scene.

Seeing that the time was about the same as before, he intended to put away the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"Brother, wait a moment longer!"

Sun Luyuan hesitated.

Because the longer the duration of spying on the Heavenly Profound Mirror, the higher the possibility of being discovered by it. Multiple attempts were safer than one long one.

But in the next moment, Sun Luoyao's words made his heart tremble.

"The human clone, it's true!"

"Brother, give me some more time! I've found some clues!"

Unexpectedly, this time it was so smooth, making Sun Luyuan ecstatic.

However, he then thought to himself, could this be an excuse created by his brother to swallow more himself?

After all, he had done such things before.

"Trust me, brother!"

The telepathic connection between the brothers made Sun Luoyao speak proactively, dispelling Sun Luyuan's doubts.

Sun Luyuan gritted his teeth and ultimately did not put away the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

There is another chapter due in about twenty minutes.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1166: Mirror People Encounter and Fight

Mirror People Contend with Each Other

"A dynasty created by mortals banished to a small world. Its existence hints at intervention by unknown powerhouses, its civilization developing at a speed defying all reason."

"Perhaps related to those who fled the Xuanhuang Realm from the Ten Immortal Sects before the Great Cataclysm."

"Preliminary assessments suggest the possibility of key members within the Immortal Alliance already being infiltrated."

Sun Luyuan scrutinized these fragmented texts, his brow furrowed.

This Great Qi Sacred Dynasty was shrouded in mystery, its specific location within the small worlds remaining unknown. The Heavenly Profound Mirror was only able to gauge its approximate strength based on the activities of its personnel within the Xuanhuang Realm.

"It's a pity we couldn't capture the complete reasoning behind the Heavenly Profound Mirror's deduction, only scattered fragments of information."

Sun Luyuan couldn't help but feel a twinge of regret.
