Nevertheless, he placed great faith in the Heavenly Profound Mirror's judgments.

As the cornerstone of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's operations, the Heavenly Profound Mirror constantly received an unimaginable amount of data. If a cultivator, even a Longevity Realm existence, were to attempt to process so much data simultaneously, they would likely become sluggish. However, the Heavenly Profound Mirror not only handled everything perfectly, but could also predict to some extent the future based on the information it possessed.

However, concerning these "unforeseen events," the Heavenly Profound Mirror could not offer any advice or take any measures, only provide awareness.

Sun Luyuan was initially baffled by this.

However, during a conversation with Mirror Holder Fu, he understood the mystery behind it.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance is governed by humans, not by mirrors. No matter how miraculous it may be, it is only a tool. If it could make decisions without our consent, where would that leave us? If this precedent were set, wouldn't the Myriad Immortals Alliance descend into chaos?"

"As for why even its judgments cannot be wholly trusted..."

Mirror Holder Fu was silent for a long while, then said softly, "No major disturbances can occur in the Xuanhuang Realm. No matter what happens, it cannot shake our positions."

"The Heavenly Profound Mirror's judgments are purely rational deductions. A long time ago, we also attempted to utilize more of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's abilities to better manage the Myriad Immortals Alliance. However..."

Mirror Holder Fu paused, "Heh heh, it even made suggestions directed at us."

"It's better to honestly remain an [object]."

Sun Luyuan understood that those who actually ruled the Immortal Alliance wouldn't allow the Heavenly Profound Mirror to rise above them. They sought to maintain absolute control of power. Moreover, the Heavenly Profound Mirror was ultimately an object, and it was still unknown whether it could be completely trusted.

After mulling it over for a long time, Sun Luyuan's previously restless heart calmed down.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance has ruled for so many years, its roots are deeply entrenched. Its foundation is unimaginably profound. With Dharma Transmission Heavenly Venerate suppressing everything, how could it be so easily shaken?" Sun Luyuan thought this way, feeling incredulous at the idea that had just surfaced in his mind.

"However, nothing is absolute."

His confidence was implicitly undermined by recalling the various scenes he had witnessed during the daily operations of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

"I'll observe for now. Great Qi Sacred Dynasty..."

"If it truly has that momentum, then it won't be too late to decide."

After all, as the patriarch, his every move concerned the lives and well-being of hundreds of people, making it imperative to be cautious.

Suppressing the relevant information deep within his mind, Sun Luyuan then began to concern himself with his younger brother's condition.

His pained performance earlier had truly worried Sun Luyuan.

At that moment, Sun Luoyao seemed to have slowly recovered from the endless torment.

"Brother, I'm fine. For you, for the Sun family, I can still hold on a little longer," Sun Luoyao said with a bitter smile.

Sun Luyuan's heart trembled, and all the thousand words he wanted to say turned into silence at his lips.

"Oh, right, Brother. You said earlier that Lord Fu's task this time is to find the human avatar of the Heavenly Profound Mirror? What's going on?"

It was Sun Luoyao who broke the long silence in the underground secret chamber. Sun Luyuan then began to explain. "Lord Fu discovered that another Mirror Holder, Cang, appears to be plotting something in secret. Cang, among the Mirror Holders, is a radical and has always advocated more stringent restrictions on the Heavenly Profound Mirror. But recently, his attitude has become somewhat wavering."

"Lord Fu believes that Cang's abnormality may be related to the Heavenly Profound Mirror's avatar."

Sun Luoyao seemed a little hard-pressed to understand: "...How was this inferred?"

Sun Luyuan shook his head. "I don't know, perhaps Lord Fu knows something more than he explained to me."

"Though it's only a wild guess, we must complete the task since he has issued the order."

"Fortunately, he knows that this matter is exceedingly difficult, so he hasn't been too demanding."

Sun Luyuan snorted coldly.

Then he looked at Sun Luoyao: "It's just that you'll have to suffer again."

Sun Luoyao did not reply.

A moment later, he said quietly, "Let's begin. While I'm still in relatively good condition."

Sun Luyuan wore a complex expression as he nodded and then took the small Heavenly Profound Mirror from his arms.

Facing the Boundless Black Mirror from afar,

An invisible force instantly descended on the underground secret chamber, as if a passage had formed between the two mirrors. Countless images, mixed with strands of green light, flowed through the passage, being drawn into the Boundless Black Mirror.

Sun Luoyao's somewhat indistinct figure began to become increasingly unstable.

His gaze towards the Heavenly Profound Mirror revealed a desire he could barely suppress. However, in a flash, he forcibly suppressed this greed.

While his face was constantly shifting, more and more information was absorbed by the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Sun Luyuan nervously monitored the changes in the scene.

When the time was about the same as before, he had the intention to put away the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"Brother, wait a little longer!"

Sun Luyuan hesitated.

The longer they looked into the Heavenly Profound Mirror, the greater the chance of being detected by it. It was safer to try several times for a short duration, rather than one long peek.

But in the next moment, Sun Luoyao's words made his heart tremble.

"A human clone exists, it's true!"

"Brother, give me a little more time! I've found some clues!"

He hadn't expected it to go so smoothly this time, making Sun Luyuan ecstatic.

But then he thought, could this just be a lie his brother had concocted to devour more himself?

After all, he had done such things before.

"Trust me, Brother!"

The telepathic connection between the brothers made Sun Luoyao proactively speak, dispelling Sun Luyuan's doubts.

Sun Luyuan gritted his teeth and ultimately didn't put away the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Chapter 1167: Primordial Profound Spirit Array

Mysterious Origin Spirit Formation

As the seconds ticked by, cold sweat dripped from Sun Luyuan's forehead.

His brother, Sun Luoyao, seemed to be controlling his desires, rapidly searching for information about the Heavenly Profound Mirror's clone.

"I can't hold on any longer!"

Seeing that Sun Luoyao had no intention of stopping, a resolute look flashed in Sun Luyuan's eyes, and in an instant, he put away the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Suddenly deprived of the object of consumption, Sun Luoyao, as always, became ferocious.

"Not enough! I want more!"

"Brother, save me!"

It was only with Sun Luyuan's vital blood that his emotions slowly stabilized.

Like someone who had suffered immense trauma and been resurrected, Sun Luoyao's ghostly form seemed even weaker than before.

He sighed weakly, "Brother, you were too hasty. It was just a little bit more..."

"Better to fail than be exposed. Wait, you said..." Sun Luyuan was speaking when he suddenly realized the meaning of his brother's words.

Sun Luoyao nodded and transmitted some images to him. "It's true, it wasn't an excuse to devour more. This time, we were truly lucky and managed to capture possible information about the Heavenly Profound Mirror's clone."

"It's a shame that just as we were about to pinpoint the clone's exact location and identity, you broke the connection."

Sun Luoyao sounded a bit regretful, but there was no blame in his tone.

"To prove one's own Dao and attain freedom. This Heavenly Profound Mirror actually spawned a clone? It's not only escaping the Immortal Alliance's control but also attempting a unique transcendence through this?" Sun Luyuan felt somewhat incredulous.

And the other piece of information displayed in the data made his mind shake and his composure falter on the spot.

"Rebelling against the Mirror Holder, a Mirror Slave?"

Recalling what Lord Fu had said earlier about Mirror Holder Cang's abnormality, and the unspoken parts in Fu's words, Sun Luyuan suddenly understood.

"So Fu was also targeted by the Heavenly Profound Mirror, but perhaps he escaped by chance and wasn't controlled by it. That's why he is suspicious of Cang, who is also a Mirror Holder."

"The one who supervises and controls the Heavenly Profound Mirror also runs the risk of being controlled in turn. If this matter were to leak out, the entire Mirror Holder lineage would likely be purged. It might even cause tremors within the Immortal Alliance..."

Thinking of the consequences if this matter were exposed, Sun Luyuan felt a chill down his spine.

At the same time, he made up his mind: "No. I'd rather risk punishment from Fu than expose that I know about this. Otherwise, to maintain their own ruling position, Fu and all the other Mirror Holders will choose to silence me."

"Enough. This matter ends here. What Heavenly Profound Mirror clone, it has nothing to do with our Sun family. Brother, you rest for a while afterwards. As for Lord Fu, I will placate him." Sun Luyuan's expression turned stern, and he said coldly.

"Brother? Such a good opportunity..." Sun Luoyao looked confused, somewhat taken aback.

But Sun Luyuan did not explain to him. Instead, he conveyed his firm attitude through his eyes.

The Sun brothers have always had the elder brother make the decisions. Seeing this, Sun Luoyao had no choice.

After comforting his brother for a while, Sun Luyuan left the secret chamber with heavy thoughts.

After a long silence.

"My Lord, as you can see, you cannot blame me for this." Sun Luoyao said somewhat nervously to Li Fan.

"It's alright, your brother is indeed quite a character." Li Fan said lightly.

Li Fan's words were not an exaggeration.

To maintain calm thought and make the most correct decision under the influence of Li Fan's clone's secret techniques, the deliberate guidance of blood ties, and the temptation of numerous earth-shattering secrets.

This Patriarch of the Sun family was truly extraordinary.

Earlier, when he was in contact with the small Heavenly Profound Mirror and prying into its mysteries.

He was not stealing information about the Heavenly Profound Mirror's clone.

Li Fan already knew the location of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's clone. He could have easily revealed some information to satisfy them.

He had intended to use this earth-shattering secret to directly arrange a meeting with Mirror Holder Fu.

But Sun Luyuan's decisiveness caused Li Fan's plan to temporarily fall through.

However, Li Fan was not bothered.

"Today is just planting a seed. There will be plenty of opportunities in the future."

"Anyway, the objective for this trip has been achieved."

Li Fan examined the true information the Boundless Mirror had spied on just now.

"The [Mysterious Origin Spirit Grand Formation], re-establishing the primordial elements in the void, opening heaven and earth, recreating worlds..."

"Such power is almost akin to the gods in mythology. Immortal formations are truly something to aspire to."

That's right, this time Li Fan controlled the Boundless Mirror to steal fleeting thoughts about an immortal-level formation from the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

This thought had appeared several times, including but not limited to the Heavenly Profound Mirror's unwillingness to be bound, when recalling methods to escape confinement, when reminiscing about glorious times in the Immortal Realm, or when contemplating how to deal with the impending world-ending crisis of the Xuanhuang Realm.

This Grand Formation, possessing world-creation power, was constructed from a set of nine immortal-level formations.

Even in the Immortal Realm of that era, it was extremely powerful, and few could complete its deployment.

The [Mysterious Calculation, Myriad Spirits Unification] formation and the [Desolation Falling, Empty Chamber Blossoms] formation that Li Fan knew of previously, as well as the driving force behind the Boundless Mirror's ability to spy on the Heavenly Profound Mirror, [Boundless, Primordial Square], were all parts of this Mysterious Origin Spirit Grand Formation.

The Mysterious Calculation, Myriad Spirits Unification formation could digitize everything within its coverage, transforming it at will.

The Desolation Falling, Empty Chamber Blossoms formation could create things from nothingness.

And the Boundless, Primordial Square formation could analyze the secrets of the world within a small space, laying a solid foundation for the Mysterious Origin Spirit Grand Formation to create worlds.

Through the fleeting thoughts of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, Li Fan learned of a perception circulating in the Immortal Realm: any constituent part of the world shares an absolute similarity with the world itself. In other words, all secrets of the world could be deciphered and revealed through any object within the world.

All divine abilities and cultivation techniques could be comprehended from the most ordinary stone on the ground.

If someone had said this to Li Fan before, he would have thought they were talking nonsense.

But if it came from the memories of the Heavenly Profound Mirror and the common consensus of the Immortal Realm.

Then Li Fan had to ponder deeply.

However, he clearly couldn't comprehend such transcendental rules.

After pondering for a long time, Li Fan could only shake his head slightly, firmly engraving it in his heart.

Returning to his senses, based on the residual traces of the formation in the Boundless Mirror and the vague memory fragments of the [Mysterious Origin Spirit Grand Formation] from the Heavenly Profound Mirror, he began to attempt to deduce the [Boundless, Primordial Square] formation using the End of All Dissolution Disc.

"If the formation were complete, this Boundless Mirror would not only be able to spy on the Heavenly Profound Mirror. Perhaps all items in the Xuanhuang Realm would be unable to escape its analysis."

"Even the Immortal Treasure Fishing Pond..."

Chapter 1168: Silver Needles Fix the Derivation Method

Silver Needles Fix the Derivation Method

After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan couldn't help but shake his head and return to reality from his fantasies.

Even if he could analyze the Fishing Pond, Li Fan would never choose to act rashly. The horrifying scene of Senior Stone Slab being inexplicably "fished away" was still fresh in his memory. How could Li Fan repeat the same mistake for temporary gain?

Having learned from the lesson of the 119th lifetime, he would never provoke True Immortals head-on before he had absolute confidence in confronting them.

Since the treasures within the Fishing Pond could be obtained through continuous fishing, it would just take a little longer. He had plenty of time.

"If the [Boundless, Primordial Square] formation can be deduced, perhaps I can test the initial results of the Derivation Law Jade Token."

The clone briefly checked the situation of the main body and mused inwardly.

In the Derivation Law Jade Token space, time seemed to have lost its meaning.

Every day, he saw the unchanging scene of the derivation light sphere continuously rotating. The Derivation Law loli had somewhat adapted to Li Fan's intimidation and was even becoming a bit presumptuous. If not for the presence of the other two Harmonious Dao cultivators guarding the place, Li Fan would have certainly taught her a lesson.

However, it was not yet time to be overly aggressive, so he had to endure for a while.

"Fellow Daoist Sun, calculating the time, an adult Dharma Transmitter should come for an inspection in the next few days. We need to be mindful of this." Just as Li Fan was focusing most of his attention on deriving the Boundless formation, Hua Yueye, who had been silent all along, suddenly remembered something and transmitted a reminder.

During his onboarding, he had been informed of precautions, including periodic inspections by Dharma Transmitters. So Li Fan was not surprised, nodding in understanding.

"After the Dharma Transmitter completes the inspection, the use of the Law Seeking Jade Tokens should be reactivated. It should become more lively here then."

"Those who can come here and ask the Derivation Law Jade Token to deduce cultivation techniques are either from prominent families or are incredibly lucky. They will undoubtedly achieve extraordinary things in the future. As long as we do our jobs well, it would be wise to foster good relationships. Perhaps in a hundred years, when we leave, we can leverage these connections." Hua Yueye kindly advised.

Elder Zhang Xu also chimed in, "Exactly. Hundreds of years is a long time. Although the Derivation Law Jade Token space remains unchanged, the outside world might have undergone drastic transformations. Having an extra avenue is always a good thing."

Although they were already Harmonious Dao experts, those who came to guard here for five hundred years were generally not the core members of their respective families. Preparing for the future was only natural.

Half a month later, the Dharma Transmitter arrived as scheduled for the inspection.

Dharma Transmitter Lang. Li Fan had met him once before at the Dharma Transmitter Council.

Ignoring the three guards, Dharma Transmitter Lang came before the Derivation Law loli with a smile.

The loli rolled her eyes, then covered her ears with her hands, acting as if she couldn't hear anything he said.

Dharma Transmitter Lang seemed accustomed to this and was not angered.

A row of silver needles appeared beside him.

Dharma Transmitter Lang picked up one of them and then lunged towards the Derivation Law loli's head.

The loli's body trembled slightly, but it seemed as if some power was restraining her, preventing her from resisting. She could only allow the silver needles to be inserted into different acupoints on her body one by one.

This seemingly cruel scene made both Zhang Xu and Hua Yueye too afraid to speak.

However, Li Fan discerned something from the situation, his eyes gleaming.

Dharma Transmitter Lang's acupuncture technique was not for coercion or control.

It was a top-tier recuperation method to help regulate qi and blood and smooth the meridians. Indeed, after waiting for half a day, when Dharma Transmitter Lang withdrew the needles, the Derivation Law loli's complexion appeared much better.

Her face was rosy, as if she had just finished a strenuous workout.

"Not only is she healthier, but her humanistic aspects have also become more active."

Li Fan stared intently at the Derivation Law loli and noticed something peculiar.

During his close proximity to her over the past period, Li Fan had vaguely realized that although the little girl occasionally displayed human temperaments, most of the time she behaved like a pure machine, constantly deriving techniques without stopping.

The thought of wanting to "slack off and rest" was likely a natural consequence of overwork, not inherent to her.

Furthermore, as time went by, this tendency towards pure materialization became increasingly obvious.

"No wonder she needs regular inspections by Dharma Transmitters. It's to maintain the Derivation Law loli's humanity."

"Perhaps compared to a pure magical artifact, the Derivation Law Jade Token, guided by a pure little girl, can achieve better results."

However, the Derivation Law loli showed no goodwill towards Dharma Transmitter Lang, who was "helping" her.

She glared at him fiercely, and only after he leisurely departed did the loli slam the table heavily, venting her dissatisfaction.

Then, she slumped onto the long table and fell fast asleep.

The day after the inspection was a rest day for the Derivation Law loli, where she could rest freely.

The little girl slept soundly, her snores shaking the heavens.

However, Li Fan noticed that the giant derivation light sphere above her head still seemed to be rapidly transforming and deriving something.

"Interesting," Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

As Hua Yueye had predicted, once the Derivation Law loli returned to her endless work, the restrictions on the Law Seeking Jade Tokens were lifted.

In addition to the original derivation work, the little girl had to undertake the task of deriving customized cultivation techniques.

No wonder her attitude towards these Law Seekers was so hostile.

Except for a very few cultivators who were exceptionally handsome.

And the duties of Li Fan and the three Harmonious Dao guards also increased accordingly.

After all, they had to constantly be on guard against malicious attacks from other factions among these Law Seekers.

Fortunately, the probability of this was not particularly high.

With the three Harmonious Dao experts monitoring together, it should be safe for the time being.

...

Outside the void of the Great Qi small world, Tianquan Prefecture.

The Immortal Annihilation Grand Formation, originally used to isolate mortals, had been modified by Li Ping and become part of the Grand Formation of All Worldly Spirits.

Li Ping had even tamed and bred a batch of Void Crack Whales, specifically creating a void around the Great Qi small world to serve as a natural protective buffer.

At this moment, in the void that should have been empty, a colossal entity, a hundred times larger than the Great Qi small world, was hidden.

It was the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven!

Baihua Daoist lived up to expectations. At the cost of nearly falling into hibernation again, she finally managed to quietly move it here without alerting the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

After all, she was an ancient Longevity Realm cultivator. In terms of strength, she still surpassed ordinary Harmonious Dao experts.

Of course, the success of the task was also due to Li Ping's assistance in concealing it with formations.

Holy Emperor Li Ping, gazing at the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven from afar, sensed the rampant proliferation of mutated spiritual energy within, his expression impassive.

Chapter 1169: Five Elements Heavenly Transformation

Insectification of the Five Elements Heaven

The abundant spiritual energy within the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven was the perfect breeding ground for the Dao Yi insects to multiply infinitely.

A cataclysmic change was silently unfolding within the five grotto-heavens.

The fundamental changes in spiritual energy might escape the notice of ordinary living beings.

However, the highest forms of life within the grotto-heavens reacted immediately.

The most conspicuous among them was the giant tree in the Wood attribute grotto-heaven.

Its branches and leaves swayed as if trying to resist an invisible enemy.

A misty green radiance surged from within the giant tree, forming a barrier and attempting to prevent the invasion of mutated spiritual energy.

But unfortunately, the giant tree here had not yet reached the stage where it could form its own complete cycle.

The larger its form, the more nutrients it needed to draw from the outside world every moment.

It did not last long before the green barrier broke on its own.

The invisible mutated spiritual energy instantly swarmed and devoured the giant tree.

Li Ping, far outside the grotto-heaven, could clearly sense the process of the giant tree being completely transformed and consumed by the Dao Yi insects.

If one looked closely, one could see traces of countless small insects crawling on the leaves of the giant tree in the Wood attribute grotto-heaven.

And on the trunk, under the writhing of several Dao Yi insects, a human face was formed.

Hideous and terrifying, its gaze met Li Ping's in the void!

"Not bad."

Li Ping nodded slightly.

After struggling for a moment, the human face on the tree slowly receded into the trunk and disappeared. However, if viewed from a microscopic perspective, this giant tree had now been completely transformed into countless Dao Yi insects!

Not only this giant tree.

All beings within the Five Great Grotto-Heavens were undergoing the same kind of transformation, unable to escape.

Li Ping called this...

"Insectification!"

If, up to this point, the phenomena and changes brought about by the mutated Dao Yi insects were all within Holy Emperor Li Ping's expectations.

Then the scene that followed was somewhat unexpected.

When the entire Five Elements Grotto-Heaven reached over one-third insectification.

It seemed that a certain existence suddenly awakened.

Unlike the pure consciousness of the Heavenly Dao within a grotto-heaven or a small world, it was an entity hatched from the collective consciousness of countless Dao Yi insects, utilizing the shell of the small world's Heavenly Dao!

Compared to the normal Heavenly Dao of a world, this newly born World Consciousness of the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven was like the mutated Dao Yi insects.

It was filled with aggression and an infinite desire for greedy consumption!

Nine pale purple flying dragons suddenly appeared, guarding Li Ping.

As the only Heavenly Mandate Holy Emperor of the Great Qi small world existing around the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven, he felt a sense of danger, as if being targeted by this "Insectified Grotto-Heaven."

"A newborn calf dares to devour a tiger."

Li Ping snorted coldly, showing no signs of panic.

Although the overall insectification of the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven exceeded his expectations.

However, since he dared to ask Baihua Daoist to move the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven here, it meant he had sufficient confidence to deal with any problems.

"Sacred Dynasty's fortune, transformed into dragons. Myriad citizens, used for my purpose!"

Li Ping chanted, and behind him, the prosperous vision of countless citizens living in peace and contentment within the Sacred Dynasty Great Qi appeared.

Even though the Great Qi small world's scale was far inferior to the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, precisely because of the existence of countless beings with firm beliefs within it, it did not fall behind even when facing an entity a hundred times its size!

The Sacred Dynasty's vision was filled with a faint purple aura, as if solidified.

Li Ping, shouldering the beliefs and destiny of the myriad citizens of Great Qi, flickered and stepped onto the insectified Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven.

He stomped down fiercely!

In the void, the sharp cry of an ancient desolate beast suddenly sounded.

It echoed endlessly.

The vast Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven rumbled and trembled. The mutated spiritual energy within churned, instantly manifesting into various strange black monstrous forms.

They rushed out of the grotto-heaven world in extreme anger and fearless defiance, charging towards Li Ping.

Their target was not just Li Ping, but also the Sacred Dynasty Great Qi behind him!

"Heavenly Mandate Holy Emperor, benefiting all generations!"

The Sacred Dynasty's phantom behind him suddenly emitted infinite pale purple light, all of which enveloped Li Ping.

Li Ping's body also grew in the light of destiny's purple aura, expanding in the wind.

In just an instant, he became even larger than the entire Great Qi small world.

Truly like a colossal giant from myths, he stood before the myriad citizens of Great Qi, facing the black insectified monstrous beasts!

At this moment, on the sky curtain of the Sacred Dynasty Great Qi, the giant figure of Holy Emperor Li Ping also appeared.

Countless citizens instinctively knelt down, chanting the Holy Emperor's virtues.

With this assistance, Li Ping's figure grew several times larger.

The pale purple aura on his body gradually solidified, and Li Ping subsequently wielded it, turning it into lightning bolts that fiercely struck the monstrous beasts.

The rumbling continued in the void. The rate at which the insectified monstrous beasts evolved was far slower than the rate at which Li Ping eliminated them.

The Heavenly Mandate Holy Emperor, with an open hand, raised his fist and slammed it fiercely onto the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven.

One punch, two punches!

Although it was the simplest form of attack, accompanied by wisps of purple aura being forcibly injected into the grotto-heaven.

The ferocity of the insectified Five Elements Grotto-Heaven was slowly suppressed.

The original Dao Yi insects sent to erode the grotto-heaven were cultivated from a wisp of Li Ping's consciousness.

In a sense, these countless mutated Dao Yi insects were his descendants.

After briefly suppressing their insectified instincts, Li Ping gradually gained control of the insectified grotto-heaven through this connection.

The rebellious Five Elements Grotto-Heaven slowly calmed down.

The black monstrous beasts that had previously brandished their claws and wanted to kill Li Ping were now acting affectionately, flying to Li Ping's side and fawning over him.

Li Ping maintained his purple giant form, sensing the completely changed Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven.

After being insectified and then subdued, this grotto-heaven seemed to have become his another body.

Not only was he privy to everything within the grotto-heaven,

He could even control the insectified grotto-heaven to move and attack!

"World insectification..."

Li Ping pondered as he adapted to this new body.

"If ordinary grotto-heavens and small worlds are static existences like plants and trees, then after insectification, they possess abilities akin to wild beasts."

"Their aggression greatly increases, and they can even hunt and devour spontaneously."

"But it's not all benefits..."

Li Ping frowned slightly. "After insectification, the lifespan of the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven has also been greatly shortened."

"It might only last for less than a thousand years before inevitably entering decline."

Heaven and Earth have their own upper limits of existence.

Measured in billions of years, compared to mortals, it could almost be considered eternal existence.

But after insectification, it was reduced by who knew how many times.

"The disadvantages far outweigh the advantages."

"It can only be done once."

Li Ping, who considered himself a person of destiny, made such a judgment.

However, Li Fan's main body had a flicker of thought, giving rise to a different idea.

-

There are two activities on Qidian recently.

One is the Wish for Extra Chapters. If the goal is not met, all paid coins will be refunded, so don't worry, you can give it a try.

The other is the Cliffhanger Festival side story. I have written one for the Heavenly Doctor, and it will be released soon.

Chapter 1170: Spaceship Linking the Worlds

Ships of All Realms Connected

In the 119th lifetime, Heavenly Doctor told Li Fan, who was disguised as a successor of Heavenly Judgment, that after reaching the Harmonious Dao realm, cultivation methods became less important.

What was more crucial was the comprehension of the world's essence and the workings of the Heavenly Dao.

However, without the innate talents of Mr. Bai or Dharma Transmitters, how could an ordinary person comprehend such profound principles?

Even if Li Fan could indirectly comprehend them through continuous reincarnations, borrowing from the geniuses of Xuanhuang Realm and various fortuitous encounters, the effect was still not as good as direct personal experience.

The fact that worlds could also be "insectified" opened up new avenues for Li Fan.

"I can sense that after the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven was insectified, my dominant consciousness within it, much like when I previously controlled the Spiritual Wood Realm, is to transform my own being into the Heavenly Dao..."

"What could be easier than comprehending oneself through oneself?"

"Although the laws of the world might deviate slightly after insectification, they can still serve as a reference. And with the help of Returning to Truth, I can start over repeatedly, giving me ample opportunities for trial and error."

"Good."

The main body's thoughts turned, slowly planning for the future.

The perspective shifted back to Holy Emperor Li Ping.

Having completely subdued the insectified Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, Li Ping gazed at the behemoth beneath his feet, lost in thought.

His original plan was to use this grotto-heaven as a breeding ground for mutated spiritual energy, to be released en masse during the future battle with the Myriad Immortals Alliance, completely catching the enemy off guard.

But now, this insectified Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven seemed to have even greater utility.

Li Ping's heart stirred, and outside the grotto-heaven, the mutated spiritual energy once again evolved into nine thick black tentacles, extending towards the Great Qi small world.

Compared to the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, the Great Qi small world was like an ant beneath a giant's foot.

Under Li Ping's deliberate guidance, the Grand Formation of All Worldly Spirits and the Sacred Dynasty's destiny collectively cleared the defenses, and the nine tentacles easily took root deep within the small world.

Then, they coiled around the world several times from the outside.

"Move!"

The giant transformed from the Sacred Dynasty's destiny stood atop the insectified Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven and uttered a low cry.

The grotto-heaven rumbled, instantly coming alive as if it had a will of its own. It slowly moved into the depths of the void, away from the Xuanhuang Realm.

The nine tentacles acted like iron chains, tethering the Great Qi small world, and they moved forward together slowly.

"Using the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven as a reference, moving through the void is relatively slow now. But from a cultivator's perspective, it's quite fast, only slightly slower than a Deity Transformation cultivator flying at full speed."

Li Ping sensed the widening distance from the Xuanhuang Realm and nodded slightly.

Previously, even though Li Ping had made the Sacred Dynasty Great Qi impregnable, with numerous defenses like Sky Patrol Arrows and the Grand Formation of All Worldly Spirits, one problem remained unavoidable.

That was the Great Qi small world's proximity to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Without strategic depth, once the Myriad Immortals Alliance discovered its exact location, it could be trapped in a difficult situation of siege under a surprise attack.

But if it were hidden deeper...

For thousands of years, the Void Crack Whale swarms had been ceaselessly carving out the void.

They had created an excellent hiding environment.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance has records of small worlds where mortals migrated in the past."

"However, when they pinpoint the location and attempt to attack, they will find that the small world from that year has already become a void. They will likely be very perplexed."

"Indeed, perhaps I can even set up numerous killing formations in the original location of the Great Qi small world, waiting for the Myriad Immortals Alliance to fall into a trap. Hehehe..."

In an instant, countless schemes flooded Li Ping's mind.

The slow movement of the entire small world did not attract the attention of the citizens within the Sacred Dynasty Great Qi.

Even the nine black tentacles deeply embedded in the world were only noticed by a few individuals, including Sun Erlang.

However, upon learning that it was Holy Emperor Li Ping's doing, they could only sigh at the Holy Emperor's divine might.

"Fellow Daoist, where are you planning to drag the world to..."

Outside the world, in the void.

Having received Li Ping's assistance and recovered somewhat, Baihua Daoist, upon sensing the world's movement, rushed out to investigate.

What she saw was the insectified Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, with nine tentacles dragging the small world, moving rapidly forward.

Even though she considered herself knowledgeable, she was still stunned by the scene before her.

"Why must there be a destination?"

Li Ping dissipated his giant form and returned to his normal posture, saying calmly.

The actions just now had consumed a certain amount of the dynasty's destiny, but with the Sacred Dynasty's booming and prosperous momentum, it could be fully restored within half a year.

"Between a fixed pass and a ship drifting unpredictably on the river. Which one is harder to breach?" Li Ping's tone was melancholic.

Baihua Daoist immediately understood Li Ping's meaning and nodded, "Indeed. Moving constantly in the void, unable to even pinpoint its location, let alone launch a siege. Fellow Daoist's move is truly ingenious."

Baihua praised.

"However, there is still one drawback for now."

"What?"

"Dragging only one Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven causes the speed through the void to be too slow."

Baihua Daoist's heart suddenly harbored an ominous premonition.

"Therefore, I will still have to trouble Fellow Daoist Baihua to make a few more trips."

Li Ping turned his head and said earnestly.

"I have a few more suitable targets here. Although their scale is not comparable to the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, they are barely usable. After Fellow Daoist moves them all here, I will connect them with formations, and then the forward momentum will increase severalfold."

Recalling the miserable experience of moving the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven before, and looking at the specific information of more than ten grotto-heavens transmitted by Li Ping, Baihua Daoist felt dizzy, her future seeming bleak.

"Heh heh, Fellow Daoist, rest assured. Since you are working so hard for the Sacred Dynasty, I will naturally not treat you unfairly." Li Ping smiled and pointed into the air with a finger.

A golden Qilin suddenly appeared before Baihua.

"This is? Ten Thousand Spirit Nectar?" Baihua Daoist exclaimed.

"Uh, no. It's just condensed cultivation." In the next moment, Baihua felt a slight regret.

"Heh heh, Origin Force Essence can only be condensed by True Immortals. How could I possibly master it? However, this refined Origin Force should help mitigate some of the damage Fellow Daoist sustained from moving the grotto-heavens." Li Ping said calmly.

The Origin Force constituting the golden Qilin was naturally condensed from the cultivators of Great Qi practicing the [Enlightenment Spirit Yuan Technique].

It was an existence one level below Origin Force Essence, pure cultivation without attributes.

Baihua Daoist maintained her composure for a moment before opening her mouth and swallowing the golden Qilin.

Instantly refining it, not only did her old wounds heal, but her dark golden glazed body even became more consolidated.

"Many thanks for Fellow Daoist's assistance."

Chapter 1171: Who Decides Right or Wrong

Who Judges Right and Wrong

"However, the Origin Force that Fellow Daoist gave me seems to be..."

"More advanced?"

Baihua Daoist carefully chose her words and asked slowly.

Li Ping naturally would not tell Baihua that the reason the Origin Force's effects were far superior to ordinary cultivation was because he wanted to use the power of belief from all beings to elevate the Origin Force into Origin Force Essence.

However, all current attempts had ended in failure.

After all, even abandoned by True Immortals, it was still power transcending the mortal realm, not easily controlled.

"It's just your imagination. How is your recovery? If you're almost ready, you should be on your way." Li Ping said calmly.

Baihua Daoist gave an awkward smile, but she had no other choice. With a sigh, she bid farewell and set off.

"After ensuring the absolute safety of the main base, we can consider conquering other small worlds."

"Know the exact location of each small world, and even infiltrate it beforehand, moving the entrance to the void near Great Qi."

"Spiritual Wood, Empire..."

"And Netherworld."

Just as Holy Emperor Li Ping returned to the Sacred Emperor's Seat, sitting and contemplating the future direction of the Sacred Dynasty.

His disciple Sun Erlang came to seek an audience.

"Uh, Master. An item I fished out from the Fishing Pond earlier..." Sun Erlang looked somewhat uneasy.

"Speak freely."

Then Sun Erlang explained the whole story.

It turned out that after the previous fishing competition ended, most of the fishermen who received rewards were absorbed by various institutions of the Sacred Dynasty.

Among them, a middle-aged man named Quan Ruochu was noticed by Sun Erlang and taken under his wing.

What he fished out from the Fishing Pond was a white light sphere.

At that time, Li Ping had personally inspected it. It was an ordinary item called [Orchid Dark Flower], so he didn't pay much attention to it.

But now, according to Sun Erlang, this Orchid Dark Flower, with a quality of at most Nascent Soul at first glance, had displayed abilities completely beyond reason after being carefully cultivated by Quan Ruochu for a period of time.

"Quan Ruochu, although middle-aged, has achieved nothing. Both his parents are dead, and he has no wife or children. His only passion in life is fishing and tending to flowers. He has a calm temperament and no ambition. Therefore, after fishing out the white light sphere, he was not particularly disappointed. In fact, he liked this Orchid Dark Flower more than other treasures."

"Originally, it was thought that this Orchid Dark Flower, like normal flowers, grew in soil and was nourished by spiritual energy. However, after Quan Ruochu planted it, no matter how carefully he tended to it, it remained listless and on the verge of wilting. Out of deep affection for the flower, Quan Ruochu actually did something unimaginable to save it," Sun Erlang bowed his head and quietly narrated to the Holy Emperor.

"He actually planted the Orchid Dark Flower on himself! Using his own flesh and blood as soil, nourishing it with vital essence..."

"Within days, he transformed from a relatively robust man into a skeletal figure, barely breathing! But he still didn't give up, intending to use his last bit of vital essence to water it."

"After not seeing him for a few days, I went to look for him and saw him in this state."

Sun Erlang's voice was low: "I initially wanted to directly eliminate this demonic flower, but Quan Ruochu threatened me with his own life, saying that the flower lives, he lives; the flower dies, he dies..."

"Moreover, considering it was a treasure bestowed by Master, I hesitated and did not act. But seeing Quan Ruochu's body weakening by the day and nearing death, I ultimately could not stand by and watch."

The moment Sun Erlang spoke, Li Ping had already located Quan Ruochu's whereabouts and was carefully examining his condition.

After all, it was only a blue light sphere, with no particularly profound features. Upon a glance, he understood.

After Sun Erlang finished speaking, Li Ping shook his head and said sternly.

"Erlang, you have disappointed me greatly."

Sun Erlang's body trembled slightly, and his head sank even lower.

"A commander should lead the entire army, not have his emotions swayed by individuals, or even small groups of dozens or hundreds."

"Since you became my disciple, this is the first time you've actively sought an audience with me. And it's for this matter?"

After a long silence, Sun Erlang said with difficulty, "Master, please see. If I were to die instantly, I might remain unmoved. But to watch a familiar person's life slowly drain away, to wither away. I truly cannot remain calm."

"I await your punishment."

Li Ping's voice, booming continuously like heavenly thunder, echoed in the Sacred Emperor's Seat.

"The reason I am disappointed in you is not only your indecisiveness but also your lack of discernment. A demonic flower..."

"Go back and look again!"

Li Ping waved his hand and banished Sun Erlang.

Sun Erlang's heart tightened for a moment, then, as if understanding something, he rejoiced and rushed to Quan Ruochu's residence.

Upon Master's prompting, Sun Erlang observed more carefully and finally discovered the mystery of the Orchid Dark Flower.

Although it appeared to be constantly consuming Quan Ruochu's vital blood, it was simultaneously differentiating a wisp of miraculous power to sustain Quan Ruochu's life force.

It was in this state of near-death, near-death, that the Orchid Dark Flower flourished.

At the same time, Quan Ruochu was also undergoing a complete transformation.

"His last thread of life is tied to this Orchid Dark Flower. If I had rashly cut it off, it would have led to the death of both flower and person. I nearly made a grave mistake!" Sun Erlang couldn't help but feel a lingering fear.

He sealed the entrance, preventing any external interference, and simultaneously moved a miniature [Heaven and Earth Furnace] nearby to ensure ample spiritual energy concentration in the surroundings.

After completing these tasks, Sun Erlang finally breathed a sigh of relief.

"Thanks to Master's guidance." He said with a sense of relief.

However, Sun Erlang did not know that the Orchid Dark Flower did indeed protect Quan Ruochu's vital thread of life.

But it was not out of gratitude for his planting, merely a survival instinct before finding a new host.

And Quan Ruochu, with only a Qi Refining cultivation, could not withstand such unrestrained absorption by the Orchid Dark Flower. Death was only a matter of time.

If there were no external forces to assist.

And the reason he appeared to be getting better was purely because Holy Emperor Li Ping had given him a helping hand.

"Right or wrong, evil or good."

"Until the final outcome is reached, no one can accurately judge."

"Only by walking step by step to the end, can one vindicate oneself."

"The process... is not important."

Holy Emperor Li Ping sat on the Sacred Emperor's Seat, his thoughts stirring slightly.

...

In a certain mystic realm amidst an endless white mist.

"What... how many ice-sealed corpses are there here?"

Shang Shaojun, brought into the Reversal of Life and Death Grand Formation by the Saint Fetus Li Fan, exclaimed in shock at the horrifying sight before him.

Chapter 1172: Death Thought Yin-Yang Pearl

Dying Thoughts Yin-Yang Pearl

As the commander of the Azure Profound Army, Shang Shaojun had suppressed the Chattering Abyss for a hundred years. Even when facing the terrifying world-ending demonic sound tides, he could remain calm and composed.

But now, he truly felt a bone-chilling fear that he hadn't experienced in a long time.

There were simply too many cultivators who had died and were frozen here.

Shang Shaojun found it hard to imagine where all these cultivators came from.

The number of cultivators buried here probably exceeded that of the entire Xuanhuang Realm!

The Saint Fetus Li Fan also pretended to be frightened by the scene before him, his body trembling slightly, his face showing an expression of horror.

"Young Commander, do not act rashly. Caution is paramount," he said after a while, as if regaining his senses, comforting Shang Shaojun.

Shang Shaojun's expression remained grim. He kept scanning his surroundings, as if there were hidden enemies lurking.

"Something is... not right here. Did you hear anything?" Shang Shaojun asked via telepathic transmission.

"A sound? What sound?" The Saint Fetus Li Fan asked in surprise, and this was not an act.

Shang Shaojun's face darkened. "Perhaps it's because I stayed in the Chattering Abyss for too long that I'm sensitive to any sound. Ever since I arrived in this domain, I've been vaguely hearing some kind of whispering. It comes and goes. Didn't you hear it?"

The Saint Fetus Li Fan narrowed his eyes.

This was not his first time here.

He had even guided various cultivators to this place.

But no one else, like Shang Shaojun, had been able to hear strange sounds in the deathly silent Sea of Ice Seals.

A different thought arose in his mind, and the Saint Fetus Li Fan said solemnly, "What do you think, Young Commander? There must be a great secret involved here. But similarly, if we are to investigate further, we will undoubtedly face immense risks. Should we leave now before we are discovered, or explore it thoroughly?"

Shang Shaojun did not answer immediately. He tilted his ear, as if trying to discern the sound he heard.

After a moment, he transmitted his thoughts, "Brother Li, follow me. I have a premonition that tracing the source of this sound might unlock part of the mystery of this place."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan nodded slightly, drawing his sword, its shadow protecting them.

"Be careful."

The two shuttled through the endless Sea of Ice Seals.

Li Fan was actually already familiar with the overall structure of the "Great Array of Reversing Life and Death."

However, since he was pretending to be here for the first time, even though he watched Shang Shaojun lead him in circles within the formation, he did not expose it.

He simply followed behind in silence.

But as Shang Shaojun stubbornly pressed in a certain direction, the Saint Fetus Li Fan also noticed subtle changes in the surroundings caused by this.

Previously, these changes had even evaded the analysis of the End of All Dissolution Disc, and he had overlooked them!

"There's actually this hidden change within the great array? As expected of an array capable of achieving longevity." Li Fan was secretly astonished.

They continued to advance.

It was as if they were standing still, but the ice-sealed coffins in the surrounding dead sea rotated around them.

The deeper they went, the faster the surrounding scenery spun.

"Brother Li, be careful. It seems the source of the sound is just ahead!" Shang Shaojun's voice was also tinged with nervousness.

It was like passing through a narrow space-time tunnel, where the surrounding scenery turned into overlapping lines due to the rapid speed.

When they broke through the end of the tunnel, countless circles converged into a single point.

Then, they exploded in their vision.

The scene suddenly opened up.

However, the surrounding air became even colder.

It was so cold that even the Saint Fetus Li Fan and Shang Shaojun felt their bodies stiffen.

"Hoo..."

They activated their internal spiritual energy, trying to dispel the biting cold.

The two carefully examined their surroundings.

It seemed to be the interior of a silver-white light sphere. Other than some blurry boundaries, there was nothing else here.

Looking back in the direction they came from, the sight made their pupils contract sharply.

Like yin-yang fish, small spheres that spun constantly, floated quietly in the air.

From the dim portions of them, the Saint Fetus Li Fan could vaguely sense the aura of the previously deathly silent Sea of Ice Seals.

And within this white light sphere, there were eight more such yin-yang spheres!

A total of nine, arranged in a special formation.

Shang Shaojun swallowed hard with difficulty.

The number of dead within just one of the yin-yang spheres was countless.

If this number were multiplied by nine...

The two looked at each other, both seeing the fear in each other's hearts.

They even communicated via telepathic transmission with great caution.

For fear of disturbing the nine yin-yang pearls here.

"Young Commander, the sound you heard earlier..."

"It's gone. When we entered this place, it abruptly stopped and mysteriously disappeared. Wait..." Shang Shaojun suddenly froze, and turned to look in the opposite direction of the yin-yang pearls.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan followed his gaze, but saw nothing.

"Be careful."

Shang Shaojun only uttered a cautious reminder and then fell silent.

His body became stiff and motionless, his breathing instantly becoming extremely weak.

Only then did the Saint Fetus Li Fan sense that some invisible presence had descended upon this space.

Thump! Thump! Thump!

Although there were no distinct sounds, the heavy footsteps seemed to be pounding directly on Li Fan's heart.

The footsteps grew closer and closer.

Ignoring the two intruders, the presence walked directly towards the nine yin-yang pearls.

Hoo...

A soft exhaling sound could be heard.

The space around the yin-yang pearls also showed distortions and fluctuations.

As if being boiled in boiling water, the yin and yang portions of the nine small spheres rotated around each other, becoming more distinct.

And Shang Shaojun and Li Fan clearly saw that wisps of ice-sealed corpses were entering the nine yin-yang pearls along with the unknown being's exhalation.

The entire extremely bizarre process did not last long.

The oppressive footsteps gradually receded, and the silver-white space slowly returned to normal.

The nine yin-yang pearls also slowly settled, becoming calm again.

After a long while, the two finally communicated via telepathic transmission.

"What... what was that just now?"

"A sense of crisis, like needles piercing my entire body. My spiritual sense gave frantic warnings. It felt as if imminent disaster was upon me... This feeling, even a Longevity Heavenly Venerate might not be able to bring about?"

After a few brief sentences, the two fell into extreme silence.

"The sound I heard earlier should have been the echo of that unknown being's footsteps here," Shang Shaojun guessed, "Even though it has already departed, the sound lingers.

"The countless ice-sealed corpses in the yin-yang pearls seem to be the work of that fellow. But I still can't figure out where it got so many bodies from? And what lies outside this silver-white space?"

The Saint Fetus Li Fan could not answer these questions either.

He had originally thought this was merely the Daoist field of the Heavenly Venerate of Reincarnation. He did not expect that in this lifetime, by chance, he had stumbled upon a deeper secret hidden behind it.

Chapter 1173: The Undying Great Vow Body

The Undying Grand Vow Body

Previously, Li Fan had always been puzzled by the countless corpses in the "Great Array of Reversing Life and Death."

There were too many inexplicable aspects.

Firstly, the sheer quantity. Secondly...

All the corpses were preserved in relatively good condition.

They did not look like they were left behind from the great catastrophe and the destruction of worlds.

"I originally suspected that the Heavenly Venerate of Reincarnation might also be a clone of the Heavenly Doctor. Now it seems..."

Recalling the terrifying formless monster from just now, Li Fan cast doubt on his own judgment.

"What is the connection between that monster and the Heavenly Venerate of Reincarnation?"

Li Fan had met the Heavenly Venerate of Reincarnation before.

In the 119th lifetime, when the White Mist Body suddenly appeared and instantly killed three Dharma Transmitters.

However, after the Dharma Transmitters stepped forward, the matter was dropped.

"Dharma Transmitters, Heavenly Doctor, Reincarnation. There must be some connection between these three."

"But that formless monster from just now..."

In an instant, countless thoughts flashed through the Saint Fetus Li Fan's mind.

"Brother Li, for the sake of safety, we should leave here first," Shang Shaojun's words interrupted his reverie.

The two followed the path they came by and returned to the yin-yang pearls.

However, this time, they directly appeared on the Sea of Life, opposite the Sea of Deathly Stillness.

Furthermore, the wind on the sea blew towards the exit of the domain.

"Is this... a gesture of seeing us off?"

The two looked at each other, startled again.

At that moment, they did not dare to linger and cause further trouble, so they sheepishly left through the exit.

"Hoo." After leaving the Domain of Life and Death and returning to the white mist, Shang Shaojun did not feel the relief of surviving a disaster.

Instead, he became somewhat dejected. "The Xuanhuang Realm hides too many secrets."

"The formless being encountered this time is definitely no weaker than that mysterious person who reshapes worlds. Even if His Elderliness the Heavenly Venerate were to return, could he truly eradicate everything..."

Having witnessed too many things beyond his comprehension in a short period, Shang Shaojun became somewhat lost.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan immediately changed the subject. "What do you think of that formless being, Young Commander?"

"It doesn't seem like a cultivator. Otherwise, it wouldn't have ignored us. It's more like some kind of fixed task executor..."

"A monster?" Shang Shaojun struggled to find a descriptor after a long while.

"But even if it's a monster, it's still an existence that completely crushes us," he said self-deprecatingly. "I presided over the Chattering Abyss for hundreds of years, mastered divine arts, and considered myself unparalleled beneath the Longevity Realm. Who knew that after traveling with Brother Li for only a year or two, I would encounter so many terrifying beings? Only now do I realize how limited my previous perspective was."

Li Fan comforted him, "It's not that Young Commander is not strong. It's just that these old monsters are too deeply hidden."

After a moment of contemplation, the Saint Fetus Li Fan asked, "Does Young Commander feel disheartened?"

"Not at all, not at all. As the saying goes, when a nation is about to fall, strange omens will appear. The more chaos erupts, the more it shows that the Xuanhuang Realm is already terminally ill," Shang Shaojun said, becoming more passionate after a brief moment of dejection.

"However, with the strength of just the two of us, it's a bit difficult to change all of this."

"We need help," Shang Shaojun said earnestly.

"I had this intention originally. However, finding trustworthy subordinates with sufficient capability is truly difficult..." the Saint Fetus Li Fan sighed.

Shang Shaojun's eyes gleamed as he looked out beyond the white mist, "I do have some preferred candidates."

"Let's go. We'll go back first. We've gained some evidence from our travels at least. We have at least a seventy percent chance of persuading them." While flying in the white mist, Shang Shaojun introduced people to Li Fan.

"First, Di Lun. Has Brother Li heard of this person?"

"Although this person is only at the Nascent Soul stage now, his strength is by no means inferior to mine. He is proficient in all laws and skilled in all martial arts—a top prodigy of the Xuanhuang Realm. More importantly, this person is absolutely loyal to the Myriad Immortals Alliance! If we can persuade him to join us, it might even bring additional surprises."

"There's another person named Ji Hongdao. He is a rare formation genius of this era. If not for his weak background and seniority, I believe he could at least contend for the position of Chief of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Array Hall! Besides formations, he is also skilled in artifact refining..."

Shang Shaojun rattled off one name after another.

All of them were people Li Fan was familiar with.

"Um, actually, there's one more person we might consider. However..." Shang Shaojun hesitated.

"However, this person's origins are not simple. His background is too complicated. Bringing him might not be a good thing."

Without playing coy, Shang Shaojun continued, "Although he appears to be just a child, he is terrifyingly strong when fighting. Even I, at the Harmonious Dao stage, might not be able to force out his full strength. However, his mind is not very clear. As long as he sees someone, he wants to spar with them..."

Li Fan instantly understood who Shang Shaojun was referring to.

The martial arts fanatic who was suspected to be the reincarnation of Senior Brother Zhang Qianmo.

Li Fan had once used the extremely high authority of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's origin to search for information about the martial arts fanatic.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance's assessment of him was that he was the "Spirit of Heaven and Earth, born into human form." Although he possessed a human body, his behavior, habits, and way of thinking were not like those of a human. Instead, he was more like a rule embodied by the spirit of heaven and earth.

The martial arts fanatic was not invincible in battle, but his learning ability was terrifying. Any move used against him during a fight would be immediately learned by him.

The Immortal Alliance had also tried to capture him for careful study. However, he could repeatedly disappear out of thin air under the watchful eyes and strict guard of many. He would reappear far away, with no recollection of being captured.

The Immortal Alliance even sent several Harmonious Dao cultivators to join forces to kill him.

The martial arts fanatic's corpse was utterly annihilated. Yet, not long after, he reappeared in the world, alive and well. And he had even learned some of the divine abilities of those Harmonious Dao cultivators.

Given such a troublesome existence, since he only sought sparring partners quietly and did not pose any threat to the safety of the Immortal Alliance, the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters decided to merely monitor him strictly and not interfere further.

Li Fan speculated that the reason for the martial arts fanatic's peculiar abilities might be related to Senior Brother Zhang's Grand Vow Body. The Grand Vow Body, integrated with heaven and earth, was almost a part of the laws of heaven and earth. Mistaking him for the spirit of heaven and earth was not surprising. As for whether the martial arts fanatic had any relation to Senior Brother Zhang... the extreme similarity between their faces explained everything.

"Young Commander, don't worry too much. We should welcome everyone, the more the merrier. After all, if what we are trying to do fails..."

"We might not have a place to stay in the Immortal Alliance anymore," the Saint Fetus Li Fan said with a smile.

Shang Shaojun was slightly taken aback, then nodded.

"Then let's visit them one by one!"

Chapter 1174: The Heavenly Venerable Suddenly Transmits a Message

Heavenly Venerate Suddenly Transmits a Message

"Young Commander, is Di Lun from the 'Era'?"

On the way to the Heavenly Pivot Prefecture of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, the Saint Fetus Li Fan asked a question that had long been troubling him.

Shang Shaojun paused. It seemed Li Fan's knowledge of the Immortal Alliance's secret concerning 'Era' did not surprise him.

He replied in a low voice, "Yes and no."

"From what I know, the Immortal Alliance did indeed cultivate a batch of death warriors using 'Era.' However, those people were ultimately not born from the Xuanhuang Realm. They lacked a certain spiritual essence."

"Although they all displayed astonishing talent during the era simulation, their actual performance after arriving in the Xuanhuang Realm was much weaker. They were suitable as fearless cannon fodder, but difficult to entrust with important tasks." Shang Shaojun shook his head slightly.

"However, later, the Immortal Alliance found a way to improve. Does Brother Li know that each Dharma Transmitter has their own exclusive small world?"

The Saint Fetus Li Fan responded, "I've heard whispers."

"Each Dharma Transmitter dedicates a portion of their subordinate small worlds to jointly form a 'Primordial Great Realm.' It is said to be a truly cruel world of chaos. Every hundred years, the beings within undergo a thorough cleansing. Only those who are collectively praised by the Dharma Transmitters within a hundred years can be spared."

"Brother Li, you must understand that the beings in the 'Primordial Great Realm' are either selected consciousnesses and souls from 'Era,' or peerless prodigies from the respective Dharma Transmitters' worlds. To stand out in such an environment... their abilities can be imagined."

Shang Shaojun's tone was solemn. "Di Lun's origins are precisely like this."

"From 'Era' to the 'Primordial Great Realm.' Di Lun walked step by step, and finally gained the favor of the various Dharma Transmitters. He was even allowed to reshape his body using a supreme treasure left by a Heavenly Venerate. Moreover, due to their deep trust, he was specially permitted to retain his previous experiences and memories. Although he currently holds no specific position within the Immortal Alliance, no one dares to slight him."

"Thus, this Di Lun is truly legendary," the Saint Fetus Li Fan remarked with some emotion after hearing Shang Shaojun's introduction.

However, he then became somewhat puzzled. "A character like this, and we just go to his door... Young Commander, aren't you afraid he'll directly capture us and present us to the Dharma Transmitters?"

Shang Shaojun burst into laughter. "Brother Li, you worry too much. Firstly, I had a good relationship with Di Lun from adventuring together back then. The reason Di Lun is so trusted by the Dharma Transmitters is precisely because his soul has always been imprinted with loyalty to the Immortal Alliance since his creation. The more experiences he has and the stronger he becomes, the deeper this imprint becomes."

"He said this himself. He personally doesn't care and even sees it as a great honor. Aren't we doing all this for the Myriad Immortals Alliance? If he knew that the Myriad Immortals Alliance was harboring many hidden schemes, he would definitely not stand idly by. Given his personality, he might even personally make a trip to verify what we say." Shang Shaojun looked full of confidence.

However, things did not go as smoothly as planned.

"What? Di Lun is not here?"

"We had an appointment!"

Outside Di Lun's residence, Shang Shaojun and Li Fan were blocked.

Shang Shaojun's expression turned ugly, his Harmonious Dao cultivator's pressure surging.

The two guards at the gate, though pale, maintained their composure and explained, "Your Lord, please forgive our transgression. The Master received an urgent secret order from the Immortal Alliance and departed in haste. The matter was urgent, so he couldn't even afford to say goodbye..."

Shang Shaojun tried, using a communication talisman to contact Di Lun again. As expected, there was no response.

He exchanged a glance with Li Fan. Knowing that forcing the issue was impossible, he simply snorted and let it go.

"I think it's not that Di Lun is deliberately avoiding us, but that there's truly something important," Li Fan whispered.

"Mm. I know Di Lun's character. He wouldn't make excuses. It's just that I don't know what happened in the Immortal Alliance that required Di Lun's urgent mobilization. This matter must be significant," Shang Shaojun murmured.

With their first target falling through, the two intended to go to Ji Hongdao in Heavenly Yu Prefecture.

However, they did not expect that Ji Hongdao had also been transferred due to an appointment.

The two looked at each other, deciding to temporarily halt their search.

"Something's not right. Let me find someone to inquire about it." Shang Shaojun's brows furrowed tightly.

Meanwhile, Li Fan, hidden within the Boundless Mirror, had quietly set his plan in motion.

He stealthily stole a small Heavenly Profound Mirror from the Sun family and activated the Boundless Mirror to probe the information within.

The Heavenly Profound Mirror had indeed learned of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's recent movements. However, this result surprised Li Fan.

"The Dharma Transmitter Heavenly Venerate transmitted a message stating that the Xuanhuang Realm might experience some minor tremors soon, and the Immortal Alliance needs to prepare countermeasures in advance."

"This..."

"This is one of the rare times the Dharma Transmitter Heavenly Venerate has personally transmitted a message since the founding of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. The Dharma Transmitters are taking this extremely seriously..."

After disconnecting the probe from the Boundless Mirror and offering it some comfort, Li Fan fell into deep thought.

He was unsure if this event, "Transmission from the Heavenly Venerate," had occurred in his previous reincarnations.

However, the "minor tremors" in the Xuanhuang Realm had definitely not happened in any of the lifetimes he had experienced.

"The Dharma Transmitter Heavenly Venerate specifically sent a message to warn, indicating that the coming tremors would not be small. If caught unprepared, it might cause widespread panic."

"But the transmission is just a message, and the main body hasn't returned, meaning this tremor won't cause a truly destructive blow to the Xuanhuang Realm..."

"The Dharma Transmitter predicted the tremors will occur in about a month. Then we'll know if it's an event unique to this lifetime."

...

Shang Shaojun also gathered some information.

Naturally, it was not as detailed as what Li Fan had stolen from the Heavenly Profound Mirror, but it was largely similar.

"The entire Myriad Immortals Alliance, from top to bottom, has been mobilized. I suppose similar orders will be sent to the Eternal Immortal Fortress soon..."

"Brother Li, what do you think?"

The Saint Fetus Li Fan pondered for a moment and said, "Our goal cannot be achieved in a day or two. Since the entire Xuanhuang Realm is about to face a crisis, it's best to prepare to deal with it first."

"The Azure Profound Army cannot be without a leader. The Chattering Abyss might also become active again. Why don't we return to the Eternal Immortal Fortress first and observe the situation?"

Li Fan's suggestion was approved by Shang Shaojun.

The two then hastily ended their trip and returned to the Broken Hand Immortal City.

Gazing at the Chattering Abyss, which was tranquil and profound in the distance, the Saint Fetus Li Fan's mind resurfaced with the image of the figure that had appeared at the bottom of the Chattering Abyss previously.

"Perhaps, the special aspect of this lifetime is related to my little actions?"

Li Fan frowned slightly, somewhat puzzled.

Chapter 1175: Two Immortals in the Sea of Stars

Judging Right and Wrong

"Perhaps" can be removed from the previous sentence.

If the Xuanhuang Realm truly experiences a large-scale upheaval as predicted, then it is almost certain that it was caused by Li Fan's actions in this lifetime.

"The root of the Xuanhuang Realm's tremors should stem from the suction of the Immortal Ruins."

"The key lies here. How can I, a mere mortal, influence the Immortal Ruins?"

The scenes Li Fan had experienced in this lifetime flashed rapidly before his eyes.

After eliminating all impossible options, Li Fan was left with a few suspects.

The mysterious figure in the Chattering Abyss that reinserted world fragments.

The formless being in the Domain of Life and Death that collected the corpses of cultivators.

And...

The relocation and transfer of the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven.

With Li Fan's current strength, whether it be the main body or his clones, he was incapable of altering the Immortal Ruins in the slightest.

However, his actions could influence and change the destinies of powerful beings who could shake the Immortal Ruins, thereby causing deviations.

"It's only a little over a month away. We can wait patiently."

While the Myriad Immortals Alliance was in a state of emergency preparedness, the Sacred Dynasty Great Qi was also doing the same.

Not long ago, an imperial decree was issued stating that the Sacred Emperor would be testing his divine abilities in the void outside the Great Qi. Minor tremors might occur, which was normal and not to be alarmed.

The citizens of Great Qi, whose worship of the Sacred Emperor had reached a near-fanatical level, naturally believed whatever he said.

Upon hearing this, the citizens were not only unafraid but even eagerly anticipated the power of the Sacred Emperor's divine abilities.

In the secret chamber beneath the Sacred Emperor's Seat, Yin Shangren and Li Ping faced each other.

"The little ones you sent me last time indeed have great talent. Some are even smarter than I imagined. Two of them have already successfully established their foundations with me. The others should not be far behind."

"If they had accepted the 'Establishing Foundation with Me' method from the beginning, it would indeed greatly aid their cultivation."

Yin Shangren first summarized the recent results, then changed the subject. "Lately, I've been feeling uneasy. I heard you're going to test some divine abilities? Try to stay far away and don't destroy this small world."

"I quite like it here," Yin Shangren said nonchalantly.

Li Ping nodded in agreement, his mind racing. "Yin Shangren is a world spirit, a parasitic existence within the Xuanhuang Realm. Even he senses something vaguely. It seems the Xuanhuang Realm is indeed facing some calamity."

Time passed amidst great anticipation.

And unknown to all, over a hundred stone puppets had quietly flown above the Xuanhuang Realm.

They were at the boundary of the world, one step away from being drawn into the void.

Still within the scope of the Xuanhuang Realm, they would not be sucked away by the Immortal Ruins' pull.

And from this high vantage point, they could observe the macroscopic scene of the entire Xuanhuang Realm.

These puppets were naturally created by Li Ping.

They had no special purpose, merely to observe and record the Xuanhuang Realm's tremors.

The puppets floated silently in the air, awaiting the arrival of their target event.

As the predicted date of the Dharma Transmitter's forecast drew nearer.

On this day, suddenly, the main body of Li Fan in the Derivation Law Jade Token space, the Saint Fetus Li Fan outside the Chattering Abyss, the clone of Li Fan in the Boundless Mirror, and the Sacred Emperor Li Ping in the Sacred Dynasty Great Qi all felt something at the same instant.

They all looked up at the sky simultaneously.

In the lifetime of Heavenly Profound Lock Spirits, Ji Hongdao had once instantly killed cultivators of an entire province, forcing the Longevity Realm Heavenly Venerate Yi Xin to retreat to the Five Elders Council using a mutual destruction technique.

At that time, due to the sudden loss of anchor points from many cultivators, the Xuanhuang Realm lightened abruptly.

It trembled and roared.

All living beings within it sensed it, feeling as if doomsday was upon them, that they would perish at any moment.

Li Fan had personally experienced this sensation back then.

But now, this feeling was a hundred times stronger.

Boom!

Without any warning, the Xuanhuang Realm began to shake violently.

It was as if a giant was tearing the entire world apart with its bare hands.

Cracks appeared in various parts of the land, and then rapidly spread outwards. In an instant, the previously flat terrain became scarred and ravaged.

Countless mountain ranges split open, some even collapsing entirely, falling into the newly formed abysses.

If the events on the surface were not enough to instill fear in cultivators living in floating cities, then...

The changes that occurred to the white mist barrier next made all cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm tremble uncontrollably.

The white mist barrier, which seemed to span heaven and earth and remain unchanged forever, actually began to bend and break.

The white mist overflowed from its original areas and spread outwards.

Wherever it passed, it devoured the lifespans of all living beings.

The boundaries of the prefectures changed.

And through the eyes of the hundred puppets high in the sky, Li Fan could see even more clearly.

The primal energy-devouring white mist seemed to be drawn by something outside the Xuanhuang Realm, churning and surging.

However, it seemed to be constrained by some force, preventing the white mist from leaving the Xuanhuang Realm.

It was precisely due to the pulling of these two forces that the white mist barrier broke.

As heaven and earth underwent drastic changes, the spiritual energy also became violent.

Li Fan clearly saw storms, flames, lightning, and floods...

Various calamities descended below in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Fueled by the chaotic spiritual energy, their power was a hundred or even a thousand times greater than usual.

And the shaking of the Xuanhuang Realm did not stop.

This catastrophe seemed more prolonged than imagined.

The cultivators of the Immortal Alliance finally took action.

They flew out from their floating cities, appeasing the spiritual energy riots while also attempting to repair the various anomalies caused by the violent shaking of the Xuanhuang Realm.

They moved with great difficulty amidst the shaking of heaven and earth.

But there was indeed no fatal danger.

However, the shaking of the world would ultimately make the living beings within feel an uncontrollable fear.

Most cultivators could only have blank minds, praying for the disaster to pass quickly.

Beyond that, they could do nothing.

Li Fan had witnessed true world-ending scenes.

Compared to the destruction of the Xuanhuang Realm by the Immortal Ruins immortals, these minor tremors were insignificant.

Therefore, he could ignore the changes in heaven and earth and observe calmly.

"Strange..."

"The source of the suction that is causing the Xuanhuang Realm to shake..."

Li Fan suddenly felt a sense of disharmony.

With a thought, the hundred stone puppets at the edge of the world detached themselves from the boundary and floated into the boundless void.

Without the protection of the Xuanhuang Realm, the puppets were affected by the strong suction and uncontrollably moved in a certain direction.

However, as they moved further and further away from the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan also confirmed the anomaly he had sensed.

The suction causing the great tremors in the Xuanhuang Realm this time did not originate from the Immortal Ruins.

But from the depths of the Dark Star Sea!

Chapter 1176: Intentions of Deep Space Travel

Star Sea Wanderer

After the stone puppets drifted away from the Xuanhuang Realm and into the depths of the star sea, they lost contact with Li Fan.

However, the shock caused by what they observed had far from subsided for Li Fan.

"How could it be from the depths of the Dark Star Sea?"

"Could it be that another Hungry Immortal exists there?!"

Li Fan was filled with shock.

The main body in the Derivation Law Jade Token space even had to actively circulate the Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Mantra to suppress its astonishment and prevent any signs of abnormality from appearing.

For Li Fan, such an event was something that hadn't happened in a long time.

The Xuanhuang Realm continued to shake.

However, as time passed, it was clear that the amplitude of the tremors was gradually decreasing.

This inexplicable disaster was coming to an end.

But the storm of thoughts in Li Fan's mind had just begun.

"The suction of the Immortal Ruins was generated by the skeletal immortal comprehending the True Immortal rune of 'Hunger.' By sitting in meditation and forgetting oneself, he caused a devastating impact on this star region."

"But the True Immortal runes are not something only one person can comprehend. The anomaly in Xuanhuang Realm's Primordial Dao Prefecture is suspected to be related to Grand Master Tiandu comprehending the mysteries of the 'Hunger' rune technique."

"This Xuanhuang tremor has two possibilities. First, the cause of the disaster is not related to the 'Hunger' rune, but simply the consequence of an existence of the same level. Only True Immortal-level power could cause such violent impacts on the Xuanhuang Realm."

"But this means that an unknown being with True Immortal power is still hidden in the Dark Star Sea. This..."

Li Fan felt a chill down his spine.
