"The second possibility is that a survivor in the star sea, possibly even a Dharma Transmitter, is also comprehending the 'Hunger' rune technique. They recently achieved a breakthrough, thus causing this disturbance. The Dharma Transmitter Heavenly Venerate was able to transmit news in advance, so this possibility is quite high."

"But no matter which guess is correct, it cannot explain the most crucial point: why did this change happen in this lifetime?"

The Dao Dissolution Stone flashed, replaying the experiences of this lifetime repeatedly.

But he could not determine what event had caused such a significant deviation.

"Whether it's a True Immortal, or an existence capable of comprehending the 'Hunger' rune, my actions in this lifetime should not be enough to influence them."

"Yet, all this has happened."

Li Fan remained silent.

This was the consequence of reaching a certain level of strength, where even inadvertent actions could influence the outside world and even change the destinies of others. Variables gave rise to more variables, endlessly, ultimately leading to unexpected changes.

"The main body has always stayed in the Derivation Law Jade Token space, so it can be ruled out. Clone Li Ping only stirs up trouble in the Great Qi small world. Even moving the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven is not enough to cause such a great change. It must be the journey of the Saint Fetus that caused the problem."

After much deliberation, Li Fan finally pinpointed the source of the deviation to the mysterious figure at the bottom of the Chattering Abyss and the formless being in the Domain of Life and Death.

"These two, one collects world fragments, the other collects cultivator corpses. They should have been active mostly in the Dark Star Sea."

"Due to the Saint Fetus's interference, their trajectories have changed compared to previous reincarnations. Thus, the Xuanhuang tremors occurred..."

"What else is hidden in the Dark Star Sea?"

At this moment, a flicker of curiosity arose in Li Fan's heart. He had previously assumed that only the Xuanhuang Realm survived in the Dark Star Sea, and the rest was just scattered world fragments and deathly silence.

But now, it seemed there were still unknown secrets hidden there.

"Indeed. I've always had a question: in what form do the remnants of cultivation worlds exist in the Dark Star Sea? Affected by the suction of the Immortal Ruins, even complete cultivation worlds could not avoid falling towards the Immortal Ruins. These fragments should have been swallowed by the Immortal Ruins long ago, unable to resist."

"But based on the constant patching and mending of the Xuanhuang Realm, and what Han Zhong saw in the 'Tian Beast's Eye,' it can be inferred that a large number of world fragments still exist in the Dark Star Sea, in ways I do not yet understand..."

Sensing the intermittent tremors of the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan suddenly had an idea.

"Right! Previously, due to the suction of the Immortal Ruins, I couldn't escape the Xuanhuang Realm to explore the Dark Star Sea. But now, with this inexplicable suction from the depths of the Dark Star Sea's influence, perhaps..."

"There's no time to delay. The tremors are about to cease. My time is limited."

In the Broken Hand Immortal City.

During the Xuanhuang Realm tremors, even the Chattering Abyss became much quieter, emitting no disturbance.

The Azure Profound Army, which had guarded the abyss for a hundred years and could withstand the terrifying demonic sound tides, now turned pale and trembled when faced with the true terrifying catastrophe of heaven and earth.

If not for the Saint Fetus Li Fan having previously taught them the Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Mantra, many among them might have succumbed to their suppressed negative emotions, losing their minds and becoming completely insane on the spot.

Let alone the ordinary Azure Profound Army soldiers, even their leader, the Harmonious Dao cultivator Shang Shaojun, despite knowing in advance that the Xuanhuang tremors would occur, was somewhat lost and out of sorts when faced with such a catastrophe.

"I never imagined that the vast Xuanhuang Realm could also be like a small boat on a river in a storm, constantly in danger of capsizing," Shang Shaojun said with a bitter tone.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan had no time to comfort him.

"Young Commander, please quickly help me with something."

"What?" Shang Shaojun was a little slow to react, asking blankly.

"Help me prepare these items, as quickly as possible." After transmitting a list of materials to Shang Shaojun, the Saint Fetus Li Fan looked up at the sky of the Xuanhuang Realm with a serious expression.

"Gathering these materials should be no problem. Most of them are available in the Eternal Immortal Fortress. But Brother Li, what do you need these for?" Shang Shaojun looked in the direction Li Fan was looking.

"Such immense power, the entire world is as fragile as a toy before it. Doesn't Young Commander wonder?"

The Saint Fetus Li Fan's eyes were firm, even showing a hint of madness.

"I intend to fly out of the Xuanhuang Realm, trace the source, and investigate thoroughly!" he declared firmly.

"Absolutely not! Outside the Xuanhuang Realm, there is..." Shang Shaojun's expression changed drastically, and he repeatedly tried to dissuade him. He stopped halfway through, inexplicably.

"Hahaha, Young Commander, are you trying to say 'Immortal Ruins'?"

Shang Shaojun was utterly shocked, looking at the Saint Fetus Li Fan with disbelief.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan did not explain how he knew this ultimate secret. Instead, he waved his hand, his expression solemn. "Precisely because the Immortal Ruins exist, now is the rare and opportune moment!"

"Brother Li, what exactly are you..." Shang Shaojun asked, full of doubt.

"Does Young Commander think the culprit behind this catastrophe is the Immortal Ruins?" Li Fan countered.

Chapter 1177: Crossing the Dust out of Xuanhuang

Crossing the Dust to Leave Xuanhuang

"That's completely wrong!" Before Shang Shaojun could answer, the Saint Fetus Li Fan refuted him coldly.

"The source of this power is not nearby. It is in the depths of the star sea!"

"Ah?"

Hearing Li Fan's words, Shang Shaojun was astonished.

"I know Young Commander doesn't believe me. But it doesn't matter. When I successfully break free from the Immortal Ruins' shackles and fly out of the Xuanhuang Realm, you'll know I was right!"

"Please grant me your assistance, Young Commander!" The Saint Fetus Li Fan actually bowed respectfully, his face full of seriousness.

Shang Shaojun dared not accept Li Fan's bow and quickly stopped him.

"Brother Li, why are you doing this? It's just a matter of some materials. With our friendship, it's just a matter of saying the word."

"Yan Huan!" Shang Shaojun called his trusted subordinate forward and instructed him to handle the matter.

"Don't worry, everything will be ready in three days at most."

"Too slow! This is a heaven-sent opportunity, and it won't come again. One day!" the Saint Fetus Li Fan said without reservation.

Shang Shaojun pondered for a moment, then gritted his teeth. "Alright! One day it is!"

He then seemed to whisper some instructions.

After completing these tasks, he looked at Li Fan, wanting to speak yet hesitating.

"Brother Li, you are really going to..." Shang Shaojun still seemed incredulous.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan smiled slightly and explained his judgment. "The powerful force causing the Xuanhuang tremors originates from the depths of the star sea. It is completely different from the Immortal Ruins' suction that has always been drawing the Xuanhuang Realm."

"If it were in the past, rashly flying out of the Xuanhuang Realm without the world's protection, let alone cultivators like you and me at the Harmonious Dao stage, even ordinary Longevity Realm cultivators would likely only meet their demise. Perhaps only existences like Dharma Transmitter Heavenly Venerates could barely resist. But it's different now..."

Before Li Fan, a pool of water suddenly appeared.

In the center of the water, a huge vortex spun rapidly, the water flowing turbulently and swallowing everything around it.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan pointed lightly.

Outside this vortex, another vortex of the same magnitude appeared.

The forces of the two vortices interfered with each other, causing the water flow to become unstable.

Shang Shaojun instantly understood Li Fan's meaning.

"However, these are just Brother Li's speculations, right? If you guess wrong..."

"If one hears the Dao in the morning, one can die contentedly in the evening." The Saint Fetus Li Fan's face was calm, showing no fear.

"If I miss this rare opportunity, even if I survive, I will regret it for the rest of my life."

"So I must go." Li Fan's tone was resolute.

"I want to see what kind of existence possesses such immense power." His eyes shone with light.

Shang Shaojun fell silent.

The efficiency of the Azure Profound Army was trustworthy.

Within a day, all the materials Li Fan needed were prepared.

"Outside the star sea, dangers are everywhere. Brother Li, aren't you making any more preparations before crossing the star sea?" Shang Shaojun muttered inwardly.

"If there were enough time, naturally, I would build a sturdy flying ship. But time is not sufficient, is it? I can only use the Immortal Alliance's Dust Crossing Boat as a temporary substitute."

The Dust Crossing Boat was the only designated flying artifact currently used by the Immortal Alliance to travel to and from the White Mist Domain.

In the 114th lifetime, Li Fan had arrived at the Chattering Abyss with Ji Hongdao on this boat.

The Dust Crossing Boat was forged from various rare materials and possessed numerous protective formations. The Eternal Immortal Fortress only had two of them.

Being able to contribute one of them showed Shang Shaojun's true loyalty.

"However, as long as I can withstand the most intense clash point between the two forces outside the Xuanhuang Realm, there should be no danger." The Saint Fetus Li Fan seized the last moment to modify the Dust Crossing Boat.

In reality, there was one more point he had not explicitly stated. The greatest reliance for the Saint Fetus Li Fan daring to traverse the star sea was not external objects, but his own Foundation Establishment Innate Treasure, the Black Sword Heavenly Wonder!

As a manifestation of laws, the Black Sword was far more indestructible than most things in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Moreover, unlike ordinary protective materials that would gradually wear down, the Black Sword could be continuously "tempered" by external forces, making itself more adaptable.

"Thanks also to the Heavenly Venerate's new Dharma. Even if I abandon my physical body, as long as the Sword Law does not extinguish, I can survive in the void."

While full of confidence, the Saint Fetus Li Fan also considered various unexpected situations that might arise after flying out of the Xuanhuang Realm.

For example...

The laws of the Black Sword Heavenly Wonder were the embodiment of the Xuanhuang Realm's sword dao laws.

If he left the Xuanhuang Realm without the world's support, would his strength immediately decline drastically and become extremely weak?

Furthermore, the Heavenly Doctor had mentioned that outside the Xuanhuang Realm, in the void, there was a kind of "illness" to worry about.

Li Fan had seen this illness on Han Zhong.

It was dark and decaying, infecting the soul.

Even the Infinite Yin-Yang Method, used to repair the soul, had no effect on it.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan did not expect to be immune to this illness, only hoping to use large amounts of precious materials that nourished the soul to extend the time he could endure in the void.

Another day passed in a flash.

The tremors of the Xuanhuang Realm were visibly nearing their end.

The cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm showed expressions of relief at having survived, while many others remained fearful, worried that this terrifying disaster might strike again.

Outside the Chattering Abyss, the Saint Fetus Li Fan was fully prepared.

The Dust Crossing Boat was vastly different from its original appearance. Li Fan bid farewell to the Azure Profound Army members and slowly walked into the flying boat.

Looking at Li Fan's retreating figure, Shang Shaojun wanted to speak but hesitated.

He even felt an impulse to follow and, together with Li Fan, rush out of the Xuanhuang Realm to investigate the secret behind that immense power.

As cultivators, how could they not be curious about power at that level?

However...

He was not alone. He had too many people to consider.

Shang Shaojun suddenly felt envious of the figure on the Dust Crossing Boat.

"Young Commander, at this moment, do you wish to cast aside life and death with me?"

As if he could read minds, the other party suddenly transmitted a telepathic message before departing.

Without waiting for Shang Shaojun's reply, the Saint Fetus Li Fan smiled and said, "That won't do."

Shang Shaojun was slightly stunned.

"Does Young Commander not remember that there are still hidden malicious individuals plotting within the Xuanhuang Realm?"

"If both you and I leave, wouldn't we be allowing those wicked people to succeed?"

"I thought you would have already forgotten about this matter," Shang Shaojun muttered inwardly.

The Dust Crossing Boat slowly ascended.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan's voice echoed in Shang Shaojun's ears.

"The future of the Xuanhuang Realm and the Myriad Immortals Alliance rests on Young Commander's shoulders."

"If I am fortunate enough to survive this great calamity, I will definitely return to assist Young Commander!"

Shang Shaojun followed the Dust Crossing Boat as it left the white mist and watched it disappear into the horizon.

He felt a sense of loss.

Although he had not known Li Fan for long, he was deeply impressed by his strength and demeanor.

"Live well."

Shang Shaojun said inwardly.

Chapter 1178: White Day Sword Star Appears

White Day Sword Star Appears

After putting on a show in front of Shang Shaojun, the Saint Fetus Li Fan then focused his attention on observing the changes outside the Dust Crossing Boat.

At this moment, the Dust Crossing Boat had reached the boundary of the world.

The entire Xuanhuang Realm lay beneath him, fully visible.

Previously, Li Fan had observed the Xuanhuang Realm from such a perspective. However, at that time, the Xuanhuang Realm, like the world seen through the super-distance teleportation array, was shrouded in a layer of hazy yellow light, appearing like a large ball of light. The detailed scenery within the world, on the ground, was completely unclear.

But now, under the influence of the massive suction force from the depths of the star sea, that faint yellow light had been partially peeled away.

Revealing the true appearance of the world hidden beneath.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan saw the distorted white mist barrier, and...

"A monster stitched together from severed limbs and broken flesh."

This phrase suddenly appeared in Li Fan's mind.

Even from high above the nine heavens, one could still discern subtle differences between regions. While creatures within the prefectures might find it hard to distinguish, from a vantage point outside the Xuanhuang Realm, this disharmony was immediately apparent.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan quickly roused himself from his brief moment of daze.

The Dust Crossing Boat began to emit creaking sounds, a sign of being subjected to intense external pressure.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan showed no fear, disregarding the pressure and even accelerating the speed of the Dust Crossing Boat.

Upon completely breaking free from the Xuanhuang Realm, he felt the surroundings suddenly darken.

It was like dusk, where the sun had instantly set below the horizon.

Darkness, coldness, silence...

All sorts of feelings surged into the Saint Fetus Li Fan's heart.

The Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Mantra activated spontaneously, resisting these negative emotions for Li Fan.

"Compared to the imagery and the puppets' knowledge, experiencing it firsthand is truly different."

"Whether it's the puppets' synchronized sensations or the lingering influence from the Medicine King Cauldron, none are as real as this moment."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan was just thinking this when he suddenly turned his head.

In that instant, he felt an inexplicable sense of insecurity, as if something behind him would suddenly appear and deliver a fatal blow. Even though his divine sense scan clearly told him there was no danger behind him, the feeling in his heart continuously urged him to turn his head and look personally.

Only after he was certain that there was no imagined crisis did the strange feeling slowly subside.

At this moment, the Dust Crossing Boat, which had been creaking slightly before, was now making booming sounds.

It was as if countless ancient fierce beasts were constantly attacking the hull, and cracks began to appear on the boat.

The formations carved on it also began to show signs of shattering.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan was already prepared to abandon the boat.

Ninety-nine sword shadows appeared around him, swirling and circling, creating a buffer zone of absolute space.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan's body also began to wither, his flesh losing its color and taking on a strange metallic sheen.

Although the immense force from the depths of the star sea had indeed influenced the Immortal Ruins' suction to some extent,

The Immortal Ruins were still the local advantage, and some time had passed since the anomaly occurred. The unknown force in the star sea had also significantly weakened.

Therefore, the Dust Crossing Boat did not, like the previously deployed stone puppets, drift towards the depths of the star sea.

Instead, it inevitably began to fall towards the Immortal Ruins.

However...

Whether it was the curvature of the trajectory change or the magnitude of the speed alteration.

It was far from the situation when Li Fan had actively flown into the Immortal Ruins with the Medicine King Cauldron.

"My guess was correct! It truly was a rare opportunity to escape the Xuanhuang Realm!"

Seeing the Dust Crossing Boat about to shatter completely, the Saint Fetus Li Fan no longer hesitated.

"Ten Thousand Swords Like Me!" Behind him, the figures of the myriad rusted swords from the Sword Tomb vaguely appeared. Moments later, these sword shadows all merged into his body.

The dark void around the Dust Crossing Boat was illuminated, and a dazzling white light erupted from Li Fan's body.

It completely engulfed him.

Man and sword became one.

Then, as if opening the heavens and the earth, a brilliant sword light was instantly unleashed.

The Dust Crossing Boat was swallowed by the sword light and disappeared without a trace.

However, the white sword light, contrary to the Immortal Ruins' pull, resolutely moved towards the depths of the star sea!

This sword light was too bright, too dazzling.

Even from the Xuanhuang Realm sky below, a white sun-like star appeared, capable of rivaling the great sun in the sky.

At this moment, countless cultivators turned their gaze towards the location where the Saint Fetus Li Fan was.

And Shang Shaojun was instantly lost in thought, filled with a sense of loss.

The sword light, peerless, advanced rapidly.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan felt the constraints of the Immortal Ruins growing weaker.

The reason for this smooth progress was not only due to him transforming into the Black Sword Heavenly Wonder and unleashing an ultimate sword strike, but more importantly, it was due to the influence of the mysterious force from the depths of the star sea.

Outside the Xuanhuang Realm, without the interference of various laws within the world,

He could more clearly sense the remaining forces in the void.

"Unlike the Immortal Ruins' suction, which is eternal, this star sea power is like tides, intermittent and surging."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan felt waves of immense power surge towards him, even giving him the illusion that he was currently captaining a small boat, tossed about on a stormy sea.

"Hmm? Are those the stone puppets I placed earlier ahead?"

After traveling through the void for not long, the Saint Fetus Li Fan once again sensed the previously lost connection.

However, what made Li Fan's heart skip a beat was that not all the puppets were intact.

At least one-third of the puppets had disappeared for unknown reasons!

"Perhaps they were unfortunate enough not to escape the Immortal Ruins' clutches."

"But it's also possible..."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan was rapidly approaching the location of the puppets.

But suddenly, he instinctively slowed down.

Because just moments ago, another puppet had inexplicably disappeared among the remaining seventy-four!

Right before his senses and surveillance! It vanished inexplicably!

And Li Fan had no idea how that puppet had disappeared!

"The Dark Star Sea is indeed full of dangers."

A chill inexplicably surged into the Saint Fetus Li Fan's heart.

Controlling his flight speed, he let the remaining seventy-three puppets lead the way, while he followed far behind.

And subsequently, the occasional sudden disappearance of puppets demonstrated the perils of the void within the Dark Star Sea to Li Fan.

As the number of disappearing puppets increased, Li Fan gradually regained his composure.

"These puppets don't seem to have been attacked by any strange entity. Instead, it's the areas they passed through."

"There..."

"Space itself no longer exists. Only pure void remains."

"It's like one dark, bottomless cave after another on a flat road. If you accidentally step into one, you'll vanish without a trace, with no hope of recovery."

While Li Fan was contemplating this, another puppet vanished.

Only sixty-one remained.

Chapter 1179: Different Time Inside and Outside

Internal and External Time Differences

Li Fan did not know the consequences of falling into these voids, nor could he discern their existence.

He could only adopt a desperate measure, continuing to use the remaining stone puppets to scout the way, while he himself avoided the routes taken by the puppets that had inexplicably disappeared.

As the number of stone puppets continued to decrease, Li Fan's heart sank.

At this rate of attrition, he would absolutely not be able to reach the depths of the star sea in this lifetime.

But the problem Li Fan was worried about did not occur.

When only thirty-three puppets remained, after a long period of flight through the void, no more puppets suddenly disappeared.

"It seems these voids are not widespread throughout the Dark Star Sea but are densely clustered in a certain region."

"Outside the Xuanhuang Realm?" the Saint Fetus Li Fan mused.

With thirty-three puppets in front and Li Fan's sword light trailing behind,

Their speed increased, moving towards the unknown darkness ahead.

"It's going a bit smoother than I expected."

"I've already traveled a considerable distance from the Xuanhuang Realm, but my sword dao clone, formed from the Xuanhuang Realm, hasn't felt any weakening of its power."

"This is quite interesting."

Under normal circumstances, without the support of the world's power, laws wandering outside the world would inevitably be weakened to some extent.

But this weakening was not occurring now.

Even...

The bottleneck in sword dao, which had reached its limit in the Xuanhuang Realm and could not be furthered no matter how much he comprehended, had loosened just by staying in the void for a while.

Even though this Saint Fetus's talent was not exceptionally outstanding, he felt thoughts and insights uncontrollably pouring in.

It was as if he had suddenly transformed into some peerless genius.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan even felt an urge to abandon everything and focus all his energy on comprehending the Dao.

However, Li Fan forcefully suppressed it by circulating the Immortal Heart Mantra.

This abnormal phenomenon made Li Fan's imagination run wild.

"Does the entire Dark Star Sea share the same set of law systems?"

"The sword dao of the Xuanhuang Realm is only a part of the common sword dao of the entire star sea."

"Upon seeing a broader world outside the world, the upper limit is being invisibly expanded..."

"As expected, it's a place where danger and opportunity coexist."

"Perhaps the Heavenly Doctor and Dharma Transmitter frequently travel to the Dark Star Sea, and this is also part of the reason."

Recalling the Heavenly Doctor and Dharma Transmitter, Li Fan's heart grew even more serious.

After only a short stay, he had already gained such significant rewards.

It was hard to imagine what level these two, who had lived in the star sea for thousands of years, had reached.

The Heavenly Doctor's advice was indeed golden.

Even he was cautious about the "illness" in the void, yet it had descended upon the Saint Fetus Li Fan.

Without any warning.

Just as Li Fan was immersed in the joy of his impending breakthrough in sword dao comprehension, a sense of inexplicable weakness suddenly surged into his heart.

Upon internal inspection, a black spot had indeed appeared in his soul.

That black spot corroded his soul, as if it were directly occupying it.

Regardless of the precious treasures he had swallowed earlier to protect his soul, they could not stop its invasion.

And the methods prepared for nourishing his soul were also ineffective.

"The maximum strength of the soul has decreased, rather than the soul itself being damaged."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan was somewhat somber.

Fortunately, the black spot was not spreading too quickly, giving Li Fan time to take corresponding measures.

Within his soul, a sword shadow appeared.

The sword light shone, directly cutting off the portion of the soul occupied by the black spot!

And as the soul was divided, the Saint Fetus Li Fan's sword body was instantly split into two.

The part not infected by the black spot suddenly accelerated, fleeing from its original location.

The infected half stopped moving.

Sitting cross-legged in the void, concentrating on comprehending the strange blackness within his weakened soul.

The pain of splitting his soul was indescribable.

Even with the Immortal Heart Mantra's enhancement, the Saint Fetus Li Fan felt his vision darken, almost fainting on the spot.

A feeling of weakness, even greater than the erosion by the black spot, surged into his heart. He ignored the pain and weakness,

He quickly absorbed the essence of the soul-nourishing treasures he had refined earlier.

Without the inhibitory effect of the black spot, Li Fan's clean soul slowly began to strengthen again.

"This is what is called scraping the bone to heal the wound."

Li Fan sighed with emotion.

It was only because of the peculiar new Dharma, the indestructible foundation of cultivation, and the unbroken physical body. And with the Xuanhuang Sword Dao as the foundation of his cultivation,

That he could afford to cut his soul so recklessly, rather than becoming mentally impaired on the spot.

"Unfortunately, without the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven and the Infinite Yin-Yang Method, relying on external objects is ultimately not a long-term solution."

"Every time I cut, I become a little weaker than before."

"..."

"I hope I can persist until the depths of the star sea."

Li Fan closed his eyes, temporarily clearing all distracting thoughts, and began to repair the soul's injury.

Meanwhile, the other half, separated earlier and infected by the black spot, left behind in the void, had already met its ultimate end.

It was a more desperate and terrifying end than dying of old age.

Like a mortal suffering from Alzheimer's, the half that was originally comprehending the black spot, its thoughts became slower and slower.

Its mind became duller and duller, even needing a long time to recall what it wanted to do.

Even synchronized consciousness from other parts of the body seemed to be blocked by layers, unable to be understood at all.

Finally, it completely fell into a state of mental stillness.

Like the soul, it turned into absolute silence.

...

"It's like this Dark Star Sea."

In the Xuanhuang Realm, within the Derivation Law Jade Token space.

Li Fan's main body felt the image and information transmitted by the Saint Fetus, and inwardly felt a chill.

What made him frown was not the formless voids or the black spot plague in the star sea.

But the time difference between the main body and the Saint Fetus.

The Saint Fetus, having transformed into a sword, using the power of the star sea, had already traveled a considerable distance from the Xuanhuang Realm.

Therefore, Li Fan discovered that between the Xuanhuang Realm and the depths of the Dark Star Sea...

There was a discrepancy in the flow of time.

"It seems it's still influenced by the Immortal Ruins."

"Even if it's not as terrifying as the Immortal Ruins' edge, where millennia pass in an instant, it's still slower than the flow of time in other parts of the Dark Star Sea."

"Currently, it's about a one-to-two ratio."

"And as the Saint Fetus continues to move further away, this ratio is still increasing."

Li Fan couldn't help but think further.

"The Dark Star Sea within the high walls is inevitably affected by the Immortal Ruins. Whether great or small."

"Does this mean that the flow of time inside and outside the high walls is also different?"

"Is it possible that tens of thousands of years have passed since the ancient immortal road was severed in the Xuanhuang Realm?"

"While outside the high walls, it has actually been..."

"Much longer?"

Thinking of this, Li Fan couldn't help but close his eyes, concealing the faint glint within.

Chapter 1180: Wanderer of the Star Sea

Star Sea Wanderer

Although the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Council did not develop slowly during their confrontation, with various methods emerging one after another.

In reality, this period of rapid development only lasted for less than three thousand years. After the great catastrophe of the severed immortal path, for tens of thousands of years, the Xuanhuang Realm was mostly in a state of mutual killing and strife.

Civilization regressed instead of advancing.

"If my speculation is true, then I dare not imagine what kind of civilization gap would exist between the inside and outside of the high walls."

A closed civilization, deeming itself the strongest nation in the world. Then, one day, the passage to the outside world is suddenly opened, and facing the military force of an enemy that is several eras ahead, there is no power of resistance, and it quickly falls and perishes.

Such events are common in the history of civilization development.

Let alone before crossing over, even now, there are still small worlds that have lost contact with the Xuanhuang Realm and have forgotten the existence of cultivators. They have established prosperous mortal powers, and their historians have written eulogies praising their achievements.

Yet, a single Foundation Establishment cultivator can easily destroy such a "prosperous dynasty."

Li Fan's lifelong goal has always been transcendence and longevity.

For this, he has reincarnated countless times, solely to carve out a path in the Xuanhuang Realm, fraught with crises and imminent disasters.

Ultimately, he wants to leave this Dark Star Sea and go beyond the high walls.

But at this moment, the speculation about the possible existence of civilization outside the high walls made Li Fan inwardly vigilant.

"If a cultivation civilization truly exists and has developed for so many years, it might have even mastered power comparable to True Immortals, or even to some extent influence the 'Return to Truth'..."

Li Fan's gaze flickered, his thoughts churning.

However, he did not feel afraid.

'Return to Truth' is his greatest trump card.

Being able to trace back time repeatedly and bring memories and experiences back to the established anchor points, even if the outside of the high walls were infinitely ahead, he could simply equalize the gap between the two sides through a few reincarnations.

"I just need to be careful. Before the situation is clear, I will not use my clones or Saint Fetus to go out. Stability first!"

"I am not afraid of monsters outside the high walls, but I am afraid that there is nothing outside the high walls."

...

In the dark void, the Saint Fetus Li Fan, transformed into sword light, followed closely behind twenty-nine puppets.

Since he broke through the barrier and left the Xuanhuang Realm, barely half a year had passed in Xuanhuang Realm.

And from the Saint Fetus Li Fan's perspective, he had already been away from the Xuanhuang Realm for a full ten years.

The difference in time flow, as he entered deeper into the star sea, further magnified.

Not long ago, it reached its peak, a daunting fifty to one ratio.

But as the Saint Fetus Li Fan continued to advance, the time difference between his location and the Xuanhuang Realm slowly returned to convergence.

From fifty to one, it gradually decreased to ten to one.

It was not much different from when he had just left the Xuanhuang Realm.

Li Fan knew that this was because he was slowly approaching another colossal power source that distorted the flow of time.

"The star sea is vast. Even with the unknown power, my speed has reached over a hundred times the maximum speed of flying in the Xuanhuang Realm, yet it took me this long to reach my destination," the Saint Fetus Li Fan sighed faintly.

During these ten years, he had sliced up his soul more than three hundred times.

From his peak, when he could almost rival Xuanhuang Harmonious Dao cultivators, to now, possessing only the strength of an ordinary mortal.

The pain he endured, even with Li Fan's tenacious will, he did not wish to experience a second time.

Fortunately, in the last few years, perhaps because his strength had weakened to an extremely negligible level, the frequency of the black spot's infection also significantly decreased.

Moreover, after more than three hundred dissections and comprehending the insights gained, the Saint Fetus Li Fan had developed some personal methods for dealing with this inexplicable plague.

"Although I still haven't figured out the principle behind its appearance, I can be sure that this black spot is related to the destroyed and vanished cultivation worlds in the Dark Star Sea."

If it were just one of the three hundred infiltrated soul fragments, perhaps Li Fan would not have sensed anything.

But now, all these withered souls, left behind in the Dark Star Sea, all gathered together, allowing Li Fan to find their commonality.

Seemingly completely dormant, they did not remain in place.

Instead, they flowed silently towards different parts of the Dark Star Sea.

Their method of movement was quite marvelous, not normal movement in space.

It was more like water droplets naturally rolling from high places to low places, rapidly traversing the Dark Star Sea.

Upon reaching their destination, they would sequentially and permanently vanish from Li Fan's perception.

"Those locations, between the depths of the star sea and the Xuanhuang Realm, seem to overlap with the 'voids' I passed through."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan looked back and remained silent.

"It seems that all the incredible phenomena in the Dark Star Sea are interconnected."

"Then what exactly is this force, comparable to the Immortal Ruins' power? Why did I not sense it at all when I was in the Xuanhuang Realm, and only now has it suddenly erupted?"

His heart filled with confusion, Li Fan became even more curious about the unknown path ahead.

"Hmm?"

While lost in thought, he suddenly became alert and looked forward.

That illusion of being watched by something re-emerged.

And this time, it was far more intense than anything he had experienced in the past ten years.

It made the Saint Fetus Li Fan's hair stand on end and his heart pound wildly.

It was as if there was an extremely terrifying existence in the darkness ahead!

Li Fan moved his mind, first controlling a stone puppet to charge towards the source of the sensed danger.

Immediately thereafter, a sword light was unleashed from afar.

The stone puppet seemed to collide with something, emitting a muffled sound.

And then, the puppet vanished from Li Fan's perception.

As his soul was weakened, the sword light Li Fan unleashed was far less brilliant than when it first left the Xuanhuang Realm.

But it was still enough to illuminate the surrounding dark space.

A pair of enormous eyes suddenly appeared in the darkness.

Staring dead at Li Fan.

And a dried, withered, large hand had, at some unknown time, quietly reached Li Fan's front, about to capture him!

"Damn it!"

In the dark void, after more than ten years of sailing.

He had not encountered any other living beings besides himself.

Now, to suddenly encounter such a terrifying existence, Li Fan's heart suddenly pounded, and his scalp tingled.

Subconsciously, countless sword shadows flew out.

Whether it was because his power had weakened too much, or because the monster was too strong.

These sword shadows, which could cleave mountains and part seas in the Xuanhuang Realm, caused no damage at all.

Seeing that he was about to fall completely into the monster's grasp, Li Fan was about to fight to the death.

But he soon discovered something was wrong.

The giant, withered human body in front...

Showed no signs of life.

Its movements and expressions remained unchanged.

Only one chapter today.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1181: Reincarnating True Immortal Script

Encountering the True Immortal Rune Again

"Dead?" Li Fan, still shaken, felt a wave of relief.

But the lingering sense of danger in his heart told him that things were not that simple.

As expected, after the few sword lights Li Fan sent out touched the corpse in front, they vanished into the darkness like extinguished candles.

There was no sound of collision.

The giant, withered corpse, like a primordial beast hidden in the void, devoured everything that dared to approach it.

A spell illuminated the surrounding space again.

This time, the view was clearer.

The dried corpse, overall, looked similar to an ordinary human, only its size was abnormally large.

Over thirty feet tall, its hand alone was larger than Li Fan.

It seemed to have drifted in this void for a long time, its clothes already rotted.

However, after careful observation, what made the Saint Fetus Li Fan even more shocked was that this dried corpse...

Seemed to be a newborn infant.

Its hair was sparse, and its teeth had not yet grown.

A locket-like ornament hung around its neck, and a rotten red string was tied to its ankle.

Its fearful, outstretched gesture resembled a child startled and urgently seeking its parents.

"A juvenile form, and already this giant. I can hardly imagine its size when adult."

Li Fan suddenly thought of the Eternal Immortal Fortress outside the Chattering Abyss.

That fortress in the white mist was also known as the Broken Hand Immortal City.

It was because the entire fortress was built from a giant, ancient Heavenly Venerate's severed palm that floated out of the white mist.

"Perhaps there is some connection between the two," Li Fan mused inwardly.

After all, he had never seen any records of such primal giants in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Although the giant was dead, it still emanated an ominous mysterious power, dragging everything around it down.

"This mysterious power should be the culprit that caused its death and the source of my extreme unease."

The Saint Fetus Li Fan pondered for a moment, a look of determination flashing in his eyes.

Even though he no longer wanted to try, he still swung his sword at his soul, cutting off a clone.

"Ah..."

After his soul became extremely weak, his ability to endure pain also greatly diminished. Li Fan could not bear it and let out a cry of anguish.

His face turned deathly pale, and he panted heavily.

Without hesitation, he bypassed the giant corpse before him and continued to press forward towards the depths of the star sea.

And the clone left behind, after recovering for a moment, actively floated forward and touched it.

Knowing oneself and knowing the enemy, one can fight a hundred battles. It was foreseeable that for a considerable period to come, the Dark Star Sea would be a place Li Fan needed to venture into. Therefore, rather than constantly avoid these dangers in the Dark Star Sea, it was better to take the initiative and investigate thoroughly.

After all, the main body was far away in the Xuanhuang Realm, and with 'Return to Truth' as a safety net, he was not afraid of any consequences he could not bear.

The clone, separated from the giant corpse, was still some distance away when its vision went black.

It completely lost all perception of the outside world.

Its consciousness was still there, but it was as if it had been locked in a cage. It was surrounded by absolute, eternal darkness.

No sound, no light, no passage of time.

It was as if only oneself remained in the world.

Even his connection to the Saint Fetus and the main body was becoming increasingly distant and dim.

And the Saint Fetus and the main body experienced something peculiar as well.

The clone, although a part of himself, felt increasingly unfamiliar.

More importantly, the endless loneliness that enveloped the clone began to slowly erode him, following the connection between the main body and the clone. It was only then that Li Fan discovered that after being engulfed by the darkness, the clone's state seemed to be permanently fixed.

It was frozen, unable to make any moves.

It could not even commit suicide.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan's expression changed slightly, and he sent several sword lights towards the clone's location.

He wanted to sever the connection between the clone and himself.

But it was to no avail.

Like the sword light touching the giant corpse before, all attacks vanished silently.

After several attempts, he had no choice but to give up.

He frowned slightly, sensing the invasion of the endless sense of loneliness, and felt slightly relieved.

The distance in space and time still played a role in limiting this incredibly strange existence.

The main body's erosion speed was very slow.

Based on the current situation, it would not threaten his soul's safety for a hundred years.

However, the Saint Fetus, being too close, was in a precarious situation.

It was estimated that he would only last about thirty days before succumbing.

The time units here were all absolute time as experienced by each individual.

"However, as I continue to move further away, the situation will gradually improve."

"Although unavoidable, it will buy me enough time. As long as I can see the true face of the magnificent power that caused the Xuanhuang tremors, even death would be acceptable."

"Moreover, the reason the main body can sense the clone is primarily through me. If I disappear, the main body will be safe."

With this thought, the Saint Fetus Li Fan stopped his distractions and urged the remaining stone puppets, at full throttle, to speed towards the depths of the star sea.

While flying rapidly, he also contemplated the mysterious power enveloping the dried corpse he had just encountered.

The mysterious power was invading Li Fan, and Li Fan was observing it in turn.

"This feeling is not unfamiliar."

A flash of inspiration struck the Saint Fetus Li Fan, and he already had a guess.

"True Immortal Rune! Another True Immortal Rune!"

According to the Hundred Flowers Daoist's account, the calamities encountered by various realms in the Dark Star Sea were different.

Some were 'Lack,' some were 'Chaos,' some were 'Hunger'...

And what the Saint Fetus Li Fan encountered in the void now was another True Immortal Rune that caused catastrophe.

"Is it 'Solitude'? Or 'Loneliness'?"

Without seeing the physical form of the True Immortal Rune, Li Fan could not know the truth.

He could only speculate based on the external manifestation of the True Immortal Rune's power.

"True Immortal Runes, wreaking havoc across realms. Although it may not be the true body, but a copy, it still caused the demise of countless cultivation worlds in this star field."

"And among these True Immortal Runes, the 'Hunger' rune is close to the Dao path of the Immortal Ruins immortals. He gained inspiration, sat in meditation among the ruins of the immortal path, attempting to comprehend the true meaning of the 'Hunger' rune."

"For him, it was probably just a fleeting moment of enlightenment, but it created the terrifying existence of the Immortal Ruins, causing the entire star sea to sink..."

"This is the power of 'Immortals' above the mortal realm."

The Saint Fetus's thoughts churned.

"And now, not far ahead, there is an existence comparable to the power of the Immortal Ruins."

"What could it be?"

There is one more chapter due before 12:30.

Chapter 1182: Survivors of Civilization

Civilization Survivors

By comparing the flow of time with that of the Xuanhuang Realm, the Saint Fetus Li Fan could roughly estimate the distance to his destination.

When the time flow ratio between the two eventually lowered to three to one, the Saint Fetus Li Fan knew that the unknown existence he was seeking was just ahead.

On his journey, in addition to the desiccated giant corpse, he encountered other remnants from ancient shattered immortal cultivation worlds.

These included, but were not limited to, cultivators' remains and ruined structures.

Li Fan even found some magical treasures that cultivators had once used.

However, having floated in the void for too long, they had all lost their spiritual essence and were irreparable.

But judging from their crafting methods and external characteristics, they originated from various distinct immortal cultivation worlds.

These "junk" items, resembling refuse, seemed to have remained stationary in this location due to a delicate balance achieved between two forces in the void.

They were neither attracted towards the Immortal Ruins nor pulled towards the depths of the star sea, but simply lingered.

As if forgotten by the entire world.

The further he advanced, the more of this detritus from the void he encountered.

All were scattered testaments to the existence of different immortal cultivation worlds in the past.

Uncertain whether these debris were still contaminated with the power of True Immortal Runes, the Saint Fetus Li Fan dared not touch them.

He could only control his puppets and sword body, constantly evading.

Consequently, his speed inevitably slowed.

“Fortunately, my guess was correct. The closer I get to that great power of the star sea, the weaker the influence of the ‘Solitude’ technique becomes on me.”

“I have temporarily escaped the danger of being consumed.”

However…

The power of True Immortal Runes was not to be underestimated.

Although not completely eroded, the Saint Fetus Li Fan could already feel various changes in his behavior and thoughts.

For instance, a desire for reclusion would inexplicably surge in his mind, urging him to distance himself from everything.

Furthermore, the Black Sword Heavenly Wonder within his cultivation foundation subtly seemed to develop a rift with him.

From a worldly perspective, this was an utterly inconceivable matter.

After all, once the Saint Fetus Li Fan had absorbed it and integrated it into his own Dao foundation, they were as one.

Man as sword, sword as man.

Yet, the power of the True Immortal Rune could forcibly revert this integration.

“Completely and utterly alone?”

“Loneliness?”

A new anxiety subtly arose in the Saint Fetus Li Fan’s heart.

Would this power of solitude affect the main body and ‘Return to Truth’?

Although ‘Return to Truth’ possessed a sufficiently high status, the main body’s current strength was still far from satisfactory!

Even a slight possibility was a risk Li Fan could not afford to take.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan’s heart gradually solidified.

“Even if I have to waste this opportunity for exploration, I cannot allow the power of solitude to influence the main body.”

“Before any signs manifest, I must end myself beforehand.”

With this thought, the Saint Fetus Li Fan swallowed the last of his soul-nourishing treasures and activated the Soul Burning Art.

His speed suddenly surged. Amidst the scattered debris filling the void, he pierced through rapidly.

These relics from ancient immortal cultivation worlds formed an endless ocean, seemingly without end.

The nourishing power within him was almost depleted, yet he still had not managed to break free from this vast expanse of debris.

“These debris can be preserved…”

“Then, could fragments of past immortal cultivation worlds also be preserved in relatively good condition?”

While adrift in this ocean of relics, the Saint Fetus Li Fan suddenly recalled the actions of Transmission and Heavenly Doctor in transporting world fragments from the star sea and patching up the Xuanhuang Realm.

“Who is it?” Just as he was lost in thought, Li Fan’s heart suddenly tightened. He had actually sensed a divine sense locking onto him in the void!

He shouted out, looking towards the source of the lock.

The locking sensation vanished instantly, revealing only a blurred figure, flickering rapidly and disappearing into the darkness.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan’s face darkened as he arrived at the location where the figure had previously appeared.

“Not some mysterious, bizarre entity, but a living person?”

“In the pitch-dark star sea, besides the Xuanhuang Realm, there are other immortal cultivation civilizations that have survived?”

The Saint Fetus Li Fan was utterly shaken.

Not only because he sensed the figure’s aura, but more importantly, the figure had voluntarily left behind a message.

To Li Fan, it seemed somewhat inexplicable, not an obvious divine sense message that only cultivators could use.

“Bing San, Seven Days of the First Month?”

“Jiu?”

Li Fan gazed at these short phrases, falling into deep contemplation.

“It should be some kind of code. But with this universal script of immortal cultivation, it’s undoubtedly a surviving cultivator.”

Although he had not yet encountered the great power of the star sea that caused the Xuanhuang Realm’s tremors, knowing that there were other sparks of civilization in the star sea was already of immense significance to Li Fan.

“To survive in the pitch-dark star sea for so many years, besides having enough resources for survival, the most crucial factor is the ability to resist the Immortal Ruins’ suction. And this place, situated at a subtle balance point between the two forces, has created a safe zone.”

“This also indicates…”

The Saint Fetus Li Fan’s gaze flickered. He looked at the divine sense message of the unknown cultivator, cautiously refraining from replying.

“The great power of the star sea, capable of contending with the Immortal Ruins, did not suddenly appear recently.”

“But due to some unforeseen event, it suddenly erupted intensely, thus being sensed by the Xuanhuang Realm, which is far from the Immortal Ruins.”

“…”

The figures of the Immortal Ruins and Heavenly Venerate Transmission appeared once more in Li Fan’s mind.

These two, having traveled extensively in the star sea, could not possibly be unaware of this.

“Interesting.”

Because of the power of solitude, the Saint Fetus Li Fan’s heart, which had grown somewhat cold, re-ignited with a restless curiosity upon learning of this new spark of civilization.

However, he forcefully suppressed it.

“Even without direct contact, surviving in such a harsh environment clearly indicates they are not easy to get along with.”

“Moreover, the laws in the Dark Star Sea are even more complete than those in Xuanhuang. The upper limit is higher. These people have been here for so long…”

“Their strength should not be underestimated.”

However, Li Fan did not worry about the Xuanhuang Realm.

The Xuanhuang Realm was teeming with monsters, and with the addition of Heavenly Venerate Transmission’s new Dharma,

And within this sea of ruins, resources were scarce. If a conflict were to erupt between the two sides, the Xuanhuang Realm would undoubtedly crush them.

“Perhaps I am overthinking. The distance is so great; without a fortunate coincidence, even meeting would be a luxury.”

Temporarily setting aside the idea of a cage match between the two surviving civilizations of the Dark Star Sea,

Li Fan’s immediate problem was that his remaining time was running out.

Should he continue advancing into the depths of the sea of ruins to find the source of the star sea’s great power?

Or should he try to establish contact with the civilization here?

Without lengthy contemplation, after a brief pause, the Saint Fetus Li Fan made his decision.

He chose the latter.

“They have lived here for a long time and are bound to have a greater understanding of that great power of the star sea.”

“Instead of wandering aimlessly like a headless fly, it is better to ask for directions.”

The Saint Fetus Li Fan’s eyes flickered.

Chapter 1183: The Sea of Relics Hides Mysteries

Secrets Hidden in the Sea of Ruins

Although he had decided to seek information about the great power of the star sea from this other surviving civilization, the Saint Fetus Li Fan did not rashly approach them.

After all, he had traveled across half the Dark Star Sea, constantly severing his divine soul to resist the erosion of the void’s black spot plague, resulting in a significant weakening of his strength.

If his attempt to gather information failed and he was instead captured alive by them, wouldn’t that be a colossal joke?

“This place can support a surviving civilization, so they likely have methods to avoid the various anomalies that invade the void. I will first lie in wait secretly, slowly recover my strength, and then make plans.”

In an instant, the Saint Fetus Li Fan devised his strategy.

First, he pointed to his own brow, creating a restriction within his already extremely weak divine soul. Should anything go wrong, he could instantly extricate himself, scattering his soul into oblivion.

Only then did Li Fan conceal his form and begin exploring this ocean of relics.

He did not follow the sneaky figure he had encountered earlier, fearing it might be a trap to lure him into a dangerous area. The Saint Fetus Li Fan chose a different direction and ventured deeper.

“The void is fraught with peril. If there are cultivators hiding, they would surely rely on formations, restrictions, and the like for protection. As long as I can find these traces, I can follow them. My mastery of formations is generations ahead of Xuanhuang Realm, so I should be unrivaled here as well.”

This was Li Fan’s initial thought.

However, after searching the ocean of relics for more than ten days, he found no sign of formations or any other signs of civilization. He hadn’t even sensed a trace of life.

This led the Saint Fetus Li Fan to doubt whether the shadowy figure he had encountered earlier was just an illusion.

But he did not give up easily, like a patient hunter lurking in the shadows, waiting for his prey to appear.

Seventeen more days passed, and he finally had a breakthrough.

A small team of three cultivators, clad in strange armor, moved cautiously back-to-back.

The way they appeared was also quite unexpected.

The surrounding desolate relics floating in the void shifted, and a passage materialized out of thin air.

After the three emerged, the desolate relics returned to their original positions, and the entrance to the passage closed.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, surveying the area. He observed all the cultivator relics near them.

After a moment, he understood.

“Brilliant! It’s not an isolated formation, but one modified based on these naturally floating relics, almost completely integrated with the surrounding environment.”

“More importantly…”

The Saint Fetus Li Fan slowly approached these floating relics.

“These items from shattered immortal cultivation worlds are, to varying degrees, contaminated with the power of True Immortal Runes. This forms a natural protection, able to maximally shield cultivators’ divine senses from perceiving them. This is also why I searched so diligently before but still couldn’t find their hiding place…” Li Fan instantly understood.

In reality, the sophistication of this formation was average. However, by incorporating the power of the True Immortal Runes that caused the destruction of various realms, its level had dramatically increased. Even with Li Fan’s current array mastery, he had no easy way to break it.

Of course, if he were to disregard the potential side effects of those relics and forcibly break the formation, he could still do it. However, this would contradict his initial plan of lurking and gathering information.

Li Fan glanced at the concealed entrance to the passage and ultimately abandoned the idea of forcing his way in.

Instead, he followed behind the three, observing them meticulously.

Aside from their peculiar armor, these three cultivators looked no different from people from the Xuanhuang Realm.

Their excursion seemed to be for the purpose of collecting supplies in this ocean of relics.

However, the items they sought were somewhat strange to Li Fan.

They did not seem to have any commonality; they collected everything from fragments of magical treasures to building ruins, and even some withered cultivator bones.

Instead of storing them directly in spatial rings, they tied them together with a black rope and dragged them behind.

“This scene…” Li Fan was momentarily stunned.

It reminded him of Transmission’s act of moving world fragments with golden chains in the void.

“Could there be some connection?”

After a little more than half a day, when the number of relics tied behind them had reached more than twenty, the three cultivators seemed divided.

However, under the leadership of the one at the front, they eventually abandoned their search.

Carrying their haul, they turned and flew towards the passage entrance.

Li Fan, concealing himself, followed discreetly.

The range these three cultivators ventured out seemed to have a limit; they did not stray far from their hiding place. Soon, they arrived back at the hidden passage.

Then, the armor of one of them suddenly began to flash with rhythmic light.

Li Fan sensed a peculiar wave of rhythm emanating from the armor.

As if triggering some mechanism, the surrounding desolate relics shifted rapidly, and a circular entrance quietly appeared.

The three cultivators, pulling their more than twenty items together, flew into it.

Li Fan also concealed his form, intending to enter with them.

Unexpectedly, as he approached the passage entrance, a shrill alarm suddenly sounded.

Li Fan’s heart leaped. He attached one of his prepared divine sense clones to one of the items.

He himself rapidly retreated far behind.

Because of the clone’s presence, the alarm did not cease as the Saint Fetus Li Fan withdrew.

The three cultivators nervously scanned their surroundings, but finding no signs of an intruder, they turned their attention to the items they had collected this time.

After a short discussion, they separated these items and tried to bring them in one by one.

Eventually, they found the one Li Fan’s clone was attached to.

Instead of destroying it, they forcefully hurled it towards the depths of the ocean of relics.

With the source of the threat gone, the warning sound ceased.

The three then turned and returned.

Not far away, watching the slowly closing passage entrance, Li Fan ultimately chose not to force his way in.

“Interesting. Their warning system could actually detect me.”

His eyes gleaming, he approached the relic that had been thrown away.

“As expected, there’s something peculiar. On the surface, the influence of the True Immortal Rune remains. But in reality, the attached power has become extremely weak.”

“After such a long time, my weak divine sense clone has not suffered any damage…”

Retrieving his clone, Li Fan picked up the relic and examined it again.

It appeared to be a banner-like magical treasure, but the flag itself was rotted, leaving only a bare pole.

Having lost its spiritual essence, it could no longer exert its original abilities.

“Why are they collecting these things?”

Chapter 1184: The Origin Power of Immortality

The Power of Immortal Origin

The material of this banner-like magical treasure was also ordinary. In this ocean of relics, it had no particular value that would warrant special selection.

“Could it be for the True Immortal Rune power attached to it, whose side effects have already dissipated?”

A thought struck Li Fan, and he instantly understood.

He slowly stroked the banner, sensing a familiar aura.

“‘Chaos’ Rune…”

“However, with the passage of time, even the power of True Immortal Runes eventually reaches its end.”

The complete character ‘Chaos’ flashed in his mind. A moment later, the Saint Fetus Li Fan’s hand, holding the banner, stiffened slightly.

Because he discovered that, at this very moment, the last trace of power attached to the banner had completely vanished.

In its place, his comprehension of the ‘Chaos’ Rune had subtly deepened!

This progress was very minute.

However, Li Fan’s own understanding of the ‘Chaos’ Rune was merely at the basic level of imitation, making the improvement relatively noticeable. It was instantly captured by Li Fan.

“It can actually serve as a material for comprehending the Dao?”

The Saint Fetus Li Fan was somewhat shaken. His gaze now fell upon the countless floating relics in this place with a completely different perspective.

“It’s a pity, though. It seems only relics with the power of True Immortal Runes on the verge of dissipation can serve as such Dao-comprehension material. Otherwise, there’s a risk of harm. The method to distinguish them…”

The Saint Fetus Li Fan’s gaze shifted towards the concealed hiding place.

For the next half a year, Li Fan remained hidden in the shadows. Each time cultivators ventured out to collect relics, he followed the same procedure.

He sent out his divine sense clones, attaching them to the collected relics.

One purpose was to study the method by which the alarm was triggered, and the other was to acquire any relics suitable for Dao comprehension related to True Immortal Runes.

In the Xuanhuang Realm, the Ever-Ending Dissolution Disc within the main body’s sea of consciousness was working at full capacity, deciphering the unknown formations.

Meanwhile, based on his research of the eight acquired relics, the Saint Fetus Li Fan became even more convinced of his judgment.

The other surviving civilization in this Dark Star Sea was collecting these relics precisely to study, and perhaps even utilize, the power of True Immortal Runes.

“They’ve actually developed a means to discern the degree of this power…”

“It seems their strength should not be underestimated.”

Of these eight relics, three were related to ‘Chaos,’ and two were related to ‘Hunger.’

As for the remaining two, they were influenced by other True Immortal Runes, currently unknown.

Li Fan also discovered the difference between them.

He had personally witnessed the original forms of the ‘Chaos’ and ‘Hunger’ True Immortal Runes. Even though they were counterfeit replicas, they provided a general understanding of their essence. Thus, he could smoothly absorb the residual power on the Dao comprehension relics and convert it into material for Dao comprehension.

The situation with the other two relics was vastly different.

With only the residual power on the verge of dissipation, it was difficult to even sense their nature, let alone comprehend their essence.

Their efficiency in being utilized, compared to ‘Chaos’ and ‘Hunger,’ was less than ten thousandfold!

“This is the difference between ‘from top to bottom’ and ‘from bottom to top.’ Knowing the original intent of the True Immortal Runes, one can understand everything from a superior position.”

“But starting from ignorance, like a blind person touching an elephant, exploring and researching slowly on one’s own…”

“It’s as difficult as ascending to heaven! With mortal power, trying to probe True Immortal power…”

At the same time, Li Fan mused.

“Not all cultivators have enough fortune to personally witness the original intent of True Immortal Runes.”

“The ‘Chaos’ Rune was hidden in the Reversing Manifestation Domain within the White Mist, something an ordinary person might never encounter in their lifetime. The ‘Hunger’ Rune, furthermore, was inscribed upon the Immortal Ruins! To see it meant death. If not for my ‘Return to Truth,’ I would never have been able to master it.”

“And the ‘Nothingness’ Rune, I coincidentally discovered it within a golden skull of a destroyed minor world…”

Li Fan looked at the unknown civilization hidden in the darkness, and a thought naturally arose.

“‘Rare goods are often hoarded.’ The value of these original intents in this civilization might be even higher than I imagined.”

…

More than thirty days later, the Ever-Ending Dissolution Disc finally broke through the means that triggered the alarm.

As a precaution, the Saint Fetus Li Fan did not venture in himself.

Instead, he still used his divine sense clone to test the waters.

Over the past half-year, although he had severed many divine souls, the vicinity of this civilization’s hiding place seemed to contain a peculiar power.

It could resist all sorts of strange invasions from the void, allowing the Saint Fetus Li Fan to recover quickly.

Severing his divine souls had become merely a slight discomfort.

The Ever-Ending Dissolution Disc was indeed trustworthy.

This time, the relic with the attached divine sense clone successfully passed the inspection and entered the passage.

The psychic connection became much weaker, but he could still vaguely sense the situation inside the hiding place.

The three cultivators continued to drag the collected relics with a black rope, passing through three layers of passage defenses before finally reaching a safe zone.

They eagerly took off their armor, complaining continuously.

“There are fewer usable relics near the Immortal Vessel. We only found this much this time…”

“The next mission will likely require us to venture outside the safe zone.”

“We’ve been stationed here for a hundred years? I don’t know why we haven’t moved yet.”

“It is said there was originally a plan to change our docking location, but recently…”

“Hush, it’s better to discuss it less. Wu Xing was confined for ten years because of this matter.”

The three wisely avoided discussion.

Taking their spoils, they continued deeper into their hiding place.

“Immortal Vessel?” Li Fan heard their conversation and mused.

After passing through a narrow, dark passage, the view ahead suddenly opened up.

They had arrived in a serene mountain valley with clear waters.

An elder with white hair, holding a peculiar book-like artifact, was waiting for the three of them.

“Let me see this time…” The elder’s face was initially smiling, but upon seeing the quantity of relics behind the three, it immediately turned grim.

“Elder Gu, please forgive us. Our luck was truly poor on this outing,” the oldest-looking cultivator among the three said with a wry smile.

The elder shook his head, sighed, and ultimately said no more.

A beam of light emanated from the book-like artifact in his hand, enveloping all the relics.

As the beam retracted, it seemed the inspection of the relics was complete.

“Try to make up for it next time.”

“You know the situation with the Immortal Vessel. If we consistently fall short by one or two items each time, it might be acceptable for a while. But if it goes on for too long, who will suffer if not all of us?” the elder snorted.

The elder cultivator did not retort, only nodding repeatedly.

“Take these relics to the ‘Immortal Severing Pavilion’ for me,” the elder then instructed.

Chapter 1185: Dark Gold Three-Eyed Skull

The Dark Gold Three-Eyed Skull

Upon hearing the elder’s request, the three cultivators were all slightly stunned.

“Elder Gou, this is against the…”

“Hmm?” The elder heard this and immediately gave the three a cold scrutiny.

The three could only swallow their words and retreat.

Under duress, the eldest cultivator cupped his hands and, still dragging the relics, left the valley.

On the way.

“Brother Zhao, the Immortal Vessel’s laws clearly stipulate that collected world-ending relics must be submitted to the ‘Immortal Pivot Court.’ Violators will be punished for treason. Now he wants us to take them to the Immortal Severing Pavilion…”

“Exactly! Everyone on the Immortal Vessel knows that the Immortal Severing Pavilion and the Immortal Pivot Court are at odds. That old fellow wants to curry favor with the Immortal Severing Pavilion but won’t do it himself, simply ordering us around. If something happens, we’ll definitely not escape.”

The elder cultivator, addressed as Brother Zhao by the other two, also had an unpleasant expression, but he did not join the complaints. Instead, he gestured with his eyes, signaling the two to quiet down.

Afterward, he seemed to transmit something secretly, and only then did the two become obedient.

The three did not fly, but walked step-by-step along a small path out of the valley.

The scenery before them suddenly changed, as if returning to the void of the star sea.

However, this void was not as cold and dead as the outer Dark Star Sea.

A gentle breeze blew from the void, carrying a sense of vitality.

Faint colorful star points could be seen flashing intermittently in a trance.

Contrasting this harmonious and warm scene was an extremely bizarre sight: a colossal giant, standing tall in the void.

Its eyes were tightly closed, its body desiccated, like a zombie that had died long ago.

But its chest continued to rise and fall, its breaths stirring up warm winds that blew in all directions.

If it were merely a dying giant, all would be well. But what was horrifying was that a thick branch extended from the giant’s mouth.

It grew upward tenaciously, forming a dense canopy.

Looking closer, branches pierced the giant’s body from all over. And the giant’s lower body had already transformed into dense, intertwined root systems.

They swayed with the wind from time to time, as if alive.

This bizarre scene, whether it was a tree parasitizing a human or a human transforming into a tree.

The three were long accustomed to this sight, merely sighing, “It looks like this ‘Path-Chasing’ giant is almost finished. I wonder what the Immortal Pivot Court will come up with next.”

“The Immortal Severing Pavilion talks a better game than they sing, claiming to completely solve the energy deficiencies of the Immortal Vessel. They’ve been saying this for so long, yet they still haven’t produced any effective results.”

“Let’s wait and see. It’s said they’ve finally made a revolutionary breakthrough this time; otherwise, that dog elder wouldn’t have shown such favor all of a sudden.”

…

The few chatted casually.

After leaving the valley and flying into the void, a streak of green suddenly appeared beneath their feet, forming an aerial path to other locations.

Without needing to fly, this green path was already moving rapidly.

Once in the void, the overall appearance of the Immortal Vessel finally came into view.

It was like a collection of myriad stars, with countless floating continents distributed everywhere.

Giants parasitized by strange trees in the void.

Innumerable green thread-like paths extended from the giant trees, appearing and disappearing, connecting the various continents.

Li Fan’s divine sense clone, hidden within the ‘World-Ending Relics,’ secretly observed all of this.

This form of immortal cultivation civilization, so different from the Xuanhuang Realm, piqued his interest.

“Immortal Vessel…”

“When the ancestor of the Medicine King Sect, Sun Piao Miao, traveled beyond the heavens, he recorded beacon information for eighteen immortal cultivation worlds. Among them was a colossal flying ship that roamed erratically in the void, trading between worlds. Its interior formed a world of its own, named ‘Xuan Shang.’”

“I wonder if there’s any relation to this Immortal Vessel.”

Li Fan then looked at the giant whose life force was being continuously extracted, radiating vitality outwards: “The Path-Chasing race?”

The formless green path moved extremely fast in the void. The Zhao-Surname cultivator and his companions arrived at the so-called Immortal Severing Pavilion not long after.

A circular orb of dark gold light.

Upon closer inspection, it too was built upon the skeletal remains of a giant.

However, this time it was not a complete body, but a single, colossal skull.

What made Li Fan’s heart tremble was that in the center of this skull, there was a glaring eyeball!

The eyeball had not lost its vitality with the skull’s death.

It was merely closed, still subtly rotating.

An inexplicable sense of crisis arose in Li Fan’s heart. Li Fan’s divine sense clone decisively escaped from the World-Ending Relic he was attached to.

He merely remained in the void, not following the three into the Immortal Severing Pavilion.

His judgment was correct.

The giant eyeball suddenly opened, scanned the surroundings. Finding nothing unusual, it closed again.

Only then did the Zhao-Surname cultivator and his two companions enter the Immortal Severing Pavilion.

Li Fan’s divine sense clone no longer focused on the three-eyed skull, but patiently waited outside the Immortal Severing Pavilion in the void for them to return.

“Dark gold skull, three eyes.”

“It resembles the one I discovered the ‘Nothingness’ Rune on. But this one in the Immortal Vessel…”

“Seems a bit weaker?”

It wasn’t that bigger automatically meant stronger.

The dark gold three-eyed skull Li Fan had encountered previously, even though its third eye was gone and it had purely become a breeding ground for the ‘Nothingness’ Rune’s gray mold, still gave Li Fan an extremely dangerous feeling. It seemed capable of reviving at any moment. Thus, Li Fan had kept it sealed with multicolored divine light, not daring to foolishly research it.

The skull before him, though even larger, and with a living eyeball,

Gave Li Fan the impression that it was utterly dead and had no chance of revival.

This was an unfathomable sensation.

“I haven’t encountered many things outside the Xuanhuang Realm in my past reincarnations, and yet here, not long after arriving, I’ve encountered almost all of them.”

“It seems this Immortal Vessel truly has some depth…”

“Without complete world resources, they must inevitably obtain survival necessities from the Dark Star Sea, making use of everything. It seems the foundation of this Immortal Vessel may far exceed my imagination…”

Li Fan’s thoughts churned, constantly calculating where to find an entry point.

From the conversation of the three cultivators earlier, he learned that the Immortal Vessel was currently caught in a power struggle between the Immortal Pivot Court and the Immortal Severing Pavilion.

This situation was favorable to Li Fan, an outsider.

“Only in chaos can one fish. I must find a way to make this Immortal Vessel stir things up a bit.”

Not long after, the Zhao-Surname cultivator and his two companions emerged from the Immortal Severing Pavilion.

Contrary to their disgruntled demeanor on the way there, they were now all beaming with suppressed excitement in their eyes.

Standing on the formless green path, reaching the center of the void, they finally began to discuss heatedly.

“I never expected the Immortal Severing Pavilion to actually find a way to utilize the power of world-ending remnants!”

“The relics in the void are endless. Now we truly don’t have to worry about running out of energy!”

“Now we can watch the show!”

Chapter 1186: Destroying Souls Invisibly

Soul Annihilation in the Formless

“Yes, the Celestial Pivot Court has always disagreed with research on world-ending power. For countless years, they’ve aggressively suppressed it. Who knows how many cultivators have become nourishment for the ‘Divine Tree’ because of it? If they hadn’t been utterly unable to hold on in recent years, I don’t think they would have compromised.”

“Thinking about it, the Immortal Severing Pavilion made such significant progress in just over five hundred years. The Celestial Pivot Court held power for nearly ten thousand years and achieved nothing, causing the Immortal Vessel to decline day by day. The Celestial Pivot Court truly deserves death.”

“The sky of the Immortal Vessel is about to change. We brothers should make our plans early. Perhaps with this opportunity, we can even shed our status as condemned criminals…”

The three exchanged glances, seeing the ambition in each other’s eyes.

However, their whispered words stopped in the deserted void.

Upon returning to the original valley, they fell silent and appeared disgruntled once more.

After reporting to Elder Gou, they settled into the wooden huts within the valley.

A total of one hundred cultivators resided here.

Periodically, some of them would venture out of the Immortal Vessel to collect world-ending relics.

The people of the Immortal Vessel seemed extremely fearful of the outer Dark Star Sea. Before each mission, they appeared visibly anxious.

And the task of collecting relics did indeed have a high fatality rate.

It wasn’t due to any direct harm encountered in the outer star sea, but rather, their lifespans seemed to be significantly reduced with each excursion.

Zhao Tianjiang, the cultivator with the surname Zhao, showed noticeably deeper wrinkles on his face after two outings.

“No wonder I haven’t seen any young cultivators here. They’re all middle-aged and elderly,” Li Fan mused inwardly.

The hundred-odd people in the valley did not cultivate on a daily basis.

Other than undertaking the mission to collect world-ending relics, they had no other duties.

From their daily idle conversations, Li Fan gathered a considerable amount of information about the Immortal Vessel.

This valley was called the “Sin Suppression Valley,” a place of exile for cultivators who violated the Immortal Vessel’s laws but whose crimes were not severe enough for execution.

Collecting world-ending relics was a means to atone for their sins.

Once they fulfilled their contributions, they could leave this place and resume their normal lives.

Through their hopeful words, Li Fan glimpsed the daily lives of the Immortal Vessel’s inhabitants.

All matters, large and small, on the Immortal Vessel were managed by the “Immortal Pivot Court.”

Ordinary Immortal Vessel inhabitants did not have to worry about survival; the Immortal Pivot Court provided a fixed amount of provisions annually.

But these were just enough to sustain life.

The Immortal Vessel had strict controls over its total population and the number of cultivators.

Not only did one need approval to procreate, but cultivation was also strictly regulated with fixed quotas.

Besides obtaining cultivation qualifications through a lottery, one could also achieve it by making outstanding contributions to the Immortal Vessel.

For instance, by venturing out to retrieve world-ending relics.

In this Sin Suppression Valley, most individuals had no cultivation.

This was why they exhibited such great fear towards venturing out.
