As mortals, they could move freely in the Dark Star Sea and remain immortal only because of the secret Immortal Pivot Court’s immortal armor worn during their missions.

Besides ensuring their personal safety, this armor could also identify which relics were qualified and could be exchanged for merits.

As for the ultimate purpose of the Immortal Pivot Court in collecting these world-ending relics…

The common folk of the Immortal Vessel naturally had no idea.

…

“It seems the Immortal Vessel is even more stratified than the Xuanhuang Realm.”

“There is limited information to be gathered here. I need to find a way to leave this place.”

His divine sense clone’s strength was currently too weak to withstand any depletion.

It was almost impossible for him to cross the Immortal Vessel’s void independently.

And the strange green, formless paths in the void only appeared with permission; anyone attempting to approach the void without authorization would be shattered and become fodder for the Immortal Vessel.

Therefore, Li Fan’s divine sense clone remained hidden, waiting for an opportunity.

However, instead of an opportunity, what he waited for was a catastrophe.

The cause was that Zhao Tianjiang and the other two cultivators he had been lurking near suddenly fell ill.

Initially, Zhao Tianjiang thought he was just tired and stayed in bed for several days.

Later, he couldn’t sleep at all and began to feel itchy all over, unable to sit still.

Zhao Tianjiang seemed to recall something, and endless fear flooded his eyes.

However, he did not share this with others.

He even suppressed his discomfort, appeared before everyone a few times, and voluntarily submitted a request to go out and collect relics.

It wasn’t until he began coughing uncontrollably, and black spots appeared on his skin, that Zhao Tianjiang hid himself in his house and refused to come out.

Holding a jade-like artifact, he was engrossed in something unknown.

Later, blood continuously flowed from all seven orifices, and the smell of blood began to spread. Only then could the situation no longer be concealed.

“Alas. His time is running out. It’s best to send him back quickly to reunite with his family.”

“Truly, fate is unpredictable. Old Zhao was the most physically fit among us, yet he still couldn’t avoid contracting the void’s strange illness.”

“He even concealed his condition, all for the sake of earning more merits for young Zhao before his death…”

Everyone sighed, displaying a sense of shared misfortune.

Elder Gou, however, showed no emotional fluctuation, merely carrying out his duty and sending Zhao Tianjiang away.

Soon, the Immortal Vessel sent someone to Sin Suppression Valley to replace Zhao Tianjiang.

After Zhao Tianjiang’s death, the other two cultivators who had been with him soon exhibited symptoms and tragically perished.

In Sin Suppression Valley, everyone lamented their bad luck.

However, only Li Fan knew that their successive deaths from the so-called void’s strange illness were likely due to his divine sense clone’s prolonged proximity.

“The bodies of these Immortal Vessel inhabitants…”

“Are so fragile. They can’t even withstand a bit of void aura carried by my divine sense clone. If my main body were to enter, wouldn’t it become a destructive source of contagion?”

Li Fan was somewhat speechless.

The fact that he had caused the deaths of three individuals was not intentional.

It was simply because he had traveled across half the Dark Star Sea and spent too long in the void.

His divine soul had likely become contaminated with certain mysterious powers of the void.

Although his own divine soul was resilient and immune to these strange powers, fragile Immortal Vessel inhabitants might not be so lucky.

In Sin Suppression Valley, it was as if ten years passed in a single day.

The entire Immortal Vessel seemed like stagnant water, utterly devoid of movement.

The opportunity Li Fan’s divine sense clone was waiting for never arrived.

Until one day…

Elder Gou, who had always been stern and unsmiling, suddenly changed his demeanor.

He summoned all the personnel of Sin Suppression Valley.

They were all marched out of the valley, apparently awaiting the arrival of some important figure.

The valley inhabitants were filled with apprehension, while Li Fan’s divine sense clone sensed a powerful aura rapidly approaching from afar.

“Harmonious Dao stage?”

“More than that. But not as oppressive as the Longevity Realm.”

“Hmm? And it seems to contain a trace of True Immortal Rune power?”

Chapter 1187: Sneaking into the Immortal Ship Alone

Infiltrating the Immortal Vessel Alone

“It’s the ‘Hunger’ Rune…”

From the Harmonious Dao cultivator of the Immortal Vessel nearby, Li Fan’s divine sense clone quickly made a judgment based on the faint fluctuations.

He did not approach closely, but observed from within the wooden hut.

“Elder Yan…” Elder Gou, who was normally stoic, was now bowing and acting obsequiously towards Elder Yan.

The valley inhabitants grumbled inwardly but dared not show it, even lowering their heads to avoid looking directly at the Harmonious Dao cultivator.

After all, to mortals, Harmonious Dao cultivators were almost like legendary immortals.

“Gou Lang, I heard that five people died in Sin Suppression Valley recently?” Elder Yan asked sternly.

Gou Lang trembled and repeatedly replied, “Indeed, such a thing happened. But it was just those few sinners’ bad luck; they only went out to work two or three times before their conditions worsened and they died. The Sin Suppression Valley itself has not experienced any major disturbances…”

“Hmph! What luck…” Elder Yan’s eyes flashed with a cold glint, offering no further explanation.

His vast divine sense instantly enveloped the entire Sin Suppression Valley.

“As expected, this place has been contaminated.”

Elder Yan’s expression instantly turned grim. He conjured a speck of starlight at his fingertip and pointed it towards Li Fan’s divine sense clone’s dwelling area in Sin Suppression Valley.

Boundless light and heat instantly annihilated everything within the area.

…

Outside the Immortal Vessel.

The Saint Fetus Li Fan, who was in seclusion and comprehension, slightly raised his head.

“As expected of a civilization that has survived in the Dark Star Sea for so long; they are so cautious.”

“It seems that if I want to infiltrate, I need to solve the problem of being a major source of contagion myself. Otherwise, no matter how well I hide, causing a mass death of those around me will inevitably expose me.”

“My divine soul has been in the Dark Star Sea for too long, and the contamination is too deep. I still need to sever a wisp of divine soul to infiltrate. With the previous experience, I can do it this way…”

For the next two full months, no one from the Immortal Vessel went out to collect world-ending relics.

But faced with the seemingly endless relics outside the Immortal Vessel, they obviously could not give up.

Thus, Li Fan finally waited for a new scavenging team.

Following the previous experience, Li Fan’s divine sense clone, mixed with the relics, entered the Immortal Vessel.

However, this time, the Immortal Vessel’s processing of the relics was clearly much more cautious. While in proximity to the relics, the Immortal Vessel cultivators consistently wore their armor. After transporting the relics to a sealed space, a blurry illusory talisman appeared above the space after they left.

“This is…”

The talisman emitted a faint radiance, shining upon the dozen or so relics below.

Li Fan’s divine sense clone, also bathed in the light, was unaffected.

He merely watched as the power of the True Immortal Runes, on the verge of dissipation, attached to the surrounding relics, was absorbed into the illusory talisman above through this dreamlike radiance.

Li Fan’s divine sense clone even felt that the various mysterious powers surrounding him were being drawn away by the talisman.

It did not take long for the power attached to the dozen or so relics here to completely disappear, turning them into worthless junk from the star sea.

The talisman flashed with a faint light and left this space.

“The Immortal Vessel’s utilization of the power of True Immortal Runes is slightly higher than I imagined.”

This space was completely sealed, and Li Fan’s divine sense clone could not escape. However, he was not in a hurry.

Someone would eventually handle these leftover “junk.”

As Li Fan had predicted, two days later, two Qi Refining stage cultivators entered, led by a Foundation Establishment stage cultivator.

“Move all these items onto the ship.”

“Be careful, everyone. Although the world-ending power on these items is gone, they are still genuine ancient artifacts. If they could survive in the star sea for so long, it means their material itself is quite extraordinary. Send them all to the ‘Star Forging Workshop.’ Perhaps they can be repurposed.” the Foundation Establishment cultivator instructed.

The two Qi Refining cultivators were only about fifteen or sixteen years old, appearing quite naive.

Li Fan’s divine sense clone pondered for a moment, attached himself to one of them, and followed the three, leaving the sealed space. They took a small flying boat to the so-called “Star Forging Workshop.”

It was a sealed, annular building constructed from an unknown white metal.

In the center of the ring was a scorching fireball.

The terrifying heat waves constantly churning on the surface of the fireball spoke of the immense energy contained within.

One could vaguely see wisps of flame being drawn into a small hole in the annular building.

The person in charge of reception at the Star Forging Workshop was not a human.

Instead, it was a strange half-human, half-beast being, with a crimson body, two horns on its head, and a long tail trailing behind it.

The three seemed to be quite fearful of it. After setting down their items, they impatiently piloted their flying boat away.

After some turmoil, they finally returned to their residence.

The place was called the “Dao Proving Academy.”

It was also a separate continent floating in the void.

The academy towered high, piercing the clouds.

They arrived at the lower level of the academy to report to their master.

The master of the three was a Nascent Soul stage cultivator named Zhao Wuji, who was already white-haired.

Seeing the three return, he put down the book-like artifact he was reading and asked kindly, “Did you finish everything?”

The three lowered their heads and replied, “Reporting to Master, everything has been handled properly.”

“Do you know why I asked you to make this trip specifically?” Zhao Wuji asked again.

The three were stunned, unsure how to answer.

“Not long ago, Sin Suppression Valley was razed to the ground. The survivors were all taken away for observation. It is said that the incident was caused by the improper collection of relics from Sin Suppression Valley, which led to the spread of ‘World-Ending Power.’”

“Heh heh…”

“This procedure was established by the Immortal Pivot Court. It has been this way for the past thousand years. Even if minor errors occurred occasionally, they never caused major trouble. This time, however, such a significant commotion has arisen,” Zhao Wuji suddenly stopped.

At this moment, the Foundation Establishment cultivator among the three suddenly realized, “Master, are you saying that this is the Immortal Severing Pavilion seizing the opportunity to make a move?”

“Indeed.” Zhao Wuji showed a look of appreciating his student’s understanding. “It’s not just Sin Suppression Valley. From now on, all areas within the Immortal Vessel that fall under the jurisdiction of the Immortal Pivot Court will face the onslaught of the Immortal Severing Pavilion.”

“The Immortal Pivot Court has held power for too long. Those who covet leadership of the Immortal Vessel have waited for too long.”

Zhao Wuji sighed slightly.

Zhao Wuji’s three disciples’ expressions differed upon hearing this.

The Foundation Establishment disciple’s eyes darted around, seemingly calculating something.

Among the two Qi Refining disciples, one lowered his head, carefully pondering his master’s words.

The other, currently possessed by Li Fan’s divine sense clone, appeared indifferent.

His mind wandered, seemingly lost in thought.

Chapter 1188: The Immortal Boat Splits in Two

The Immortal Vessel Splits into Two

“Zhao Xian!” Zhao Wuji saw this and let out a cold snort.

Zhao Xian immediately snapped back to attention.

“Tell me, what does the dispute between the Immortal Severing Pavilion and the Immortal Pivot Court have to do with us being sent on this mission?” Zhao Wuji asked, narrowing his eyes.

“Master is showing his stance and also extending goodwill. This is the first time the Immortal Severing Pavilion is collecting relics after taking over Sin Suppression Valley. Everyone is watching to see how the Immortal Severing Pavilion’s new method compares to the Immortal Pivot Court’s traditional approach. Sending useless relics for repurposing… this is a trivial matter that Master deliberately had a few of us handle personally. It’s both to show your attitude to the Immortal Severing Pavilion and to signal to other observing forces outside…”

Zhao Xian said listlessly.

Zhao Wuji nodded repeatedly, satisfied with Zhao Xian’s analysis.

However, upon seeing his indifferent expression, he couldn’t help but become angry.

Just as he was about to say something, Zhao Xian interrupted him. “Master, I truly don’t understand. The Immortal Vessel is in this state now, yet why can’t we unite? Why must we first fight amongst ourselves until one side is destroyed?”

Zhao Wuji’s expression changed, and he waved his hand, preventing his disciple’s voice from leaking out.

“You unfilial disciple…”

“Is there something wrong?” Zhao Xian asked, head held high, showing no fear.

Suddenly, Zhao Wuji produced a ruler, raised it high, as if to strike Zhao Xian’s head,

But ultimately did not strike with full force.

“Xian’er, you don’t understand.”

“This Xuan Immortal Vessel must have, and can only have, one helmsman. The tragedy from many years ago already demonstrated the horrifying consequences of a disunified supreme decision-making layer,” Zhao Wuji sighed deeply.

Upon hearing this, Zhao Xian also appeared dejected and ceased his arguments.

“You may leave now,” Zhao Wuji suddenly said, his interest waning.

“Do not go out for the time being. Cultivate diligently in the Academy. Since Master has already taken a side, we just need to wait for the outcome. Even if the Immortal Severing Pavilion loses, the Immortal Pivot Court would not dare to do anything to our Dao Proving Academy. At most, they would reduce our resource allocation.”

The three disciples obeyed and retreated to their respective residences.

The Dao Proving Academy, the name was quite imposing.

However, Zhao Xian’s living quarters were rather rudimentary.

It bore no resemblance to a cultivator’s resting place, merely a single room barely sufficient for habitation.

The only commendable aspect was that the spiritual energy concentration within the room was significantly higher than in other areas of the Immortal Vessel.

It was sufficient for cultivation below the Golden Core stage.

Closing the door, he expertly sealed it with a restriction. Zhao Xian’s eyes flashed with excitement. He dug out a book-like artifact from under his bed.

Just as he was about to use it, he suddenly fell asleep.

Li Fan’s divine sense clone slowly materialized.

He took over the book-like artifact.

“Hmm… similar to the Heavenly Profound Mirror, it connects to the Immortal Vessel’s information network and allows one to exchange contribution points from the Academy for corresponding resources. However, it is limited to the internal network of the Dao Proving Academy and cannot connect to other regions of the Immortal Vessel.”

Li Fan shook his head and set aside the so-called “Myriad Records.”

Then, he transformed into a wisp of smoke and infiltrated Zhao Xian’s consciousness.

What could a mere Qi Refining stage youth do against Li Fan’s probing?

Before long, all of Zhao Xian’s secrets, from childhood to the present, were laid bare before Li Fan.

Although Zhao Xian shared the same surname as Zhao Wuji, they were not related by blood.

The reason Zhao Wuji showed such favoritism towards Zhao Xian was entirely due to Zhao Xian’s “cultivation talent.”

He had only been in the Dao Proving Academy for a year but had already reached the late Qi Refining stage.

This cultivation speed, while insignificant in the Xuanhuang Realm, was considered outstanding on the Immortal Vessel.

Cultivation resources on the Immortal Vessel were limited. Even the Dao Proving Academy struggled, prioritizing only the most gifted disciples.

Every three academic years, there was a process of elimination.

Those who fell behind in progress had to leave the Academy, either returning home to become unaffiliated cultivators or accepting appointments from the Immortal Pivot Court to serve in various positions on the Immortal Vessel.

It was this brutal elimination system that kept the Dao Proving Academy vibrant and competitive.

Not only disciples were eliminated; cultivators like Zhao Wuji in the Nascent Soul stage also faced significant pressure.

If their disciples’ performance was mediocre, it indicated a lack of teaching aptitude.

Without strong backing, they would be removed from teaching positions and assigned to other more dangerous roles.

This was also the reason for the oppressive atmosphere throughout the Dao Proving Academy.

Everyone was uncertain when they might be forced to leave.

However, Zhao Xian was an exception.

Perhaps due to his nature, he had no strong desire to remain in the Dao Proving Academy.

Even his passion for cultivation was lukewarm.

Outsiders believed that reaching the late Qi Refining stage in one year was the result of his strenuous efforts.

Only he knew that this was merely the result of sporadic efforts, without much dedication.

Zhao Xian’s greatest interest was in searching the Myriad Records for peculiar anecdotes.

He was filled with interest regarding the origin of the Immortal Vessel, everything about the ancient immortal cultivation world, and the endless star sea beyond the Immortal Vessel…

Li Fan carefully read through his experiences over the past year.

This information was gathered not only through the “Myriad Records” but also from discussions with senior members of the Academy.

“In the ancient times, the Immortal Vessel was still intact. However, due to a sudden catastrophe of star sea world-ending calamities and internal strife. The Immortal Vessel was subsequently broken into two halves.”

“One was named ‘Xuan,’ the other ‘Shang.’”

“This vessel is the Xuan Immortal Vessel.”

“…”

After a pause, Li Fan continued reading.

“For a long time after the Immortal Vessel fractured, it drifted aimlessly in the star sea, leading to a chaotic era of complete disorder.”

“The population plummeted during that time, with nearly nine-tenths perishing.”

“Only after the Immortal Vessel finally stabilized did it appear in this sea of relics.”

“It has never left since…”

“Although it can move within a small area, it is powerless to escape the constraints of the powerful force outside the relics.”

“…”

Li Fan pondered as he read the Immortal Vessel inhabitants’ name for that suction force.

“‘Echoing Star Force’?”

“What is the meaning of the word ‘echoing’?”

Zhao Xian, a mere Qi Refining cultivator, had managed to gather so much information, a testament to his persistent nagging of senior Academy members.

The source of the Echoing Star Force was indeed beyond his knowledge.

Li Fan had to temporarily suppress his questions.

He began to consider his next move.

His divine sense clone was too weak; only by entering with the Saint Fetus could he have enough leeway to act.

The only issue to resolve was the residual power of the True Immortal Runes.

Li Fan immediately thought of the talisman used by the Immortal Severing Pavilion earlier.

Chapter 1189: Hunyuan Golden Elixir Formed (Combined Chapter)

Primal Chaos Golden Core Achieved (Combined Chapters)

“That talisman seems capable of absorbing the power of loose True Immortal Runes. It should serve as a cover.”

“However, it was a newly revealed technique by the Immortal Severing Pavilion. Even within the Dao Proving Academy, known as the source of Immortal Vessel laws, there are no related records.”

The Saint Fetus Li Fan’s divine sense clone’s gaze fell upon Zhao Xian, who was currently sleeping.

“The Xuan Immortal Vessel has a strict hierarchy. Many people have never even left their respective continents in their entire lives. A sturdy fortress must be breached from within.”

The divine sense clone lightly pointed a finger at Zhao Xian’s forehead.

In a trance, Zhao Xian seemed to have a very long dream.

In the dream, the struggle between the Immortal Severing Pavilion and the Immortal Pivot Court dragged on without a decisive victor. The conflict intensified, and the methods became increasingly extreme, ultimately leading to a catastrophic disaster. The Immortal Vessel plunged into the depths of the sea of relics and was annihilated. No one on the Immortal Vessel survived, including Zhao Xian himself.

Waking from the nightmare, Zhao Xian, usually optimistic and easy-going, was deeply shaken for a long time, his face deathly pale.

It was not without reason; the dream was too vivid. Zhao Xian could still remember many details clearly, making him feel as if he had traveled back to the past.

“In the dream, ten years later, the Immortal Vessel’s salvage team discovered a supreme treasure named the ‘Law Derivation Jade Token’ in the sea of relics. It could deduce different cultivation techniques every moment and even deduce them based on conditions. For the ownership of the Law Derivation Jade Token, the Immortal Severing Pavilion and the Immortal Pivot Court fought fiercely. In the end, it was temporarily entrusted to our Dao Proving Academy for safekeeping. Although the Academy acquired an unimaginable number of cultivation techniques during this period, it also laid the groundwork for future calamities.”

“As an elite disciple of the Academy, I had the fortune to study a portion of these techniques in the dream.”

“‘Sea Settling Divine Sword’…”

Zhao Xian subconsciously circulated the cultivation method from his dream.

A moment later, his expression suddenly changed.

“How is this possible?”

Zhao Xian recalled even more profound cultivation technique content.

“‘Great Kang Geng Metal Sword Qi,’ ‘Heavenly Emperor Qi Codex,’ ‘Dual Qi Illuminating Divine Annihilation Technique,’ ‘Boundless Heavenly Pivot Divine Severing Art’…”

Resounding peerless divine arts one after another appeared in his mind.

The subtle energy flow from reciting these techniques also made Zhao Xian realize that these were not figments of his imagination but genuine supreme divine arts!

“These cultivation techniques, let alone for me, even the entire Dao Proving Academy cannot deduce them…”

Zhao Xian’s heart pounded.

“Could it be that I have truly returned from the future to the past?”

For a full half-day, Zhao Xian could not accept this reality. No matter how he racked his brain, he could not figure out why such a bizarre event had occurred.

Since he couldn’t figure it out, he stopped thinking about it.

Zhao Xian’s thoughts quickly focused on the Immortal Vessel’s demise in his dream.

“If that were true…”

“I must change this,” Zhao Xian subconsciously clenched his fists.

Having experienced too many cruel events in his dream, the young Zhao Xian had become much more composed. He did not habitually search the “Myriad Records” for solutions, knowing that all his statements and browsing history within were monitored by the Dao Proving Academy.

“The Immortal Vessel’s downfall is too horrifying. I cannot tell anyone else, not even Master. And I definitely cannot let the Dao Proving Academy, an organization that will be completely destroyed in the future conflict, know about it, lest anyone dare to take more extreme actions, or even cause the Immortal Vessel’s destruction prematurely.”

Zhao Xian paced back and forth in his room, his mind racing. Since experiencing the great dream, his thinking seemed to have become much more flexible.

“Master was right. The Immortal Vessel must have, and can only have, one helmsman. But the conflict between the Immortal Severing Pavilion and the Immortal Pivot Court is irreconcilable. If we let them fight it out, the Immortal Vessel’s destruction is inevitable.”

“The best method is a swift decision to give one side overwhelming advantage in a short period.”

Zhao Xian’s eyes gleamed. “Although the memories of some people and details in the dream have become blurred, the memories of future cultivation techniques and secret arts are extremely clear. With the advantage of this decades-ahead information, I am confident I can help one side unify the Immortal Vessel. As for which side to help…”

He slowly recalled the actions of the two major organizations in his dream, as well as their governing philosophies. Zhao Xian ultimately decided to choose the Immortal Severing Pavilion.

“The Immortal Severing Pavilion is just emerging, desperately in need of talent. As long as I show a little aptitude, I can easily infiltrate.”

“My current strength is too weak; I need to improve as quickly as possible. Fortunately, I now have too many amazing cultivation techniques in my mind.”

“As long as the resources are sufficient, breaking through two major realms within a year is not a problem.”

Zhao Xian closed his eyes and began meditating, prepared to shock the Dao Proving Academy upon emerging from seclusion.

He did not notice that beside him, a faint, almost imperceptible figure was gazing at him.

This figure was, naturally, Li Fan’s divine sense clone.

“Without the restriction of ‘different laws cannot be cultivated simultaneously,’ countless cultivation techniques I’ve studied in the past can now be utilized to their fullest.”

“Compared to the perilous Xuanhuang Realm, this Immortal Vessel is truly like a paradise.”

Restrained everywhere in the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan, in contrast, felt an exhilarating sense of freedom on the Xuan Immortal Vessel, where his profound techniques could be maximally displayed.

…

After traversing half the star sea, encountering the Xuan Immortal Vessel civilization hidden in the sea of relics, and finally finding an entry point to infiltrate.

All this took the Saint Fetus Li Fan approximately a little over a year.

And due to the differential flow of time in various regions of the star sea, less than half a year had actually passed in the Xuanhuang Realm.

In half a year, the Myriad Immortals Alliance had recovered from the great upheaval of the Xuanhuang Realm.

The distorted white mist barrier in the heavens and earth had returned to its original state.

The cultivators’ memories of that catastrophe had gradually faded, and everything seemed to return to its starting point.

Meanwhile, in the Saint Dynasty Great Qi, a subordinate minor world of the Xuanhuang Realm, the changes in the past half-year could be described as “rapid.”

“Rapid” was not just an adjective. In the sky of the Saint Dynasty Great Qi, a wondrous phenomenon had indeed appeared, capable of rivaling the sun and moon.

Centered around five hazy rings of light, an increasing number of shining stars appeared.

Even during the day, they were clearly visible.

And at night, they completely overshadowed the original starlight of Great Qi.

Folk legends claimed that the five rings symbolized the Sacred Emperor’s five direct disciples.

The stars appearing successively around the rings represented the numerous rising talents of Great Qi.

These rumors were not unfounded, as they had solid evidence.

Just three days prior, all the citizens of Great Qi had personally witnessed a shining star near a ring erupt with thousands of times its usual brilliance.

It then transformed into a beam of light that shot directly towards the Sacred Emperor’s Seat in the capital city.

The anomaly persisted for almost half a day before the pillar of light that pierced the heavens and earth dissipated.

After this, people realized that the star in the sky had also vanished and descended to the mortal realm. If the Sacred Emperor’s disciples could trigger such a wondrous phenomenon, what about the Sacred Emperor himself?

Following the Sacred Emperor’s martial arts exhibition six months prior, which had caused world-shaking tremors, people once again engaged in discussions and speculation about the Sacred Emperor’s immense power, albeit privately.

The worship and trust of the Sacred Emperor among the entire Saint Dynasty Great Qi had reached a terrifying level of near-unanimity.

And at this moment, the unparalleled Sacred Emperor in the hearts of Great Qi’s citizens was frowning, staring at a white-haired youth sitting in meditation before him.

Contrary to folk legends, after the beam of light, said to be an auspicious omen, descended from the heavens three days ago, the Sacred Emperor Li Ping felt not only surprise but also anger and vigilance.

Because he immediately discerned the true nature of the light beam: outside the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven, one of the enormous grotto-heavens, painstakingly moved by the Hundred Flowers Daoist to the periphery of Great Qi’s minor world to drag it through the void at high speed…

Had exploded.

And the culprit behind this event was within Great Qi, within the capital city!

Yet Li Ping had been completely unaware of this matter before it happened! How could Li Ping, who considered himself a divinely appointed Sacred Emperor, accept this?

Over the past half-year, while the Myriad Immortals Alliance was busy pacifying the disaster and calming the populace, the Hundred Flowers Daoist had worked tirelessly, moving several grotto-heavens from the Xuanhuang Realm to this place.

Perhaps due to the great power’s disturbance of the Xuanhuang Realm, moving these grotto-heavens had become significantly easier for the Hundred Flowers Daoist. Even so, working day and night for half a year had left the Hundred Flowers Daoist nearly exhausted. Unable to persist any longer, she retreated into the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven to recuperate.

Unexpectedly, the disaster of a grotto-heaven exploding had occurred.

The Hundred Flowers Daoist’s expression was extremely grim. She immediately abandoned her recovery and rushed out of the Five Elements Grotto-Heaven.

At this moment, Li Fan had also identified the culprit.

Before he could even retaliate, Yin Shangren’s words made him shift from shock to pleasant surprise, his anger vanishing.

“Someone…”

“Has successfully formed the ‘Primal Chaos Golden Core’!”

Even the Sacred Emperor, upon hearing Yin Shangren’s words, trembled inwardly and lost focus for a moment.

The Primal Chaos Golden Core, as the realm following “Foundation Establishment” and one of the components of the new cultivation method, was a crucial part of Li Ping’s plan to overturn the Heavenly Venerate Transmission system.

This first step was especially difficult to achieve. Once taken, it would inevitably bring about many unimaginable changes.

When Li Ping summoned Yin Shangren to Great Qi to research the new cultivation method, he hadn’t held much hope. It was done entirely with a “let’s try and see” attitude.

After all, the Heavenly Venerate Transmission system had stood for millennia; dismantling its foundation was not so easy.

Li Ping had anticipated that the development of the new cultivation method would take at least decades, even centuries.

To his surprise, Yin Shangren delivered such a tremendous surprise just over half a year later.

At the same time, Li Fan felt a mix of doubt and vigilance.

Without asking questions, he shifted his gaze from the black-haired youth to Yin Shangren, awaiting his explanation.

Yin Shangren ignored Li Ping and gazed rapturously at the youth cultivating, marveling.

“The aura of the world…”

Li Ping’s gaze furrowed slightly.

The black-haired youth gave him a strange feeling.

He was indeed one of the children who cultivated using the “Establishing Foundation with Me” method, and he had now broken through his realm.

His fluctuating, elusive power made Li Ping feel somewhat unfathomable.

However, the youth’s vitality was too weak.

It was utterly unlike the vigorous vitality of one who had broken through realms, but rather like a candle flickering in the wind, precariously close to extinguishing.

It seemed as if his life would vanish completely the next moment.

After a long while, seeing the black-haired youth’s face contort in pain, Yin Shangren sighed deeply. “To seize the creation of a world with one’s own body…”

“How difficult it is! Although he has achieved the Primal Chaos Golden Core, he has suffered a backlash. If he cannot endure it, his only path is death.”

Li Ping automatically skipped the latter half of the sentence, focusing his attention on the first part of Yin Shangren’s statement.

“To seize the creation of a world with one’s own body? Is this the key to cultivating the Primal Chaos Golden Core?” Li Ping asked.

Yin Shangren remained silent for a moment before replying, “You have witnessed the situation. He has indeed broken through. However, the risks involved are almost death without escape….”

“The new cultivation method should not follow such a path.”

Yin Shangren explained to Li Ping the process of comprehending the Primal Chaos Golden Core through this fortunate coincidence.

“What is Primal Chaos?”

“Establishing Foundation with Me is building a cultivation foundation with one’s complete self. If a person wishes to advance further within the world, they must seek answers from the world, from heaven and earth.”

“Seizing the creation of a world does not mean directly devouring the heavens and earth like the Heavenly Venerate Transmission method…”

“Although the actual effect is similar,” Yin Shangren suddenly said, cutting himself off abruptly.

He looked up at the afterimage of the disappearing grotto-heaven in the sky before Yin Shangren continued, “Achieving Primal Chaos does not mean seizing specific matter or energy. It means seizing the ‘creation’ of the world.”

“There are fifty Great Daos, and Heaven’s evolution creates forty-nine. Because of the one that escapes, the world possesses variable factors, hence heaven and earth can remain infinitely vital after countless years.”

“But if that one that escapes is taken…”

“The light beam that appeared in the sky just now signifies their fate.”

“Of course, I also played a part in this. If external forces hadn’t intervened, it might have taken nearly a hundred years for the changes to manifest. I was trying to help this child; otherwise, with just a Foundation Establishment body, trying to covet the heavens and earth, even just a grotto-heaven, would cause one’s consciousness to be lost in the struggle within the grotto-heaven world.” Yin Shangren looked at Li Ping, showing no intention of apologizing.

“To think of things I cannot, this child is truly remarkable.”

…

From Yin Shangren’s words, Li Ping vaguely understood the meaning of this so-called “Primal Chaos Golden Core.”

As the master of the Great Qi world, and having observed and interacted with numerous minor worlds more closely, he could better understand Yin Shangren’s meaning.

“The world is like a human body. The idea of seizing a world’s creation to achieve one’s own Primal Chaos Golden Core is indeed feasible.”

“However…”

Li Ping pondered for a moment and then shook his head inwardly, rejecting the idea.

“This step is too ambitious!”

“A human body devouring a world. Even I might not be able to achieve it.”

“The new cultivation method should be a path accessible to all.”
